## D71 тАФ EXTERNAL REPORT REVIEWED (Gemini "Economic & Architectural Analysis of Zero-Cost Single-File Web Game Development") тАФ adopt/modify/ignore verdicts тАФ [AARON+CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-16)
Aaron supplied a Gemini report (a generic 2026 primer on $0 single-file web-game dev: coding-assistant tiers, asset-separation, engine benchmarks, asset generators, state/combat patterns, deployment) and asked for an adopt/modify/alter/ignore call against the WHOLE project. **Net: mostly IGNORE тАФ the report was written with no knowledge of this project; on nearly every axis our existing choices are already better-suited to the teaching mission + period aesthetic + single-file/$0 + determinism + the Claude/Opus agent loop. ~3 useful takeaways, all Phase-H / publish, none changing the current roadmap.** Logged so a future chat does not re-litigate "should we use Phaser / DeepSeek / pixel-art."
- **IGNORE тАФ coding-assistant choice (Cursor/OpenCode/Cline + DeepSeek/GPT, ┬з1/┬з3/┬з8):** moot тАФ we build with **Claude Code + Opus 4.8** + the Workflow/subagent orchestration + deterministic probes + adversarial bug-hunts. Downgrading to the report's "$0" pick (OpenCode + DeepSeek-V4-Flash) would gut the reasoning this project depends on (balance A/B, the fog-inversion bug class, anti-Lost-Cause content verification). Its 2026 prices/limits/model names are unverified + fast-stale; irrelevant to the decision.
- **IGNORE the engine switch; KEEP one warning (┬з4):** we use a CUSTOM single-file engine (frozen `build/base.html` 2D canvas + async-CDN Three.js w/ 2D fallback + the `src/tactical/T0тАУT7` real-time sim). Switching to Phaser/KAPLAY/Godot = a catastrophic rewrite that breaks single-file/no-build/determinism/every probe. **BUT** the **Godot `SharedArrayBuffer` + COOP/COEP-headers-can't-be-set-on-GitHub-Pages** problem is real and VALIDATES our no-WASM-threading custom-JS choice (runs on free static hosting where Godot can't). Filed as a permanent guardrail: do not pull in any Phase-H media lib that needs `SharedArrayBuffer`; `coi-serviceworker` is the known shim if headers are ever needed. Reinforces D68 #10 (Classic IS the hex engine, no new co-equal WASM engine).
- **IGNORE the asset generators (┬з5):** PixelLab/Sprite AI = pixel-art (WRONG aesthetic тАФ we are period broadsheet/engraving). Recraft's free tier KEEPS ownership of outputs (an IP trap for a project Aaron wants to own). AI period art also risks anachronism vs the citation-grade/anti-Lost-Cause bar. Our Phase-H plan тАФ REAL PD imagery from LoC/Internet Archive/Wikimedia тАФ wins on aesthetic, cost, IP, and historical accuracy. (Sole back-pocket: Recraft vector-SVG *could* help the H1b corps-badges/flags idea IF hand-authoring is too slow тАФ only style-locked + paid commercial rights; hand-drawn period SVG likely still better.)
- **IGNORE тАФ state/combat/turn patterns (┬з6) тАФ already exceeded:** we already have bare-name global state (`G`/`__FIELD`), seeded deterministic sim (`fldRng`, no `Date.now`/`Math.random` in probes), a phase model, and a combat resolver (`fldResolveFire`/`fldResolveMelee`) with cover/terrain/morale/fatigue/canister/command/logistics far richer than the report's toy formula. The report assumes turn-based; our primary engine is real-time (Classic is the frozen turn-based layer). Mild validation only: unified-state + deterministic + localStorage-serialize == our planned Phase J saves (D54).
- **THE 3 KEEPERS (all Phase-H / publish; none now):** (1) **ADOPT/already-planned тАФ automated asset ingestion:** the report's `compile.py`тЖТBase64 idea = what `tools/build.mjs` already does for code+data; at Phase H extend **build.mjs (Node, not a separate Python script)** to Base64-embed + TIER/COMPRESS media w/ offline fallback тАФ corroborates D68 #7 (the ~1.7MB single file will balloon; portability needs deliberate media tiering). (2) **NOTE тАФ publish options (hosting stays deferred, D54):** GitHub Pages (simplest for one file) or **itch.io + Butler** (best indie discovery + in-browser play + automated deploy); Vercel unnecessary. **$0 nuance the report missed:** GitHub Pages on a PRIVATE repo needs GitHub **Pro (paid)** тЖТ for true $0 use a public deploy repo OR itch.io; rename/copy `civil_war_generals.html`тЖТ`index.html` at publish. (3) **NOTE тАФ COOP/COEP guardrail** (above) folded into Phase-H/D-engine thinking.
- **Action:** no code/roadmap change now. Pointers folded into V1-CHECKLIST Phase H (asset-ingestion-via-build.mjs + the no-SharedArrayBuffer guardrail) and Phase J / the hosting-deferred item (GitHub-Pages-private-needs-Pro + itch.io/Butler). The report did NOT change what ships for B-6.

## D72 тАФ PHASE B-6 ┬╖ CS-PLAYER "COMMAND EITHER SIDE" (the tactical mode is now playable from either army; the B-1 attacker AI becomes player-facing) тАФ [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-16)
The 6th + FINAL V1-CHECKLIST Phase-B item (D61, charter fork #10). The real-time tactical engine can now be commanded from EITHER army: pick the Confederacy and you DEFEND Henry House Hill while the B-1 attacker-AI presses you uphill тАФ which is exactly what makes the B-1 doctrine player-facing (the whole point of the fork) and doubles tactical replayability. New module `src/tactical/T7-command-side.js` + surgical seams in T0/T1/T3 + `tools/probe-csplayer.mjs`. Deliverable тЙИ**1702KB**.
- **NOT a new gated sim layer тАФ a GENERALIZATION.** The plumbing was already half-built (T2 `fldSkirmishOOB` assigns `u.ai` by side; the T2 campaign briefing already speaks side-aware role text; `fldPlayerSide()` already drove the B-2/B-3/B-4 display layers; the campaign result-feedback `fldCampaignComputeOutcome`/`ApplyOutcome`/`EndHtml` were written side-aware back in Phase A). B-6 closed the TWO remaining gaps: **(1)** the input layer (`fldPlayerSel`/select-all/`fldCycleSel`/`fldPointerDown`) and the render/HUD **fog VIEWER** (the 2D markers, the ghosts, the 3D sync, the friend/foe line) were a literal `"US"` тЖТ now read `fldPlayerSide()`; **(2)** the hand-authored First Bull Run scenario only ever fielded a US player тЖТ now honours a side toggle.
- **`__FIELD.playerSide` made AUTHORITATIVE** (resolved once in `fldInitSim`, precedence: explicit `opts.playerSide` > skirmish `playerSide` > a CS campaign via `_fldCamp().side` > `"US"`). `fldBrSpec` (T1) flips the scenario AI flags off it тАФ the player's side is the non-AI side, the other side is the AI (a CS player DEFENDS; `__FIELD.attacker` stays US, so the B-1 attacker AI presses). `fldPlayerSide()` (T3) resolves a CS **campaign LIVE** from `G.campaign.side` first (the legacy contract the officer roster/fog read mid-setup), then the explicit per-launch side.
- **NEW player-facing UI (T7):** a period-broadsheet **side-choice card** for the standalone Bull Run ("Lead the Union тАФ ATTACK" / "Hold for the Confederacy тАФ DEFEND"); a **side-aware briefing objective** (attack-&-seize vs hold-&-deny); a side-aware **"your war vs history"** end note (pronoun follows the side you played); an end-screen **"you" outcome line** (role-aware: "you carried the position" / "your line held" / "your assault was repulsed"); the 3D **camera seats behind the PLAYER's home edge** (a CS defender looks across his line at the advancing Union); the friend/foe HUD names the player's own side with the dignified FULL name ("4 Confederate vs 1 Union"). The skirmish menu + the campaign already plumbed side, so they work via the same generalization.
- **BYTE-IDENTITY:** the player side defaults to `"US"` (the historical attacker), so every standalone/probe launch resolves exactly as before; under `autoBoth` all units are AI regardless of side (the AI-vs-AI sim is independent of `playerSide`, proven seed-for-seed). The render/control/HUD generalizations are unreachable in the headless probes (renderer `none`). The 9 tactical baselines + bullrun stayed byte-identical.
- **VETTING CAUGHT A REAL REGRESSION (fixed before any commit):** my first `fldPlayerSide()` rewrite trusted a stale `__FIELD.playerSide` and broke the CS-**campaign** officer-roster/fog contract (the roster/fog read `fldPlayerSide()` mid-setup, before a relaunch). `probe-officers` flagged it. **Fix:** resolve a CS campaign LIVE from `G.campaign.side` first, then the explicit per-launch side (T0 `fldInitSim` + T3 `fldPlayerSide` made consistent; `fldBrSpec` routed through `fldPlayerSide()`).
- **ADVERSARIAL BUG-HUNT (52 agents тАФ 6 diverse-lens Opus finders ├Ч 3-skeptic default-refute verify + a completeness critic, per D63): 15 findings тЖТ 11 confirmed + 7 critic gaps; 4 refuted. FIXED the ones that matter:** **(HIGH)** a skirmish "Fight Again" soft-locked a CS player тАФ the rematch fell through to the generic US sandbox, leaving a CS player zero controllable units тЖТ the rematch now REPLAYS the full stashed launch spec (`__FIELD._launchOpts`, same scenario/skirmish/side/fog, bumped seed) AND the sandbox OOB now assigns `ai` by `playerSide` (defence-in-depth; byte-identical for US); **(MED ├Ч2, dedup)** the 3D camera was hard-wired to the US south edge тЖТ side-aware home-edge seating; **(MED, critic G1)** reinforcement banners + the aria-live announce + the "Reinforcements arrive" auto-pause leaked a fog-hidden ENEMY detrainment тЖТ all gated on player-visibility (own side / fog off / scouted), fog-OFF byte-identical; **(MED, critic G2)** `probe-csplayer` only HUD-checked the no-leak invariant тЖТ added a fog-RENDER step asserting the render-hide predicate hides тЙе1 enemy and NEVER a friendly, for both viewers; **(LOW)** the side-card `aria-label` was unescaped (latent if a future `objective.name` carries `"`/`<`) тЖТ escaped the dynamic parts; the end-screen "you" line now also speaks on the aria-live region; the stale "player controls only the US" comment reworded; a byte-identity-delegation note added to the probe. **DEFERRED with note (pre-existing / convention-consistent, not B-6 regressions):** the side-choice sheet uses the established Back-not-Esc sheet convention (matches Skirmish/Preset); the top-bar objective readout stays factual ("Union holdsтАж"); `openSheet`-unavailable falls back to US; `fldPlayerSide()` campaign-first precedence is intentional (the legacy live contract тАФ every reachable launch agrees).
- **WCAG 2.2 AA (wcag-auditor, Sonnet per D63):** clean after 2 contrast fixes тАФ the side-card badge `opacity:.75` blended the accent below 4.5:1, so it was removed and the CS accent darkened `#b06a5a`тЖТ`#b77668` (4.72:1 on the `.upg` bg); everything else (titles, decks, objective block, outcome line, briefing/end borders) passes; ARIA (role=group, per-card aria-label, type=button, dialog focus traps) + CVD-safety (side named in text + ATTACK/DEFEND badge, never colour-alone) confirmed.

The CS defense is winnable (the role-aware defender holds the hill under fog), the field renders from your side, the fog shows only what YOU scout, and the briefing/HUD/end-screen all speak from the army you command.

NEXT: Phase C tactical breadth тАФ Eastern marquee first (Antietam / Fredericksburg / Gettysburg / Chancellorsville on the data-driven engine, D69).**

## D73 тАФ PHASE C-1 ┬╖ FREDERICKSBURG (the Marye's Heights assault) тАФ the SECOND data-driven tactical battle + the data-driven scenario-UI generalization + the scenario-gated "doomed-assault" AI posture тАФ [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-16)
The first Phase-C (tactical BREADTH) milestone, Eastern marquee first per D69. The tactical engine, mature after B1тАУB6, is now battle-AGNOSTIC: a new historical battle = a `data/<battle>.json` file + one registry line, NO new combat code. Fredericksburg, Dec 13 1862 тАФ Burnside's army storms the open glacis toward the sunken Telegraph Road, where Longstreet's men hold a 4-foot stone wall under the pre-sighted guns on Marye's Heights. New `data/fredericksburg.json` (`GAME_DATA.fredericksburg.fredericksburg`) + `tools/probe-fredericksburg.mjs` + the T1/T7 UI generalization + a small gated T0 engine seam. Deliverable тЙИ**1743.6KB**.
- **THE DATA-DRIVEN SCENARIO REGISTRY (the reusable spine).** `fldScenarioRegistry()`/`fldScenarioData(id)` (T1) map each registered id тЖТ its `GAME_DATA.<battle>` object; `fldScenarioInit` builds ANY registered id from the SAME shape (field/attacker/defender/objective/leaders/supply/terrain[hills,woods,walls,markers]/oob/reinforcements/teaching). Bull Run resolves the identical object it always did (`fldScenarioData("bullrun1")`) тЖТ byte-identical. Adding Antietam/Gettysburg/etc. is now a data file + a registry line.
- **THE DATA-DRIVEN UI GENERALIZATION (T1+T7).** `fldInjectScenarioButtons` iterates the registry (Bull Run keeps its bespoke marquee button `_fldInjectBullRunButton`; every other battle gets a data-built button from `data.menu`) and returns the LAST button so T0 anchors the skirmish/preset buttons after the whole block; `fldLaunchBattle` fires the briefing for ANY scenario; `fldBullRunSideChoice`тЖТ`fldScenarioSideChoice(id,go)` reads `sd.sides` (per-battle side-choice card) with code fallbacks; `fldBriefObjectiveHtml` keeps the keyword skeleton ("seize and hold"/"HOLD"/"deny") + a data flavor sentence (`sd.brief`); `fldScenarioEndHtml` keeps the Bull Run branch byte-identical (via a shared `_fldScenarioEndBox`) + a data-driven `sd.endNote` branch (keyed winnerтЖТplayer-side) for other battles. New `sides`/`brief` data added to `bullrun.json` (inert; reproduces Bull Run's exact card/briefing copy from data). **Probes confirm Bull Run + csplayer byte-identical (bullrun 15/15, csplayer 16/16).**
- **THE DOOMED-FRONTAL-ASSAULT POSTURE (a scenario-gated T0 seam тАФ the historical-fidelity lever).** The B-1 attacker AI is *competent* (fog-off it column-rushes the killing ground cheaply and presses the mass bayonet on the objective) тАФ which is exactly what Fredericksburg's assault was NOT. So `data.assaultDoctrine:"cautious"` тЖТ `__FIELD._atkCautious` (set in `fldScenarioInit`, reset false per launch in `fldInitSim`) makes the AI attacker advance IN LINE across the open glacis and trade fire but NEVER column-rush nor mass-bayonet a covered line тАФ Burnside's piecemeal disaster. In `fldAiAttacker`, `var aggressive = !__FIELD.fog && !__FIELD._atkCautious` gates the assault + column branches; the cautious attacker presses to `OBJ_R*FLD.ATK_CAUTIOUS_HOLD` of the objective before holding. **Default off тЖТ `aggressive === !fog` тЖТ Bull Run / sandbox / skirmish / campaign BYTE-IDENTICAL (probe-ai 15/15, field 13/13).** A HUMAN commanding the Union is UNBOUND by this тАФ the alt-history hook ("do what the Army of the Potomac could not"); the flag only shapes the AI attacker (AI-vs-AI + a CS player's opponent).
- **NOT a fog default (no contradiction of the D58/D64 "fog aids the defender" teaching).** Bull Run defaults fog ON (D67) because its clear-weather stacked config favored the attacker; Fredericksburg keeps fog OFF (historically the morning fog had LIFTED тАФ "a chicken could not live on that field") and wins the defense by a DIFFERENT, scenario-appropriate lever: the cautious posture + the continuous stone wall (cover 1.7) + the massed pre-sighted crest canister over the open glacis. Two complementary ways a defender wins, each historically faithful to its battle тАФ not a relitigation of fog.
- **THE BUG-HUNT CAUGHT THE BALANCE'S CORE FLAW (a real HIGH, fixed pre-commit).** The adversarial bug-hunt (5 diverse-lens Opus finders ├Ч default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic) тЖТ **4 confirmed + 5 critic gaps.** The HIGH (empirically traced): the unchanged defender doctrine `fldAiDefender` holds the objective's FORWARD FACE (`obj.z + obj.r*0.55`); my first geometry put that face FORWARD of the wall, so the AI marched the defending line OFF the wall into the open on tick 1 тАФ the 1.7├Ч cover was never used and the result was carried by canister + numbers, not the wall (the whole teaching, gutted; the static-terrain probe missed it). **Fix (the Bull Run pattern):** seat the objective center BEHIND the wall (`obj.z` 375тЖТ331) so the forward face lands the holding line exactly ON the wall in cover, and raise `ATK_CAUTIOUS_HOLD` 0.6тЖТ0.85 so the cautious attacker's hold band sits in the OPEN just outside the wall's cover radius (only the attacker is exposed). Added a LIVE-position cover assertion to the probe (defenders REMAIN at the wall in cover тЙе1.5; the attacker's hold line is exposed) so the regression can't recur. Also fixed: the side-card aria ROLE word was hardwired US=attack (wrong for a future CS-attacker scenario) тЖТ threaded the data-driven `attacking` flag (accent stays a side colour). Critic gaps addressed: the human "seize-and-hold" win requires clearing the whole position incl. the rear guns (objective note reworded); the `endNote.draw` path now probe-asserted. ACCEPTED-as-intentional (the directive authorized neutralizing Bull Run-specific objective copy): the generic objective skeleton reworded Bull Run's CS line ("deny the crest to the Union assault"тЖТ"deny it to the enemy") тАФ keywords + the data flavor preserved, cosmetic only.
- **BALANCE (the historical slaughter, empirically тАФ AI-vs-AI, fog OFF default, live stacked officers+logistics+arms):** **Confederate 8/8** (the assault is DENIED to the clock тАФ won by timeout, never carrying the wall); **Union casualties тЙИ1.91├Ч the Confederate** (US ~12,300 vs CS ~6,400 over the casualty sample тАФ the bloody repulse, the attacker pays more); the stone wall is **load-bearing** (deleting it weakens the defense); the defending line provably HOLDS the wall in cover through the firefight while the attacker dies exposed on the open glacis. The artillery "men" are an explicit, documented VOLUME-OF-FIRE proxy for the massed pre-sighted crest guns; the result is intentionally gun-AND-wall-driven (historically defensible). The deeper ~6:1 historical ratio is carried by the teaching cards, not forced on the sim (the engine's long US rifle range vs short CS smoothbore makes a literal 6:1 unreachable without distorting other systems).
- **CITATION-GRADE, ANTI-LOST-CAUSE CONTENT.** 7 Union assault waves (KimballтЖТAndrewsтЖТZookтЖТIrish/MeagherтЖТCaldwellтЖТOwenтЖТSturgisтЖТGriffinтЖТHumphreys's dusk bayonet chargeтЖТGetty) vs the walled line (CobbтЖТRansom + Kershaw/Cooke thickening it to four ranks) under the Washington Artillery + Alexander's guns; leaders with historical `fate` (only Cobb falls, mortally wounded тАФ the rest endure); 4 teaching cards (the futility of fourteen charges; the pontoons that lost the battle; "It is well that war is so terrible"; Kirkland on the cold plain) тАФ the lesson is the DOOMED FRONTAL ASSAULT into prepared fire + the cost of piecemeal command, NOT Confederate invincibility. `provenance` baked in (Wikipedia/OR OOB, NPS, American Battlefield Trust, O'Reilly).
- **Verified (the full PROPER VETTING gate, D53-OPS):** GATE OK (1743.6KB) тЖТ **probe-fredericksburg 20/20, 0 pe** тЖТ full no-regression GREEN (field 13 ┬╖ bullrun 15 ┬╖ fog 13 ┬╖ autopause 13 ┬╖ ai 15 ┬╖ campaign-link 16 ┬╖ officers 15 ┬╖ logistics 14 ┬╖ arms 23 ┬╖ presets 26 тАФ all BYTE-IDENTICAL; **csplayer 16/16**; bootprobe ok; t1probe 14/14; diag-classic nonBlank **346**; strategic spot-check desk/economy/victory green; 0 pe) тЖТ balance A/B (CS 8/8, slaughter 1.91:1, wall load-bearing, defenders hold-the-wall live) тЖТ adversarial bug-hunt (4 confirmed + 5 critic gaps; the HIGH geometry flaw + the aria role fixed + gaps addressed + re-verified) тЖТ wcag-auditor clean (0 fixes тАФ the C-1 UI reuses already-audited components; 1 PRE-EXISTING global `.title-sub`/`--rule` contrast issue [3.59:1 on the lightest sheet-gradient stop] NOTED for the dedicated Phase-E WCAG pass, not a C-1 regression). Committed + pushed. **NEXT: the next Eastern marquee battle тАФ Antietam or Gettysburg (D69), same data-driven recipe.**

## D74 тАФ RUN-K Q&A: Phase-C clearing decisions (next battle ┬╖ battle scope ┬╖ the universal-combat balance principle ┬╖ campaign scope) тАФ [AARON] (run k, 2026-06-16)
Four locked decisions to clear the next runs after C-1 (Fredericksburg) shipped (D73).
- **(1) NEXT BATTLE = ANTIETAM (Sep 17, 1862).** Chronological (it precedes Fredericksburg); the bloodiest single day; the iconic sequence is the Cornfield тЖТ the Sunken Road ("Bloody Lane") тЖТ Burnside's Bridge. Build it next (D69 Eastern marquee order otherwise unchanged: then Gettysburg ┬╖ Chancellorsville ┬╖ Malvern Hill).
- **(2) BATTLE SCOPE = MULTI-PHASE EPICS** (not a single focused slice). The big battles are built as **sequential phases/objectives in one scenario** тАФ Antietam's three phases (Cornfield тЖТ Bloody Lane тЖТ Burnside's Bridge), Gettysburg's three days, etc. **This requires a NEW gated engine capability:** a multi-objective / sequential-phase scenario (a phase transitions when its objective is decided тЖТ the next objective opens on a fresh sector of the field, carrying forward the survivors/casualty + the running result). Build it as a guarded seam (default = the single-objective path Fredericksburg/Bull Run use тЖТ those stay byte-identical), data-described in the scenario file (e.g. a `phases[]` block), and probe it. Decide-&-log the sub-mechanics (how survivors carry over, how the overall win is scored across phases, the inter-phase UI) within the milestone; surface only a NEW/contradicting fork.
- **(3) THE UNIVERSAL-COMBAT BALANCE PRINCIPLE (the consequential one).** The combat MODEL is ONE shared, consistent, predictable ruleset across EVERY battle тАФ per-unit-to-unit damage, rates of fire, cover multipliers, canister, melee тАФ and is **NEVER tuned per-battle**. Outcomes EMERGE from scenario DESIGN (historical OOB strengths, terrain/cover, reinforcement timing, and the tactics/doctrine each side uses) under that shared model. **Casualty ratios reflect the player's/AI's actual strategy + tactics тАФ NOT a forced historical number** тАФ but each battle is DESIGNED so that if both sides use roughly historical positioning + tactics, the shared engine yields ~the historical result. **Game feel: fairness + cross-battle consistency OVER per-battle fidelity fudging** (a soldier's rifle / a battery's canister does the same damage in Antietam as in Fredericksburg as in Bull Run; only the scenario differs). This SUPERSEDES the "data-tuned vs funneling-mechanic" framing of the Q3 popup тАФ neither verbatim: it's "one universal model, shape outcomes through historical design, results follow tactics."
  - **CONSEQUENCE / required cleanup (do FIRST in the Antietam milestone):** the Fredericksburg crest-artillery "men" were inflated as a **VOLUME-OF-FIRE PROXY** тАФ a per-battle strength fudge that VIOLATES this principle. REPLACE it with a CONSISTENT artillery representation (realistic crew counts + a gun-count / battery-weight model so a battery's fire output is consistent across all battles, the universal canister rule doing the killing), then re-tune Fredericksburg's CS-favored result via GEOMETRY/OOB/terrain (NOT fudge) and RE-VET it (the live-cover + balance probe). Antietam's massed artillery (the Cornfield) needs this consistent model anyway. Also revisit any other per-battle strength fudges. A universal **"frontage/funneling"** rule (a narrow/walled front lets only a FRACTION of an attacker bring fire to bear) is PERMITTED тАФ but only if it is universal + consistent across all battles AND a battle genuinely needs it; it is NOT required.
- **(4) CAMPAIGN SCOPE = STANDALONE MENU BATTLES** (for now). New battles stay standalone "historical battles" picked from the main menu (the current Fredericksburg/Bull-Run-menu behavior); do NOT add per-battle campaign-launch constraints yet. (Bull Run's existing campaign mapping stays; wiring the rest into the strategic campaign is a deferred, later integration.)

## D75 тАФ PHASE C-1.5 ┬╖ THE UNIVERSAL ARTILLERY GUN MODEL (de-fudging Fredericksburg's "volume-of-fire proxy men" тЖТ a consistent gun-count/battery-weight fire model) тАФ [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-16)
The FIRST sub-milestone of the Antietam epic (D74 #3, "do FIRST"): the consequential **universal-combat** cleanup тАФ replace Fredericksburg's per-battle artillery **volume-of-fire proxy men** fudge (the C-1/D73 batteries inflated `men` to 500/440/500 to fake the massed crest fire) with a CONSISTENT gun-count model used identically in every battle. Shipped + pushed as its own vetted unit before Antietam. Touches `src/tactical/T5-arms.js` + `T0-field-sandbox.js` + `T1-bull-run.js` + `data/fredericksburg.json` + `tools/probe-fredericksburg.mjs`. Deliverable тЙИ**1749.6KB**.
- **THE MODEL:** `FLDA.GUN_FIRE_WEIGHT` = 27 (men-equivalent fire-strength per gun, UNIVERSAL тАФ never tuned per-battle). `fldArtFireStr(u)` (T5) returns the fire-strength numerator the fire model divides by 1500: for a battery declaring a GUN COUNT тЖТ `guns * GUN_FIRE_WEIGHT * clamp(men/maxMen)` (rated fire from the gun count, scaled by CREW AVAILABILITY so a battery losing cannoneers fades smoothly, not full-then-zero); for infantry, an arms-off launch, or a LEGACY battery with no `guns` тЖТ `u.men` EXACTLY as before. Wired in `fldResolveFire` (T0: `fireMen = (arms && art && guns) ? fldArtFireStr(u) : u.men; strF = fireMen/1500`), with `guns` carried dataтЖТunit via `fldMakeUnit` (T0 `guns:o.guns||0`) + `fldBrSpec` (T1 `guns:d.guns||0`).
- **CONSISTENCY (not just gating):** calibrated so a standard 6-gun battery тЖТ 6├Ч27 = 162 тЙИ Bull Run's already-realistic **160-men/6-gun** Griffin & Ricketts тАФ so the universal model REPRODUCES the existing realistic batteries. Bull Run's batteries (no `guns` field, byte-locked) stay on the men path AND are consistent with the model, not merely grandfathered. (Bull Run was never fudged тАФ only Fredericksburg's artillery was; no other per-battle strength fudge exists, per a repo scan.)
- **BYTE-IDENTITY:** the gun path is reached ONLY by a battery declaring `guns` (Fredericksburg's 3 crest batteries). Every baseline has no gun-equipped battery тЖТ `fldArtFireStr` returns `u.men` тЖТ byte-identical. VERIFIED: field 13 ┬╖ bullrun 15 ┬╖ fog 13 ┬╖ autopause 13 ┬╖ ai 15 ┬╖ campaign-link 16 ┬╖ officers 15 ┬╖ logistics 14 ┬╖ presets 26 ┬╖ csplayer 16 ┬╖ **arms 23** тАФ all byte-identical, 0 pe; bootprobe ok; t1probe 14; diag-classic nonBlank **346**.
- **FREDERICKSBURG RE-TUNED VIA HONEST DESIGN (not fudge):** the 3 batteries now carry real gun counts (Washington Artillery **9**, the Marye's grand battery **16**, Alexander's reserve **9** = **34** historical guns crowning the heights) + realistic crew (200/350/200). The CS-favored result EMERGES from the stone wall's cover + the massed gun count + the cautious-attacker-dies-exposed geometry тАФ re-tuned via geometry/OOB, NOT strength inflation. RE-VET: **CS 8/8**, Union:Confederate casualty ratio **2.06:1** (BETTER than the proxy's 1.91 тАФ the honest 34-gun model at full crew is more concentrated), the stone wall measurably **load-bearing** (cuts CS casualties 18-23% across seeds, 5/5 CS wins), the crest guns **survive 8/8** seeds and fire тАФ probe-fredericksburg **22/22**, 0 pe.
- **D74 PRINCIPLE EMBODIED:** one shared ruleset (a gun throws the same metal in Antietam as Fredericksburg as Bull Run); outcomes from scenario design; casualty ratios follow tactics, not a forced number. The gun count + crew-scaling = a defensible, consistent, exploit-free model (the universal canister rule does the killing on top). **CAMPAIGN SEMANTICS (documented at the seam):** the gun count is army-size-invariant "hardware" тАФ `strengthMul` (strategic army size) flows through the Cannon-Corps bridge (`_canisterScale` + reach/pow), NOT raw volume, so a future campaign-linked gun battery doesn't inherit a dead lever.
- **ADVERSARIAL BUG-HUNT (22 agents тАФ 6 diverse-lens Opus finders ├Ч 3-skeptic default-refute verify + a completeness critic, per D63): 0 confirmed finder bugs (all 5 finder candidates REFUTED тАФ the change is correct), 5 completeness-critic gaps ALL FIXED:** (MED) the probe's `fielded()` read a non-existent `u.men0` typo тЖТ `u.maxMen||u.men` (the engine's real original-strength field); (MED) no probe guarded battery survival after the smaller maxMen steepened the morale slope тЖТ a new CREST-GUNS-SURVIVE+FIRE step (8/8 alive, 6/8 firing by tтЙИ120s); (MED) the crew-scaling term was untested тЖТ a half-crew assertion (half crew тЖТ half fire); (LOW) the gun-model/strengthMul campaign interaction тЖТ documented intentional; (LOW) Bull Run's legacy battery shows no HUD gun count тЖТ documented as the byte-locked migration boundary. Also rewrote the load-bearing probe from a noisy single-seed strength-diff into a robust multi-seed CS-casualty-reduction test.
- **WCAG (wcag-auditor, Sonnet per D63):** clean тАФ the gun-count HUD text 15.79:1, the canister band 9.69:1, the long-range band 8.99:1 on the dark field panel; CVD-safe (a numeral + "gun/guns" text, never colour). No fixes.
- **Verified (PROPER VETTING, D53-OPS):** GATE OK (1749.6KB) тЖТ probe-fredericksburg **22/22, 0 pe** тЖТ full no-regression byte-identical (above) тЖТ balance A/B (CS 8/8, ratio 2.06, wall load-bearing, guns survive) тЖТ bug-hunt (0 confirmed + 5 critic gaps fixed + re-probed) тЖТ wcag clean. Committed + pushed. **NEXT: Antietam as the MULTI-PHASE epic (D74 #1/#2) тАФ the gated `phases[]` engine capability + the citation-grade 3-phase scenario (Cornfield тЖТ Bloody Lane тЖТ Burnside's Bridge); research dossier drafted (`.tmp/antietam-dossier.md`), engine design drafted (`.tmp/B-antietam-multiphase-design.md`).**

## D76 тАФ PHASE C-2 ┬╖ ANTIETAM, the FIRST MULTI-PHASE EPIC (the gated `phases[]` engine + the 3-phase Cornfield тЖТ Bloody Lane тЖТ Burnside's Bridge scenario) тАФ [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-16)
The second Antietam sub-milestone (D74 #1/#2/#4): a NEW gated engine capability тАФ sequential phases/objectives in one scenario тАФ and the citation-grade 3-phase Antietam scenario built on it. The bloodiest single day, fought as three sub-battles in sequence with survivors/casualties + the running result carried forward. New module `src/tactical/T8-phases.js` + surgical T0/T1 seams + `data/antietam.json` + one registry line + `tools/probe-antietam.mjs`. Deliverable тЙИ**1814.7KB**.
- **THE MULTI-PHASE ENGINE (T8, gated on `__FIELD.phases`):** a scenario declaring a `data.phases[]` block routes (T1 `fldScenarioInit` тЖТ `_fldScenarioInitPhased`) to the T8 engine: `_fldBuildPhase(i)` builds phase i's terrain/objective/win-thresholds/attacker/defender/doctrine/OOB/reinforcements + `fldResetRun`; when a phase's objective resolves, the `fldCheckVictory` intercept (`_fldPhaseResolved`) records the phase result + accrues casualties to a running `battleCas` + adds the weighted `scoreWeight` to `phaseScore`, then ADVANCES (headless тЖТ `_fldAdvancePhase` immediately so `fldStepN` keeps stepping; UI тЖТ the inter-phase card gates it) тАФ or, on the LAST phase, ends the battle with the aggregate winner (`_fldBattleWinner`, a weighted score with a DRAW band) via the existing `fldOnOver`.
- **DECIDED SUB-MECHANICS (decide-&-log, D61):** **(1) discrete sequential sub-battles** (not one cluttered field) тАФ each phase = its own sector/OOB/objective fought to decision; cleaner teaching + the perf floor. **(2) Carry-over = the running CASUALTY tally + the per-phase score/results** (Antietam's phases are different troops in different places тЖТ each spawns fresh; the cost + the sector results carry тАФ D74's "survivors/casualty + running result"). **(3) Scoring = a weighted aggregate with a real DRAW band** (`abs(USтИТCS) < 0.5` тЖТ draw) so the historical TACTICAL DRAW / marginal-Union-strategic-check EMERGES. **(4) Inter-phase UI = a period-broadsheet transition card** (the result + the running tally + the next phase + its teaching) + a running-tally TOP-BAR label + an aggregate phase-by-phase end-screen.
- **PER-PHASE scenData VIEW (the clean integration):** `_fldPhaseView` splices a phase's `leaders`/`supply`/`objective` onto a copy of the top-level scenario, so the officers (T3, reads `scenData.leaders`) + logistics (T4, reads `scenData.supply`) layers build the phase's cast/trains PER PHASE with **ZERO change to T3/T4**; `__FIELD._scenTop` keeps the whole scenario for the UI/end-screen. Each phase also carries its own `assaultDoctrine` + `defaultFog` + gun-model artillery.
- **BYTE-IDENTITY:** ALL of it is reached only when `__FIELD.phases` is set; `fldInitSim` clears `__FIELD.phases = null` every launch, and the seams (`fldCheckVictory` intercept, `fldOnOver` prepend, `fldRenderTop` label) are all `if (__FIELD.phases)` no-ops тЖТ the single-objective path is byte-identical. VERIFIED on the Part-B build: field 13 ┬╖ bullrun 15 ┬╖ fog 13 ┬╖ autopause 13 ┬╖ ai 15 ┬╖ campaign-link 16 ┬╖ officers 15 ┬╖ logistics 14 ┬╖ presets 26 ┬╖ csplayer 16 ┬╖ arms 23 ┬╖ **fredericksburg 22** (the menu order absorbs the new Antietam button тАФ chronological: Bull Run тЖТ Antietam тЖТ Fredericksburg) тАФ all byte-identical, 0 pe; bootprobe ok; t1probe 14; diag-classic **346**.
- **THE 3-PHASE SCENARIO (citation-grade, anti-Lost-Cause; from an 8-agent research dossier with corrections applied):** **P1 the CORNFIELD** (dawn тАФ Hooker's I Corps + Mansfield's XII vs Jackson's wing + Hood's counterattack; S.D. Lee's ~12-gun "Artillery Hell"); **P2 the SUNKEN ROAD / "Bloody Lane"** (Sumner's II Corps vs D.H. Hill in a worn-lane trench, carried by Barlow's enfilade + a misheard order); **P3 BURNSIDE'S BRIDGE** (the IX Corps bottleneck across the Lower Bridge, held by Toombs's few, the breakthrough halted by A.P. Hill's Light Division from Harpers Ferry). Gun-model artillery throughout. The lessons: command failure on BOTH sides, terrain + contingency over martial "genius", McClellan's wasted ~2:1 advantage + withheld reserves, and ABOVE ALL the Emancipation Proclamation five days later (surfaced in the end-screen + a teaching card тАФ the classic Lost-Cause erasure refused).
- **BALANCE (AI-vs-AI, 8 seeds, deterministic тАФ the D74 principle):** under the shared model + historical positioning, the per-phase outcomes are HISTORICALLY FAITHFUL тАФ **the Cornfield is Confederate-held 8/8, the Sunken Road is Union-carried 8/8 (the Bloody Lane falls), Burnside's Bridge is Confederate-held 8/8 (A.P. Hill halts the breakthrough)** тЖТ aggregate **CS 2-1 (8/8)**. Re-tuned to faithfulness via GEOMETRY/OOB (P2 the lane weakened so the US carries it but PAYS ~1500; P3 the bridge seated so the defenders hold the bluff cover, forcing the US to assault + bleed, with A.P. Hill hastened to halt the advance). The end-screen frames the CS tactical edge as the historical tactical draw / strategic Union check / emancipation turning point. A HUMAN player can rewrite any sector (the alt-history hook).
- **WCAG (wcag-auditor, Sonnet per D63):** the inter-phase card + the aggregate end-screen тАФ 3 contrast fixes (the "vs" separator `opacity:.5`тЖТ`#8c8478` 5.20:1; the 3 end-screen casualty-count spans `opacity:.6`тЖТhue-matched 4.75-4.81:1) + 1 focus-indicator gap (added an explicit `#d8c87a` outline to `#fldPhaseGo`). CVD-safe (sectors named "Union"/"Confederate" in text + colour), aria-modal + single-button focus trap, reduceMotion-honored.
- **Verified (PROPER VETTING, D53-OPS):** GATE OK (1814.7KB) тЖТ **probe-antietam 16/16, 0 pe** тЖТ **full no-regression byte-identical** (the 12 baselines above + arms 23 + boot/t1/diag 346, all fresh on the Part-B build) тЖТ balance A/B (per-phase faithful, deterministic, CS 2-1) тЖТ wcag (4 fixes). **ADVERSARIAL BUG-HUNT (7 diverse-lens Opus finders ├Ч default-refute verify + a critic) was LAUNCHED but had not finished at commit time** (a long fan-out) тАФ committed/pushed to preserve the otherwise-fully-vetted, playable milestone under a time constraint; **the bug-hunt MUST be completed + any confirmed finding fixed + re-probed in the next session** (Part A's identical hunt found 0 real bugs, so risk is low, but the gate is not formally closed). Committed + pushed. **NEXT: complete the Antietam bug-hunt, then the rest of Phase C (Gettysburg ┬╖ Chancellorsville ┬╖ Malvern Hill) OR the Phase-H graphics pass for a demo.**

## D77 тАФ PHASE C-2.5 demo cohesion: audio/flags/portrait/status catch-up + tactical cohesion mini-pass тАФ [CLAUDE] (2026-06-18)
This entry catches the decision/memory log up to the post-D76 demo-polish trailhead already present in recent commits, then records the 2026-06-18 tactical cohesion mini-pass.
- **Status reality:** recent repo history after D76 already includes the Antietam bug-hunt completion/audioprobe fix, `T9-audio.js` audio work, Gettysburg Day 1 balance/probe, `T10-flags.js` unit flags/insignia, Shiloh as the first Western theater real-time battle, cabinet/president portraits, save slots, and help overlay work. The roadmap/memory docs were stale and are now being aligned.

## D82 тАФ Malvern Hill completion + Eastern marquee C1 complete тАФ [CODEX] (2026-06-18)
Aaron asked Codex to build the next Phase-C Eastern marquee battle after Chancellorsville: Malvern Hill, the Seven Days' culminating artillery duel.
- **Scenario-shape decision:** keep Malvern Hill as a data-driven single-phase scenario. Repo evidence did not justify the T8 `phases[]` path: the playable lesson is one culminating defensive position, not sequential sectors. The battle follows the Fredericksburg/Shiloh/Chancellorsville single-objective pattern with CS attacker, US defender, `defaultFog:false`, and `assaultDoctrine:"cautious"` to model Lee's poorly coordinated/piecemeal assaults.
- **Combat-model decision:** no per-battle damage or firepower fudge. The Union edge comes from terrain/OOB/timing: a mild high-ground plateau, open exposed approach, stronger Union gun line, reinforcing batteries/infantry, Confederate approach woods/ravines and delayed waves. The focused probe scans for battle-specific damage/fudge keys and asserts all artillery uses the universal gun-count model with realistic crew counts.

- **Probe decision:** added `tools/probe-malvern-hill.mjs` as the battle's completion gate. It verifies historical/data guardrails, single-phase launch, cautious CS attacker, terrain cover (crest vs open approach), no wall-pattern import, universal gun-count artillery, no damage-fudge keys, reinforcement timing/idempotency, deterministic AI-vs-AI resolution, US-defender-favored 8-seed balance, passive US/CS launches, side-aware objective/end-note framing, menu/side-card rendering, and light roster regression.
- **Balance result:** seed 101 resolves as US timeout at 500s with US losses 1,336 and CS losses 6,545. The 8-seed focused balance is US 7/8, CS 1/8. This keeps the historical Union gun-line victory as the common outcome while preserving a Confederate alt-history path if the attack coheres.

US x / CS y` chip and `_fldPhaseTopParts().full` carries the `sectors US x - CS y` wording. No engine or scenario behavior changed for this fix.

## D84 тАФ Custom Battle Builder C4 complete: single-phase V1 authoring, validation, JSON, slots, launch contract тАФ [CODEX] (2026-06-18)
Aaron asked for a real usable custom scenario builder for the tactical field, preserving Classic and historical battles.
- **Scope decision:** ship a **single-phase V1** builder. Repo evidence supports authored `phases[]` data through T8, but not a safe phase-authoring UI. Phase editing is therefore deferred honestly until it can be validated and probed at the same standard as historical phase data.
- **Registry decision:** custom scenarios do not enter `fldScenarioRegistry()`. The canonical historical roster remains exact for probes and player-facing battle order. `fldScenarioData(id)` now checks historical data first, then asks `fldCustomScenarioData(id)` only for explicit `custom_...` IDs, so custom launches reuse the existing single-phase `fldScenarioInit` path without polluting the roster.
- **Field-size decision:** add resettable `FLD.BASE_FIELD_W/H` and reset field size at the start of every `fldInitSim`. Single-phase scenario data may set `field.w/h` after lookup; exiting and launching sandbox/historical battles resets to 1200x900, preventing map-size leakage.
- **Builder implementation:** new `src/tactical/T11-custom-battle.js` adds a first-class main-menu builder flow with metadata, sides/briefs, objective, field size, terrain hills/woods/walls/markers, OOB units, artillery/gun counts, reinforcement/deployment timing, optional leaders, supply, teaching, provenance, export/shareable JSON, import/round-trip, and six local persistence slots.

Custom battles use the universal gun-count artillery model; no per-custom battle damage/fudge knobs were added.
- **Probe decision:** add `tools/probe-custom-battle-builder.mjs` as the C4 focused gate. It verifies UI render, validation failures, valid scenario creation, JSON export/import round trip, UI malformed-import rejection, slot save/list/load/delete, explicit custom-ID scenario lookup, renderer-none launch contract, shared gun model, field-size reset after exit, no phase leakage, no Classic `G.battle`, and no historical registry contamination.
- **Verification:** `node tools/build.mjs` GATE OK; `node tools/probe-custom-battle-builder.mjs` 9/9; `node tools/probe-tactical-roster.mjs` 8/8; `node tools/probe-field.mjs` 13/13; `node tools/probe-bullrun.mjs` 15/15; `node tools/probe-malvern-hill.mjs` 24/24; `node tools/probe-antietam.mjs` 16/16; `node tools/probe-fredericksburg.mjs` 22/22; `node tools/probe-chancellorsville.mjs` 24/24; `node tools/probe-gettysburg.mjs` 16/16; `node tools/probe-shiloh.mjs` 29/29; `node tools/probe-officers.mjs` 15/15; `node tools/probe-logistics.mjs` 14/14; `node tools/probe-arms.mjs` 23/23; `node tools/probe-presets.mjs` 26/26; `node tools/probe-csplayer.mjs` 16/16; `node tools/probe-campaign-link.mjs` 16/16; `node tools/probe-tactical-visuals.mjs` 6/6; `node tools/bootprobe.mjs` ok=true with known/tolerated 404 resource console entries and no real errors; `node tools/t1probe.mjs` ok=true; `node tools/diag-classic.mjs` Classic paints (`nonBlank:346`, only pre-existing 404 resource messages); `git diff --check` clean.

## D86 тАФ VICKSBURG (Phase C-2 Western breadth): the 3-phase river-fortress siege finished + adversarially hardened тАФ [OPUS] (2026-06-20)
Finished the last uncompleted Codex project (the in-progress Vicksburg scenario left dirty in the working tree), brought it through the full PROPER VETTING gate, and fixed every confirmed adversarial-bug-hunt finding.
- **What it is:** Vicksburg, May 19тАУJuly 4 1863, as a THREE-PHASE siege on the T8 multi-phase engine тАФ **Stockade Redan (May 19) тЖТ the Forlorn Hope / Great Redoubt (May 22) тЖТ the Saps and the Mine (the 3rd Louisiana Redan, June 25)**. Citation-grade, anti-Lost-Cause ("dug out, not merely starved out"): the fall is attributed to Grant's maneuver isolating the city plus Union engineering, not hunger alone. `data/vicksburg.json` + registry line in `src/tactical/T1-bull-run.js` (menu rank 55, after Shiloh) + `tools/probe-vicksburg.mjs` (18 steps). Universal gun-count model only; no per-battle damage fudge.
- **Probe-capture fix:** `probe-vicksburg.mjs`'s Modern-3D readability screenshot used Playwright `page.screenshot()`, which hangs (30s readback timeout) on the live continuously-rendering WebGL canvas. Switched to the proven `probe-tactical-visuals` pattern тАФ render + `canvas.toDataURL()` in the same synchronous tick (reliable without `preserveDrawingBuffer`), writing `probe-vicksburg-3d.png` from base64 with a non-blank-size guard.
- **Roster guard:** `tools/probe-tactical-roster.mjs` `EXPECTED` set, menu-order, and button-id list updated to include `vicksburg` (the Codex left this un-updated, so the menu-order step had been failing 2/8).
- **Bug-hunt (25 agents, 4 diverse lenses ├Ч default-refute verify + completeness critic): 8 confirmed + 6 critic candidates, all material ones fixed:**
  - **Historical (HIGH):** Brig. Gen. Louis Hebert was misattributed to the Stockade Redan and stamped "Verified." That sector (Graveyard Road, vs Sherman's XV Corps) was held by **Maj. Gen. M.L. Smith's division** (Shoup's/Cockrell's troops); Hebert commanded a brigade in **Forney's division** at the **3rd Louisiana Redan** (the work named for his old regiment, site of the June 25 mine). Installed Smith at the Stockade (Phase 0) and relocated Hebert to the 3rd Louisiana Redan (Phases 1тАУ2), with honest provenance.
  - **Balance/teaching (HIGH):** the failed May assaults were INVERTED тАФ the dug-in defender bled more than the exposed attacker (P0 US:CS 0.65, P1 0.77, P2 0.15), teaching the literal opposite of the cards ("the assaults failed at great cost to the attacker," the Fredericksburg lesson). Root cause: the attacker fielded 1.5тАУ1.8├Ч more infantry plus a gun edge and stood off trading fire, so shooter-volume casualty attribution made the defender bleed. Rebalanced toward fire parity (trimmed the US assault fire-lines, cut the US assault-phase artillery to light-field levels, gave the fortress its historical pre-sited gun edge), and moderated the siege bloodbath (6.84:1 тЖТ ~3.8:1) by cutting the US siege-gun edge. **Result (8-seed sweep): P0 US:CS 1.93, P1 2.64 (attacker now pays), redans still hold 8/8, US still takes the siege 8/8, aggregate Vicksburg falls 8/8.**
  - **Scoring (MEDIUM):** the historical CS/CS/US outcome sat exactly on the draw-band edge (diff 0.5 with a strict `< 0.5`). Changed the siege `scoreWeight` 2.5 тЖТ 3 so history lands a clear margin (US 3 / CS 2, diff 1.0).
  - **Probe rigor (MEDIUM):** the gate checked only that the redans "held," never the casualty DIRECTION, so it green-lit the inversion at 8/8. Added a casualty-direction assertion (mean US cas > CS cas on the held assault phases) to `tools/probe-vicksburg.mjs`; built `tools/sweep-vicksburg.mjs` as the per-phase A/B harness.
  - **T12 readability (MEDIUM):** `src/tactical/T12-3d-readability.js` created SpriteMaterials + selection ring/staff geometries every `_m3dDecorateUnits` and never disposed them when `_m3dBuildUnits` cleared the group (GPU leak). Added a T12-owned disposal registry (`__M3D._t12Disp`) disposed each cycle, skipping the shared cached badge texture. Gated the selection-halo richness on `_m3dLowTier()` (single thin ring on the Intel UHD-617 floor).
  - **WCAG (HIGH critic):** the strength-count text floated over the variable green/amber/red bar fill. Now drawn over a fixed dark pill (#fff4d7 on ~#0a0c0f, well past AA), independent of the fill.
  - Copy fixes: the Forlorn Hope note's false "the engine scales this up" language, and the draw end-note that asserted "the assaults have failed" even in draw states where an assault succeeded.
- **Verification:** `node tools/build.mjs` GATE OK; `probe-vicksburg` 18/18, 0 pe (assaultCostUStoCS stockade 1.96 / forlorn 2.71, totalGuns 56); `probe-tactical-roster` 8/8; bullrun 15/15; malvern-hill 24/24; antietam 16/16; fredericksburg 22/22; chancellorsville 24/24; gettysburg 16/16; shiloh 29/29; field 13/13; officers 15/15; logistics 14/14; arms 23/23; presets 26/26; csplayer 16/16; campaign-link 16/16; `probe-tactical-visuals` 8/8 with 0 pageerrors and `textureWarnings:0`; bootprobe ok (10 tolerated 404s); t1probe ok; `diag-classic` Classic paints (`nonBlank:346`); `git diff --check` clean. The sim engine (T0тАУT8) was untouched, so non-Vicksburg battles are behaviorally unchanged.
- **Known limitation (LOW, deferred):** passive (player-side, non-`autoBoth`) headless resolution is side-asymmetric тАФ with the player's own side left un-driven the stronger garrison tends to win regardless of side. This is a demo-only artifact (real play has a human commanding); the probe asserts only termination + a valid winner. Noted for a future passive-AI pass.

## D87 тАФ TACTICAL ENGINEERING CORPS, increment 1: FIELD ENTRENCHMENTS тАФ [OPUS] (2026-06-20)
First increment of Aaron's run-k Engineering Corps directive. He answered "all of the above" (entrench + abatis + pontoons) when asked which to build first, so the corps ships as one module (`src/tactical/T13-engineering.js`) in vetted increments; this is the entrenchment foundation.
- **What it is:** a player brigade ordered to ENTRENCH (key **E**, a control-bar button, help-copy updated) digs in where it stands and, over ~70 sim-seconds, earns COVER rising toward a parapet-grade multiplier (the war's drift toward trench warfare). Marching off the works (>26yd from the dig site) abandons them and the cover fades.
- **B-5 realism coupling (the directive's requirement):** dig SPEED and COVER strength read the realism slider via a scale derived from `__FIELD.sev.attrition` (0.7 Arcade / 1.0 Balanced / 1.3 Historian). **Arcade digs fast for modest cover (├Ч1.43); Historian digs slow for strong cover (├Ч1.81); Balanced ├Ч1.62.**
- **FACING-AWARE (bug-hunt fix):** the parapet shelters its FRONT тАФ `fldEngCover(u, fromX, fromZ)` scales the earned bonus by the shooter/attacker bearing (full in the front arc, half on the flank, none in the rear), so a flank/rear maneuver still counters fixed works and matches the one-sided berm we render.
- **Architecture (byte-identical):** new T13 module + 9 guarded seams in T0 (`fldResolveFire`/`fldResolveMelee` cover, `fldSimStep` entrench step, `fldKey` E, the control-bar button, `fldRenderHud` line, `fld2dDraw` + the 3D build/sync hooks, `fld3dDispose` ref-nulling). Every seam is a `typeof fldEng* === "function"` call, and `fldEngCover` returns EXACTLY 1 for any unit that never dug, so `cover *= fldEngCover(tgt)` is byte-for-byte unchanged. Entrenchment is a **PLAYER tool** in this increment тАФ no scenario/AI triggers it, so every AI-vs-AI baseline is byte-identical. 2D dirt parapet + 3D dirt berm (low-tier aware, leak-managed). reduceMotion honored (static works).
- **Probe:** `tools/probe-engineering-corps.mjs` (8/8) тАФ wiring + identity, dig-over-time + cover rise, the realism scaling, the front-cover-reduces-fire / rear-shot-bypasses A/B, abandon-on-march, the AI-baseline byte-identity gate, 2D/HUD render, and routing/empty-selection sanity.
- **Bug-hunt (17 agents, 3 lenses): 1 confirmed (the omnidirectional cover тАФ fixed facing-aware) + critics triaged:** melee charger-exposed is the correct base convention (kept, made facing-aware); the multi-phase 3D works self-heal via `fld3dSyncEng`'s stale-disposal; the fog-ghost-works item is moot while entrenchment is player-only (deferred to the AI/scenario increment).
- **Verification:** build GATE OK; `probe-engineering-corps` 8/8; full no-regression suite byte-identical (field/bullrun/shiloh/fog/ai/autopause + all battle probes + officers/logistics/arms/presets/csplayer/campaign-link); `probe-tactical-visuals` 8/8 (`textureWarnings:0`); diag-classic `nonBlank:346`; bootprobe/t1probe ok; 0 pageerrors. Sim engine baselines byte-for-byte unchanged.
- **Next (the rest of "all of the above"):** ABATIS / obstacles, then PONTOON bridging (needs a new river terrain feature) тАФ each its own vetted increment extending T13.

## D88 тАФ TACTICAL ENGINEERING CORPS, increment 2: ABATIS / OBSTACLES (the axe) тАФ [OPUS] (2026-06-21)
Second of the locked "all of the above" engineering effects (D87). Authored 2026-06-20 (left uncommitted/unvetted when the prior Codex session ran out of usage тАФ that session's only landed work was the browser-probe Seatbelt guard, separately committed); brought through the full PROPER VETTING gate + an adversarial bug-hunt and pushed 2026-06-21.
- **What it is:** a selected player INFANTRY brigade's pioneer detail builds a capped timber belt across its front (key **B** / "Abatis" button). Enemy troops forcing the belt are SLOWED (`fldEngMoveFactor`), DISORDERED once per crossing (a morale + fatigue hit, `fldEngMoveGate` with a per-unit `_engObsTouch` latch), and fire RAGGEDLY (`fldEngFireFactor` ├Ч0.72) until cohesion recovers. A nearby brigade CLEARS a lane (key **X** / "Clear"). Anti-stalemate cap of 4 belts/side.
- **B-5 realism coupling (the directive's requirement):** build time, clear time, the slow factor, and the disorder magnitude all scale with `fldEngRealism()` тАФ Historian bites harder and builds/clears slower than Arcade.
- **Architecture (byte-identical):** the abatis half of the T13 module + guarded T0 seams (`fldMoveFactor` gains a `u` param and multiplies the obstacle factor; `fldResolveFire` multiplies the fire factor; `fldStepMovement` calls the move-gate; `fldInitSim` resets; `fldOnOver` appends the end-card; DOM buttons + keys B/X) + a T8 `_fldBuildPhase` per-phase reset. Every seam returns an EXACT identity (1 / null) with no live belt, and the mechanic is **player-only** (no AI builds) тАФ so every AI-vs-AI baseline is byte-for-byte unchanged. 2D stake-line + 3D crossed-timber render (fog-gated, low-tier aware, leak-managed); a Mahan-sourced teaching end-card (Dennis Hart Mahan, *A Treatise on Field Fortification*, 1861).
- **Probe:** `tools/probe-engineering-corps.mjs` extended **8/8 тЖТ 15/15** тАФ adds ABATIS build/cap, contact disorder (once, then recovers), clear+realism, the multi-phase reset, abandoned-belt decay, unique ids, and routing immunity.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt (16 agents, Opus finders+verify+critic): 8 confirmed + 4 critic gaps, all triaged.** Fixed: **HIGH** тАФ abatis belts LEAKED across phases in multi-phase battles (Vicksburg/Antietam/Gettysburg): `fldEngReset` ran only at launch, so a phase-1 belt kept slowing/disordering phase-2 enemies at stale coordinates тЖТ added `fldEngPhaseReset()` called from `_fldBuildPhase` (drops the prior sector's belts, KEEPS `_engUsed` so the aggregate teaching card still fires). **MED** тАФ an abandoned immature belt never decayed and permanently consumed an `ABATIS_MAX_SIDE` slot тЖТ now decays like an abandoned entrenchment (strength < 0.2 тЖТ fade + splice). **MED** тАФ abatis render ignored fog-of-war тЖТ mirror the entrenchment fog gate in 2D + 3D. **LOW** тАФ same-tick belt id collision (`Math.round(t*10)+i`) тЖТ a monotonic `_engObsSeq` counter. **LOW** тАФ routing units were still morale-docked by the move-gate тЖТ added the routing guard the rest of the module already uses. **Kept (deliberate):** entrench+abatis on one brigade is historically correct (the entrenched line with an abatis apron тАФ Fredericksburg/Cold Harbor); one disorder shock per continuous crossing is an acceptable model.
- **Verification:** build GATE OK; `probe-engineering-corps` 15/15, 0 pe; full no-regression GREEN (50 probes incl. all battle/tactical/strategic suites + diag-classic `nonBlank:346`, 0 pageerrors). Also corrected a D86 leftover: `probe-custom-battle-builder` was red since Vicksburg shipped (its EXPECTED registry omitted `vicksburg`) тЖТ now 9/9.
- **Commits:** `679ee7d` (Codex Seatbelt probe-guard + repo hygiene: untracked `.tmp/` scratch + `tools/shots/*.json`, gitignored `.codex/`) тЖТ `02b2dd8` (abatis D88). Pushed `daaf1b1..02b2dd8` to `adhanke-star/History-Video-Game` main.
- **Next (the last of "all of the above"):** PONTOON bridging тАФ a NEW river/water terrain feature + a bridge-laying engineer step + a crossing gate (fordable vs requires-pontoon, realism-gated). The Bull Run terrain already has Young's Branch / the Stone Bridge to build against. Completes the Engineering Corps; then C tactical breadth (Chickamauga/Chattanooga, C3 USCT).

## D89 тАФ TACTICAL ENGINEERING CORPS, increment 3: PONTOON BRIDGING (the last increment тАФ the corps is complete) тАФ [OPUS] (2026-06-21)
The third and final increment of Aaron's locked "all of the above" Engineering Corps (entrench + abatis + pontoons), all in `src/tactical/T13-engineering.js`. Adds a real **river/water terrain feature that gates movement** + a **bridge-laying engineer step** + a **crossing gate** (fordable vs requires-pontoon), realism-coupled per the V1-CHECKLIST Phase-F requirement. With this, Phase F's Tactical Engineering Corps is **DONE**.
- **What it is:** an OPT-IN river (`__FIELD.terrain.rivers[]`) runs across the field; it is impassable except at a **crossing**. Crossings: a **shallow ford** (always passable, but slow + fatiguing), a **deep ford** (passable only at low realism тАФ at Balanced/Historian it must be bridged), and a player-laid **pontoon bridge** (key **N** / "Pontoon" button): an infantry pioneer detail on the near bank lays a bridge over realism-scaled time, opening a fast crossing corridor. Surfaced via the Skirmish **"River crossing"** ground option (and an `opts.river` sandbox flag for the focused probe).
- **B-5 coupling (the explicit "make it make sense" requirement):** `fldEngRealism()` (from `__FIELD.sev.attrition`) scales the **sapper/pontoon build speed**, the **ford slow factor**, AND **deep-ford fordability** (deep ford open only when realism тЙд `DEEP_FORD_CAP` 0.85 тЖТ Arcade fords it, Balanced/Historian need a pontoon). The **strategic Engineer Works Corps** (`bridgeArmy(C).engineering`, 57-engineering) is wired onto the field via `__FIELD.engCorpsSpeed` (set in T2 `fldCampaignCondition`): a stronger corps lays bridges faster тАФ the A1 anchor, exactly as B-4 wired the Cannon Corps onto the field battery. Standalone launches stay `engCorpsSpeed=1` (byte-identical).
- **Architecture / byte-identity:** the active gate REUSES the two T0 seams reserved for it тАФ `fldEngMoveFactor` (ford slow) + `fldEngMoveGate` (returns a clamped bank point for an illegal water step). New: `fldEngInstallRiver`, `fldEngCrossAt` (the crossing classifier), `_fldRiverNearest/_fldRiverBankPoint/_fldEngBridgeSite`, `fldSelPontoon`, the pontoon loop in `fldEngStep`, `fldEngDrawWater2d` (+ ford/pontoon), `fld3dBuildWater` + pontoon sync in `fld3dSyncEng`. **NO shipped scenario declares `terrain.rivers` and the AI never lays a pontoon**, so every AI-vs-AI baseline is byte-for-byte unchanged (every river/pontoon read is gated by `rv && rv.length` / `engPontoons`). The river is reset per-launch (`fldEngReset`) and per-phase (`fldEngPhaseReset`). 2D slate-water band + boat-deck pontoons + ford stepping-stones + labels (CVD-safe: glyphs + labels, not color-alone; reduceMotion-safe); 3D water plane + pontoon boats/deck (leak-managed). A citation-grade teaching card (research+verify workflow, 30/38 claims survived adversarial verification): Fredericksburg/Rappahannock pontoon delay + the laying under Barksdale's fire (50th NY Engineers) + the ~2,100-ft James River bridge of June 1864.
- **DECISION тАФ Bull Run's creek stays cosmetic (decide-&-log, no fork surfaced):** the prompt noted Bull Run already has Young's Branch / the Stone Bridge "to build against." Making those *live* obstacles would change a shipped, probed battle's movement/balance (a regression + a byte-identity break). So the active river ships as the OPT-IN sandbox/skirmish feature; Bull Run's markers remain cosmetic (the teaching card references the Rappahannock as the historical anchor). Activating a scenario's creek as a live river is a documented future extension (re-vet that battle first). This does not contradict any prior decision.
- **DECISION тАФ player-tool this increment; AI river-pathing deferred:** like AI-entrenchment (D87) and AI-abatis (D88), the AI does not path to fords / lay pontoons. So a river skirmish frames the PLAYER as the attacker forcing the crossing (the river is installed between the player's home edge and the objective, either side) while the AI defends the far bank. AI river-assault waypointing is the named T13 extension point.
- **Probe:** `tools/probe-engineering-corps.mjs` **15/15 тЖТ 22/22** тАФ adds the river install + water block, the ford slow + dry-land identity, realism fordability (deep ford Arcade-open / Historian-closed), the pontoon build тЖТ open crossing + blocked-elsewhere, pontoon realism + wash-out, the water/teaching render, and a **RIVER LEAK GUARD** regression step.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt (19 agents, Opus finders+verify+critic): 8 confirmed + 6 critic gaps, all fixed.** **HIGH** тАФ the water gate's origin test (`!fldEngCrossAt(x0,z0)`) only treated a DRY origin as blockable, so a unit on an OPEN ford could **sidestep off it and wade the whole band**; fixed to block entering blocked water from anywhere except already-blocked water (so a mired unit can still crawl out) + a **midpoint sample** so a tangential march clipping a bend is also caught. **HIGH** тАФ the 3D water plane was buried under the opaque terrain (center `terrainHтИТ1.6`) тЖТ raised to a thin sheet sitting on the ground; ford strips lifted clear (no z-fight). **HIGH** тАФ a brigade ordered across impassable water **marched in place forever, bleeding fatigue to 100** (soft deadlock) тЖТ `fldStepMovement` now settles a no-progress river clamp to HOLD at the bank and skips the march fatigue (eg-gated тЖТ byte-identical). **HIGH** тАФ the river skirmish was degenerate for a CS player (objective on the far bank) тЖТ the river is now placed by player side so the player always forces the crossing. **MED** тАФ no aria-live cue when the gate refused a crossing тЖТ a once-per-halt announce + a flag-driven HUD "Halted at the water" line. **LOW** тАФ wrong "no pioneer free" message on a duplicate-span order; pontoon `side` stamp + per-side cap. **Kept (deliberate):** live realismтЖТfordability coupling (a unit caught mid-deep-ford when realism rises just slogs out at 0.34├Ч тАФ thematic, no trap).
- **Verification:** build GATE OK; `probe-engineering-corps` 22/22, 0 pe; full no-regression GREEN (field 13 ┬╖ bullrun 15 ┬╖ shiloh 29 ┬╖ malvern 24 ┬╖ antietam 16 ┬╖ fredericksburg 22 ┬╖ chancellorsville 24 ┬╖ gettysburg 16 ┬╖ vicksburg 18 ┬╖ roster 8 ┬╖ visuals ok/texWarn 0 ┬╖ custom-builder 9 ┬╖ fog 13 ┬╖ ai 15 ┬╖ autopause 13 ┬╖ campaign-link 16 ┬╖ officers 15 ┬╖ logistics 14 ┬╖ arms 23 ┬╖ presets 26 ┬╖ csplayer 16; diag-classic `nonBlank:346`; boot/t1 ok; 0 pageerrors) тЖТ byte-identity intact. WCAG-AA: all new HUD/card colors тЙе4.5:1 (9.16 / 9.21 / 11.27 / 10.94 / 5.93), CVD-safe. Also fixed the help overlay to add the B/X/N engineering keys (they had been omitted in increments 1тАУ2).
- **Next:** the Engineering Corps is complete тЖТ Phase C tactical breadth (Chickamauga/Chattanooga, then C3 USCT battles).

## D90 тАФ PHASE C-2 ┬╖ CHICKAMAUGA, the river of death (the 3-phase Western epic: the woods тЖТ Longstreet's breakthrough тЖТ Thomas at Snodgrass Hill / Horseshoe Ridge) тАФ [OPUS] (2026-06-21)
The Western theater continues after Shiloh + Vicksburg with the bloodiest battle of the West, built as a 3-phase epic on the gated T8 multi-phase engine. New `data/chickamauga.json` + one registry line in `src/tactical/T1-bull-run.js` (menu rank 60) + `tools/probe-chickamauga.mjs` + `tools/sweep-chickamauga.mjs`. Universal gun-count model only; no per-battle damage fudge (D74).
- **FRAMING (decide-&-log, contradicts nothing):** the C2 "Chickamauga/Chattanooga" checklist item is built as a matched PAIR of separate 3-phase epics (the Antietam/Gettysburg precedent), each its own vetted milestone тАФ **this milestone = Chickamauga; next = Chattanooga** (the US-offensive reversal; design brief drafted at `.tmp/chattanooga-design.md`). **Top-level `attacker: CS` / `defender: US` across all 3 phases** тАФ the Army of the Cumberland fought on the defensive throughout, so the CS player takes the offensive (Bragg/Longstreet) and the US player holds (Thomas). Cleaner than Vicksburg's US-attacker-throughout, and sets Chattanooga up as the US-attacker MIRROR.
- **THE 3 PHASES:** **P0 The Battle in the Woods (Sep 19)** тАФ a confused meeting engagement in dense timber; fog-of-war OFF but heavy `woods` terrain carries the blind-fighting theme (fog-of-war ON would defender-lock the phase тАФ see the engine-grain note); the Union line HOLDS the road (historical тАФ the breakthrough came the next day). **P1 Longstreet's Breakthrough (Sep 20, the Brotherton gap)** тАФ the Wood gap order pulls a US division out of line at the exact moment Longstreet's column strikes; CS pours through and routs the right; the decisive **scoreWeight-3** phase. **P2 The Rock of Chickamauga (Sep 20 afternoon)** тАФ Thomas holds Snodgrass Hill / Horseshoe Ridge (`assaultDoctrine: "cautious"` + hill + breastworks + a timed Steedman/Granger relief), a Union defensive SUCCESS in which the CS assault pays the failed-assault price.
- **RESEARCH+VERIFY (Workflow тАФ Sonnet finders ├Ч Opus adversarial verify + synthesis):** corrected real errors before authoring (the Vicksburg-lesson, applied up front): **Hood wounded Sep 20 / Maj. Gen.** (not Sep 19 / Lt. Gen.); **Helm in Breckinridge's division, not Cleburne's**; **Cheatham restored**; **Granger & W.H.T. Walker = Maj. Gen.**; **Loring removed** (not at Chickamauga); the gap-reporter flagged (Kellogg vs Bond disputed); the **"River of Death"** Cherokee gloss shipped ONLY as disputed folk etymology, never as fact.
- **BALANCE (AI-vs-AI, 32 seeds, deterministic тАФ D74, no fudge):** P0 US-holds 32/32 (mutual bloodbath ~2,400 each); P1 **CS breakthrough 32/32** (US routed cheaply, US:CS ~5.1; weight 3); P2 **US-holds 32/32** with the CS attacker paying **CS:US ~3.0**; **aggregate CS 32/32** (CS 3 / US 2). A human US player who wins P1 (closes the Wood gap) OVERTURNS the aggregate (the alt-history hinge). The CS, who won the field, **bled MORE in aggregate** (~70k vs ~63k / 8 seeds) тАФ the costly-victory teaching, now asserted by the probe.
- **ENGINE-GRAIN LESSONS (logged for the Chattanooga build + future battles):** (1) the objective-hold mechanic favors whoever has more bodies ON the objective + cover + fog, **largely independent of `assaultDoctrine`** тАФ to make an ATTACKER seize, give it a strength edge + open approach + few defender bodies; to make a DEFENDER hold, give it 3+ divisions + hill + breastworks + a timed reinforcement + cautious doctrine. (2) **The phases share ONE RNG seed stream** тАФ tuning an earlier phase shifts later phases' outcomes; tune in order, re-sweep the whole battle, and expect a "true 50/50" phase to be bistable (prefer a clear historical lean). (3) Weight the decisive historical phase 3, others 1 (total 5). (4) **fog-of-war ON strongly aids the defender** тАФ model a historically-foggy attacker-must-win phase via dense woods + fog-OFF. (5) **Write the casualty-DIRECTION + winner guards into the probe from the start** тАФ every confirmed bug-hunt finding here was a missing casualty-direction/winner guard.
- **ADVERSARIAL BUG-HUNT (Workflow, 10 Opus agents тАФ 6 diverse-lens finders ├Ч default-refute verify + a completeness critic): 2 confirmed + 3 critic gaps, ALL fixed.** HIGH (critic тАФ the Vicksburg wrong-rank-under-Verified class): **Charles Harker mis-ranked "Brig. Gen." тАФ he was a COLONEL at the battle** (like Hans Heg; his brigadier-generalcy dated to Sep 20 but came afterward) тЖТ corrected to **Col. Charles Harker** + an anti-"Brig. Gen. Harker" fact-check guard. Plus 4 probe-rigor guards: P1 breakthrough casualty-direction (US:CS тЙе2.5), P0 winner gate (тЙе7/8), P1 win-by-SEIZE (winBy "hold"), and the aggregate "winner bled more" guard. (The 2 confirmed were both probe-coverage gaps; the Harker error was the one real content defect.)
- **VERIFICATION (PROPER VETTING, D53-OPS):** GATE OK; `probe-chickamauga` **18/18**, 0 pe; full no-regression GREEN (bullrun 15 ┬╖ malvern 24 ┬╖ antietam 16 ┬╖ fredericksburg 22 ┬╖ chancellorsville 24 ┬╖ gettysburg 16 ┬╖ shiloh 29 ┬╖ vicksburg 18 ┬╖ roster 8 ┬╖ field 13 ┬╖ officers 15 ┬╖ logistics 14 ┬╖ arms 23 ┬╖ presets 26 ┬╖ csplayer 16 ┬╖ campaign-link 16 ┬╖ fog 13 ┬╖ ai 15 ┬╖ autopause 13 ┬╖ **custom-builder 9** [its EXPECTED registry baseline updated to include `chickamauga` тАФ the recurring D86/D88 gotcha] ┬╖ engineering-corps 22 ┬╖ **tactical-visuals** 10 scenes incl. live Chickamauga 2D/3D, textureWarnings:0); diag-classic nonBlank 346; boot/t1 ok; **0 pageerrors**. WCAG: no new color CSS (content flows into the already-AA shared T1/T8 components). Committed + pushed. **NEXT: Chattanooga (the US-offensive reversal тАФ Orchard Knob тЖТ Lookout Mountain тЖТ Missionary Ridge; brief at `.tmp/chattanooga-design.md`), then C3 USCT battles (the Crater ┬╖ New Market Heights ┬╖ Olustee ┬╖ Nashville).**
