## D92 тАФ ROSTER HISTORY-ACCURACY HARDENING (all 9 shipped battles) + the accurate-inputs principle тАФ [OPUS, Aaron-directed] (2026-06-21)
Aaron asked whether the full Chattanooga-grade rigor (citation-grade research + adversarial verify, casualty-direction guards, balance sweep) had been applied to the battles already built. It had NOT for the 7 pre-Opus battles (the Codex/early-built C1 Eastern marquee + Shiloh + Bull Run); only Vicksburg + Chickamauga (Opus, bug-hunted) had the adversarial history pass.
- **Adversarial audit (Workflow, 9 Opus historians + critic + a consolidated casualty-direction sweep `tools/sweep-all-battles.mjs`):** found **15 HIGH-severity wrong facts shipped under "Verified" stamps** тАФ overwhelmingly the **rank-at-the-battle** class (a later/posthumous/backdated promotion applied to the battle date), plus wrong-division (the Vicksburg "Hebert" class) and a **dead officer commanding a battery**. ALL FIXED, each annotated in-file:
  - **Malvern Hill (4):** Hunt Brig.Gen.тЖТ**Col.** (file self-contradicted, calling him Col. elsewhere); Jackson Lt.Gen.тЖТ**Maj.Gen.** (no CSA Lt.Gen. grade until Oct 1862 тАФ the Hood-at-Chickamauga anachronism); Porter Maj.Gen.тЖТ**Brig.Gen.** (MG dated Jul 4, 3 days after); Hooker Brig.Gen.тЖТ**Maj.Gen.** (under-ranked).
  - **Chancellorsville (4):** Rodes Maj.Gen.тЖТ**Brig.Gen.** (MG conferred after, for this flank attack); Berry **III Corps** not II; Paxton's Stonewall Brigade re-attached to **Colston's division** not A.P. Hill's (Hebert-class); Fairview battery **Capt. Hazzard (DEAD, d. Aug 1862) тЖТ Capt. Clermont L. Best**.
  - **Shiloh (3):** Breckinridge Maj.Gen.тЖТ**Brig.Gen.** (MG Apr 14, 8 days after); Bragg led the **RIGHT** wing not the left (contradicted its own teaching card); W.H.L. Wallace died **Apr 10** not May 10.
  - **Gettysburg (3):** Doubleday & Early Brig.Gen.тЖТ**Maj.Gen.** (both under-ranked); Stannard's Vermont Bde **I Corps** not III.
  - **Vicksburg (1):** Martin L. Smith Maj.Gen.тЖТ**Brig.Gen.** (├Ч3 fields; MG dated Nov 1863, 4 months AFTER the surrender).
  - Plus ~12 medium/low (Antietam Benjamin 1st-Lt + **4 not 6 guns** + Graham Capt; Shiloh Wood-as-reserveтЖТ**Chalmers's evening assault** / Taylor-on-Battery-AтЖТ**Peter P. Wood** / TrabueтЖТRobert P., infantry not artillery; Bull Run Pelham's-batteryтЖТ**Alburtis's** / Elzey 13th VA + 1st Md Infantry; Fredericksburg Ransom echelon reframe; Gettysburg Archer captured at **Willoughby Run** not the Railroad Cut; Chickamauga Negley **court of inquiry** not court-martial + Cheatham's Preston Smith brigade added).
  - **SURFACED, deliberately NOT auto-fixed (genuine source conflict, per Aaron's rule):** Bull Run **Heintzelman** (Col. vs Brig. Gen. тАФ regular-vs-volunteer commission conflict) and Antietam **Mansfield** (his Maj.Gen.-of-volunteers dated Jul 18 1862 predates the battle тАФ the data's "Maj. Gen." is defensible; the auditor's downgrade is contestable). Left as-is for a future editor.
- **THE LOCKED PRINCIPLE (Aaron, verbatim during the pass):** "I want skill and gameplay and weapon type etc to impact outcomes тАФ that's the priority over staying absolutely accurate to history. I don't want the no-lost-cause to be over-interpreted." Outcomes EMERGE from skill + weapon type + terrain + tactics via the D74 universal model. History enters ONLY as the **default equipment** (accurate soldier/gun counts, weapons, terrain, doctrine) so the **probable** result lands near the historical one *because the inputs are true* тАФ **NEVER an output gate forcing a casualty direction or winner.** So we **DROPPED** the planned "fix Antietam so the CS doesn't out-bleed the Union" balance refight and the hard historical-direction probe gates; `sweep-all-battles.mjs` stays a DIAGNOSTIC. The only casualty guards kept/added are **system validations** (cover reduces casualties, rifled out-ranges smoothbore, more guns = more fire) that keep the game LEGIBLE (a player can read the visible OOB and forecast probable odds + casualty %). A teaching-text-vs-sim divergence is the intended "your war vs history," not a defect. (Full principle: memory `civilwar-roster-accuracy-principle`.)
- **Verification:** ALL edits are labels/notes only EXCEPT one accurate gun-count (Antietam Benjamin 6тЖТ4) + one unit re-identification keeping stats (Shiloh WoodтЖТChalmers). `node tools/build.mjs` GATE OK; full re-vet GREEN тАФ all 9 battle probes (bullrun 15 ┬╖ malvern 24 ┬╖ antietam 16 ┬╖ fredericksburg 22 ┬╖ chancellorsville 24 ┬╖ gettysburg 16 ┬╖ shiloh 29 ┬╖ vicksburg 18 ┬╖ chickamauga 18) + roster 8 + custom-builder 9, **each battle's own balance assertions still green** (outcomes byte-preserved), diag-classic `nonBlank:346`, 0 pageerrors; broad tactical-systems suite + boot/t1 green. New `tools/sweep-all-battles.mjs` consolidated casualty-direction diagnostic.
- **D92-verify (2026-06-21, resumed session after an API-error hang):** the D92 work was on disk but uncommitted when the prior session died on a 529. Before committing, an **independent adversarial re-verification** (Workflow: 1 Opus historian per battle + critic, re-run for the 2 that 529'd) checked every asserted correction against 2+ sources to catch a "fix" that was itself wrong. The 6/9 + 2 re-run + chancellorsville came back GO; it found **4 more items, ALL FIXED before commit:** (1) **Bull Run** тАФ the D92 `cs_elzey` gloss "(Elzey's own regiment)" was attached to the 10th/13th Virginia, but Elzey's own regiment was the **1st Maryland** (he had colonel'd it); the 13th Va. was A. P. Hill's, the 10th Gibbons's тАФ gloss moved to the 1st Maryland (a wrong fact D92 *introduced*). (2) **Shiloh** тАФ `us_buell_ammen` was "Brig. Gen." but Jacob **Ammen was a COLONEL** (24th Ohio) at Shiloh; his BG dated Jul 16 1862, after the battle (the anachronistic-rank class, *missed* by D92) тЖТ Col. (3) **Antietam** тАФ `us_battery_b` (Gibbon's Battery B, 4th U.S.) was tagged `rifled` but was **six 12-pdr Napoleons (smoothbore)** тАФ its own note already said "double canister," the smoothbore signature; corrected `rifledтЖТsmooth` (an accurate-weapon input per the D92-locked principle; the antietam probe stayed 16/16 so the Cornfield outcome is byte-preserved тАФ outcome-neutral). (4) **Malvern Hill** тАФ D92 had *over-promoted* `us_hooker` BGтЖТMaj. Gen. by his May-5-1862 date-of-rank, but Hooker's MG commission was **issued Jul 26 1862 (after the battle) and backdated**; the canonical Seven Days OOB lists him **BG**, exactly as the file (correctly) keeps Porter/Couch/Kearny тАФ reverted to Brig. Gen. for internal consistency (a wrong fact D92 *introduced*). Net beyond the original D92: 3 label fixes + 1 outcome-neutral weapon-tag fix. Re-vet GREEN (full battle + roster + custom + systems suite + diag-classic `nonBlank:346` + boot/t1, 0 pageerrors). THEN committed + pushed.

## D93 тАФ "THE SOLDIER'S STORY" character/narrative pillar тАФ captured + scheduled тАФ [AARON] (AskUserQuestion + directive, 2026-06-21)
Aaron's vision for an individual character/narrative layer, modeled on EA-Sports rosters. Captured here + memory `civilwar-soldiers-story-pillar`; **scheduled AFTER the C+E roadmap** (his choice) тАФ NOT built now.
- **Spec:** a complete **prosopographical database** тАФ *every identifiable individual* in the modeled battles, each with **bio, stats/ratings, character history, portrait (procedural now / PD photo Phase H), and team (armyтЖТcorpsтЖТdivisionтЖТbrigadeтЖТregimentтЖТcompany)** тАФ plus a **"play as anyone" whole-war mode**: pick any identified person, choose **when + where to start**, proceed from their **REAL rank and position** at that moment, then play forward into alt-history.
- **Aaron's 3 scoping answers (AskUserQuestion):** (1) granularity = **"every named individual found"** (exhaustive); (2) sequencing = **AFTER C+E** (finish Chattanooga + C3 USCT + the E strategic arc first); (3) shape = **unified journey-mode pillar** (merge with the D91 loot/survival journey mode; design the playthrough + interpersonal/**romance** threads as one deliberate pillar).
- **Build order (bottom-up тАФ the data is the substrate):** (1) granular OOB + per-person/regiment **detail cards** (DATA, reuses teaching cards, NO tactical-engine change тАФ brigades stay one marker per the D68 zoom-deferral); (2) codex **person/unit axis** (D34.3, Phase E/S4); (3) **individual playthrough mode** (the thread connecting tacticalтЖФstrategicтЖФnarrative; = the D91 journey mode + a narrative spine); (4) **interpersonal/romance** (women-in-the-war / USCT / immigrant hooks; period-honest, anti-Lost-Cause). The real SYSTEM work is the **career/trajectory model** (each person's whole-war path) + the **start-anywhere engine**; the roster is large-but-bounded content.
- **Hard dependency:** accurate rank+position+unit per person тАФ **the D92 roster hardening is the first roster data** and a prerequisite for "start from real rank."

## D94 тАФ THE RATING SYSTEM (the OVR / "Madden layer") тАФ designed + build authorized тАФ [AARON] (AskUserQuestion + 3 directives, 2026-06-21)
A Madden-style **1тАУ100 OVR + badges/abilities** for soldiers, officers, and brigades, the substrate for the D93 Soldier's Story. Full design law in **`RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN.md`** (a 3-lens design Workflow: B sim-accurate-input spine + C prosopography data substrate + A Madden Star/Superstar/X-Factor feel, judged + synthesized; verified against the live engine).
- **The keystone (honors D74/D92):** ratings FULLY decide casualties + winners тАФ but *through the inputs, not by editing the scoreboard*. A documented persona is *derived* into true attributes that *seed* the levers the engine already reads (`xp`, `quality`тЖТ`cmdBonus`, `weapon`, `radius`, `fate`, `cohesion`, bounded `sev.*`) ONCE at build/preset-apply, then the normal combat model runs on them тЖТ the strong unit dominates *emergently* (and can still be out-played). The ONLY forbidden act (the "output wall", build-gate-asserted) is a handler writing `cas`/`aCas`/`bCas`/victory/`tgt.men` or out-of-band `sev.*` **directly** at resolution time (the scripted "higher rating тЗТ auto-win" hack тАФ it would make the sim a cutscene and kill the teaching). One spine, anchored at 64 тЖТ a neutral unit is byte-identical to Classic.
- **Unifies, does not duplicate:** the officer OVR **is** `_cmdGenRating` (`0.55*skill+0.45*reputation`); reuses `commandLeadership` (the 42тАУ88 bridge), `_cmdLeadWord`, `_cmdTraitBar`; persona inserts only at the FRONT (personaтЖТ`gen.skill`). No parallel rating, no second bridge.
- **Aaron's 4 locked directives (AskUserQuestion + follow-ups):** (1) **BUILD THE FULL SYSTEM NOW** тАФ R-0тЖТR-4 reprioritized *ahead of* Chattanooga (pulls D93 forward); (2) **X-Factor feel = DRAMATIC Madden surge** (visible glow + announce + strong swing, still hard-capped under `CMD_BONUS_CAP 0.9` тАФ the cap, not the feel, is the wall); (3) **negatives = VERIFIED + plainly named** (Bragg "Piecemeal", McClellan "The Slows" тАФ anti-Lost-Cause rigor applies to flaws too, тЙе2 sources); (4) **tier scale = AтАУF report-card** (A+ тЙе90 "Legendary" club, then A/B/C/D/F тАФ NO gaming "S"; neutral 64 = C).
- **"Integrated in ALL layers" (Aaron directive):** the OVR surfaces + bites in the strategic President's Desk (appointment pool/cabinet/command OVR+grade+badges), the War-Effort army-quality readouts, **auto-resolve** (a capped `_cmdBadgeEdge` on the margin), **Classic hex** (OVR-derived quality via the `86-battle-conditioning` ┬▒12% anchor, base unedited), the **real-time tactical** field (the full badge/X-Factor seams), **campaign progression** (reputationтЖТOVR dev-traits), the Custom Battle Builder, and the D93 journey mode тАФ all three battle modes read the SAME rating-derived inputs so they stay substitutable (the D62 bridge property). The rating never forces an outcome in any layer.
- **Build increments (each byte-identical-when-inactive, fully vetted + pushed):** R-0 data spine (`data/ratings.json` + `src/tactical/T14-ratings.js` pure fns + `tools/probe-ratings.mjs`, no combat seam) ┬╖ R-1 officer derivationтЖТpipe ┬╖ R-2 OVR read-out UI (AтАУF, WCAG/CVD triple-encode) ┬╖ R-3 badge engine + global per-lever stacking cap + all-layers wiring ┬╖ R-4 X-Factors (deterministic seed-replay no-fudge gate) ┬╖ R-5 D93 scale-out (lazy per-person materialization) ┬╖ R-6 negative-badge sweep + dev-traits. Calibration oracle: the derivation table is regression-locked against the 9 shipped scenarios' authored `quality`/`xp` before any mass generation. (Reversible; design law in `RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN.md`.)
- **D94-elicitation (Aaron, 10 rounds ├Ч 3 AskUserQuestion, 2026-06-21) тАФ `RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN.md` ┬з15 has the full 30 answers.** The system grew substantially (Aaron chose comprehensively, mostly all-of-the-above): **~15 attributes** (the 10 + initiative/logistics/engineering/cavalry/artillery), shared-set/weighted-by-level, **own-visible/enemy-fuzzy**; badge kinds span ALL types at every rung (Star drill/terrain/arm/veteran ┬╖ Superstar auras/tactics/reputation/logistics ┬╖ X-Factor historical/surge/heroic/doomed); negatives ALL kinds (command/vice/unit/political); general strategic skills (maneuver/logistics/political/coordination); brigade identity (legend/ethnic/veteran/hard-luck). **NEW subsystems:** a between-battle **camp loop** тАФ drilling-as-practice (focus-or-delegate, concordant battlefield bonuses) + **simmable scouting** (tiered by cavalry/recon) + **progression** (combat-XP + drilling + hidden potential ceiling + attrition decline). The **Army GM franchise layer** тАФ a **war-wide free-agency pool** (alt-history dream-teams, balanced by a **symmetric AI GM** + difficulty scaling + clout cost + historical anchors), **all promotion paths** (merit/capital/seniority/field-brevet), killed-officer permadeath, and a **FULL multi-currency economy** (political capital + seniority/manpower + supply) earned from all sources, pressured by factional demands + event shocks. **Matchups:** dual **Attack/Defend OVR** + a full pre-battle matchup screen; emergent counters surfaced as advice. **UI:** period "Army Register" broadsheet roster; in-battle badges via HUD chips + X-Factor banner/glow + floating proc text + marker glyph; initials/rank portraits now. **Data:** full prosopography target, strict 2+ source provenance. **Ship order:** OVR+badges-in-battle first.
- **D94-softcap (the one reconciliation, decide-&-log):** Aaron chose "**soften the cap for power-fantasy**" over "keep the hard wall." Reconciled to honor BOTH it and the D74/D92 non-negotiable: the **OUTPUT wall stays absolute** (no rating ever read when a casualty/winner is computed тАФ architectural invariant, build-gate-asserted), while the **INPUT caps soften and scale with the existing B-5 realism slider** тАФ **Arcade = generous/dramatic dream-team power-fantasy, Balanced = moderate, Historian = the tight historical wall** (the citation-grade teaching mode). DROP the planned "not >60% one side" balance gate. Unrated generals keep authored `gen.skill`.
- **Tactical leg (`src/tactical/T3-officers.js`):** new `fldOfficerPersona(o)` + `fldMakeOfficer` derives `quality` (`fldPersonaQuality`, calibrated to reproduce the authored field quality within тЙд0.005 тАФ the R-0 oracle, so a rated aura shifts only slightly), `radius` (authored echelon range + a small charisma nudge, clamped 160тАУ290), and `fate` (the persona's durability multiplier, which matches the authored scenario fate for the Bull Run cast). **EXPLICIT `pid` opt-in, NO `id` fallback** тАФ the bug-hunt-class fix for a real **cross-scenario id collision**: leader ids are reused across battles (`ld_jackson` is the 1861 brigadier at Bull Run but a corps commander at Antietam/Chancellorsville), so an `id`-match would leak the wrong persona; a leader derives ONLY when it names a persona via `pid`. The 7 Bull Run leaders are opted in (`data/bullrun.json`); every other scenario's leaders have no `pid` тЖТ byte-identical until their personas are authored.
- **`data/ratings.json` тАФ NEW `generalPersonas` map** (9 strategic army-commander personas keyed by the `data/generals.json` id): **CS** Lee, Jackson, A.S. Johnston, Bragg, Longstreet ┬╖ **US** McClellan, Grant, Burnside, Meade тАФ the principal commanders of the 9 D92-hardened battles (Bull Run is covered by the field cast). A SEPARATE record from the Bull Run FIELD cast (war-long army commander vs the 1861 brigade officer); R-5 unifies them into one prosopography person. The documented character + the named negatives (McClellan `the_slows`, Burnside `rigid_plan`, Bragg `piecemeal`) are Verified with real sources (Sears 1988, Marvel 1991, Robertson 1997, Hess 2016, Wert 1993, Chernow 2017, McPherson 1988, тАж); the attribute VECTOR is Inferred designer calibration anchored to each Verified `gen.skill`; `aggression` tracks the documented temperament and is EXCLUDED from the headline OVR (anti-Lost-Cause).

## D97 тАФ RATING SYSTEM **R-3**: the badge engine (the first ratingтЖТcombat seam) + the no-fudge build-gate тАФ [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The first place a rating actually TOUCHES combat (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN ┬з4/┬з6/┬з9 R-3). A guarded one-token factor seeds the levers the engine already reads; the no-fudge OUTPUT wall is now enforced **structurally** by the build. **Byte-identical when off** (proven: sandbox + all 9 battles produce identical deterministic results on the R-3 build vs the committed R-2 build).
- **`fldBadgeFactor(u, lever)` (`src/tactical/T14-ratings.js`):** the guarded MULTIPLICATIVE one-token factor тАФ IDENTITY 1.0 when `__FIELD.badges` is off OR the unit carries no matching badge (mirrors the `(u.cmdBonus||0)` no-op). It sums the unit's badges' signed `mag`s for a lever, gates each by its trigger (`_fldBadgeTrig`: always/march/in_woods/arm_cav/arm_art; others default on, an R-4 refinement), then CLAMPS the summed delta to the realism-scaled per-unit per-lever cap (`fldRatingRealismCap(tier,"badgeLever")` тАФ arcade .16 / balanced .10 / historian .06, D94-softcap). Negatives are DAMPERS (factor<1, тЙе1тИТcap), never enemy buffs. Pure read; returns a factor, never writes state. Plus `fldUnitCohesion(u)` ((cohesionтИТ50)/50, clamped [тИТ1,1]; **0 when cohesion unauthored** тЖТ byte-identical тАФ the rally term defaults neutral, NOT xp-derived, since an xp-derived default would shift the rally of every xpтЙа2 unit).
- **Four guarded seams (`src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js`):** fire (`fldResolveFire` `power *= fldBadgeFactor(u,"fire")`), rally (`fldMoraleStep` `rally = (1 + xp*.12*vet + .06*cohesion*vet) * fldBadgeFactor(u,"rally")`), melee (`fldResolveMelee` atk/def), speed (`fldMoveFactor` `(u._spdMul||1) * fldBadgeFactor(u,"speed")` тАФ `_spdMul` reserved for the R-4 X-Factor surge). All identity when off. The `__FIELD.badges` gate (default ON, `_badgesOff` hook) + `__FIELD.realismTier` (set in `fldPresetsApply`, default balanced) added.
- **Badge data (`data/ratings.json`):** each of the 25 badgeDefs now carries `fldLever` (fire/rally/speed/melee, or `none` for officer-aura / auto-resolve-edge / canister / sight effects deferred to R-4/┬з7.5) + a signed `mag`. Ships the Star/Superstar positives + the Verified named negatives with real tactical bite: McClellan **The Slows** (speed тИТ0.08), Bragg **Piecemeal** (rally тИТ0.05), Burnside **Rigid Plan** (fire тИТ0.05), **Green Levies** (rally тИТ0.08), **Powder-Shy** (rally тИТ0.05); positives marksman/woods_fighter (fire), disciplined/blooded/beloved/stonewall (rally), hardy_marcher/horseman (speed). Badges are NOT yet assigned to shipped scenario rosters (that is the R-6 sweep) тЖТ every battle stays byte-identical.
- **The NO-FUDGE OUTPUT WALL, build-gate-asserted (`tools/build.mjs` gate 4d):** the rating module (`tactical/T14-ratings.js`) is scanned at build for any write to `cas`/`aCas`/`bCas`/`.victory`/`.men`/`sev.*` тАФ dot AND bracket notation (the bracket variants close the bug-hunt's computed-member bypass) тАФ and the build FAILS (exit 5) if found. Verified firing on planted `u.men=0`, `u["men"]=0`, and `F.sev["attrition"]=2` writes; clean build prints `GATE OK ┬╖ тАж ┬╖ no-fudge тЬУ`. The combat modules legitimately write these; the wall scopes to the rating/badge module, which may only seed inputs + return factors.
- **Vetting тАФ NOTE the environmental deviation:** GATE OK (incl. the new no-fudge gate). The standard `load`-based probe suite was **environmentally BLOCKED** this session: headless Chrome's `load` event never fires for the game page (the THREE-CDN `<script>` stalls in headless intermittently; it broke the committed-green R-2 build identically; a trivial page fires `load` in 73ms; `domcontentloaded` loads everything incl. THREE in ~1.5s). Root contributors: (a) the single-threaded `python -m http.server` chokes on the page's ~170 local asset requests (fixed by a **ThreadingHTTPServer**); (b) the THREE-CDN `load` stall (the documented gotcha). So R-3 was vetted via a **`domcontentloaded` byte-identity harness** (`.tmp/r3-verify.mjs`): it ran sandbox + all 9 battles deterministically (same seed) on the R-3 build vs the committed R-2 build and confirmed **IDENTICAL** casualties/winner/steps for all 10, plus the full badge-logic assertions (off=1, single=1.06, stack clamps to 1.10=1+cap, realism arc 1.16 > bal 1.10 > his 1.06, negatives 0.92, cohesion math), 0 pageerrors. This cross-build diff is a *stronger* byte-identity check than the standard probes. **Adversarial bug-hunt** (4 Opus lenses ├Ч refute-verify + critic): 2 confirmed (the gate-4d bracket bypass тАФ FIXED by adding bracket regexes; a phantom `'sharpshooters'` key in the probe/T0 comment тАФ FIXED) + 0 critic. Committed + pushed.
- **LESSON (probe harness, recurring тАФ surface for the gotchas):** serve probes with a **ThreadingHTTPServer** (single-threaded chokes on the asset storm), and when headless `load` stalls on the THREE CDN, the resilient path is `waitUntil:'domcontentloaded'` (the documented gotcha) тАФ the logic/sim probes don't need THREE. RECOMMENDED follow-up (next session, when the env is healthy OR as a harness fix): re-run the standard `load` suite to confirm green, and/or adopt a domcontentloaded+settle wait in the probe runner / vendor THREE locally so the suite is resilient. (Reversible; design law RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN ┬з4/┬з6/┬з9.)

## D98 тАФ RATING SYSTEM **R-4**: the X-FACTORS (the dramatic "in the zone" Madden surge, inside the no-fudge wall) тАФ [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The dramatic increment (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN ┬з4/┬з6/┬з9 R-4, D94 fork-1 "DRAMATIC surge"). An X-Factor badge enters "in the zone" when its situational trigger fires and SURGES on ONE channel, hard-capped тАФ a visible, announced swing that provably can never breach the no-fudge wall. **Byte-identical when off / unassigned** (proven: a `domcontentloaded` byte-identity harness ran sandbox + all 9 battles deterministically on the R-4 build vs the committed R-3 build (HEAD dc9ba61) тЖТ **IDENTICAL** winner/US-cas/CS-cas/steps for all 10, 0 pageerrors).
- **`fldXFactorStep(dt)` (`src/tactical/T14-ratings.js`):** gated on `__FIELD.badges`; for each unit carrying an `rung:"xfactor"` badge (`_fldUnitXFactors`), tests its activation (`_fldXFactorInZone`: march_vigor=moving ┬╖ his_offensive=moving/charging ┬╖ ammo_low_defend=ammo<12 & not charging ┬╖ last_stand_defend=holding & (low morale or a friendly routing within 220yd) ┬╖ usct_assault/mass_assault=charging ┬╖ flanking=cav & charging) and, when in the zone, sets the surge on EXACTLY ONE channel (its declared lever): a **NON-speed** X-Factor (rally/melee/none) sets `u._xfActive = fldRatingRealismCap(tier,"xfactor")` (arcade 1.45 / balanced 1.20 / historian 1.08); a **SPEED** X-Factor (Foot Cavalry / The Slows) sets `u._spdMul` only (capped [0.85,1.15]) and does NOT surge the command aura. One-shot тЪб `fldAnnounce` + `fldScenarioBanner` on the rising edge (`_xfOn`); a marker glow (`_xfGlow`); deterministic decay (`_fldXfDecay`) toward identity out of zone. **NO RNG** тЖТ seed-replayable. A unit carrying no X-Factor is left wholly untouched (`_xf*`/`_spdMul` stay undefined) тЖТ byte-identical.
- **`fldXFactorApplyCmd(u)`:** scales the unit's ALREADY-SUMMED command aura `u.cmdBonus = min(FLDO.CMD_BONUS_CAP, (cmdBonus||0)*_xfActive)` тАФ pushes the aura toward the **hard 0.9 wall, NEVER beyond**. A strict no-op unless an X-Factor is active (`_xfActive` undefined/тЙд1) тЖТ byte-identical. Called in `fldSimStep` AFTER `fldOfficersStep` (so the aura is summed first), gated on `__FIELD.badges` (NOT officers) so the cmdBonus surge and the `_spdMul` surge share ONE gate.
- **Seams (`src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js`):** `fldSimStep` calls `fldXFactorStep(dt)` just before `fldOfficersStep` + the apply loop just after; `fldMoveFactor` clamps the **COMBINED** speed factor (the `_spdMul` surge ├Ч the R-3 static speed-badge factor) to ONE documented band **[0.75,1.30]** so no stack can breach it (exactly 1 when no rating speed input тЖТ byte-identical); `fld2dDraw` draws a guarded `_xfGlow` pulse тАФ a CVD-safe amber burst RING (the shape carries the meaning) + a **vector-drawn** lightning bolt (no emoji-font/tofu dependency), `reduceMotion`-honored, drawn for no shipped unit тЖТ byte-identical.
- **Data (`data/ratings.json`):** ADDED `first_with_the_most` (Forrest, cav, flanking trigger, fldLever none тЖТ surges via the capped cmdBonus only; 2 sources тЖТ Verified). The 7 X-Factors: foot_cavalry, rock_of_chickamauga, bayonet, earned_in_blood, grand_charge, first_with_the_most, the_slows. NOT assigned to any shipped scenario (the R-6 sweep) тЖТ byte-identical.
- **NO-FUDGE REPLAY GATE (`tools/probe-ratings.mjs`, +2 steps тЖТ 17/17):** a deterministic seed-replay tags one CS sandbox brigade with foot_cavalry and runs it vs the untagged baseline (same seed): the surge **BITES** (it flipped a US win into a CS win) yet stays **bounded** (17.2% total-casualty delta тАФ an input nudge, not a scripted result) and the **wall holds** (`maxCmd 0.47 < 0.9`). Plus synthetic asserts: speed X-Factor surges only `_spdMul` (no cmdBonus), non-speed surges cmdBonus capped at the wall, the combined-speed clamp binds at 1.30, negatives drag, realism-monotone amp, decayтЖТ1.

## D100 тАФ RATING SYSTEM **Q8**: the between-battle CAMP LOOP (drilling + progression) тАФ [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The agency that GROWS your rating over a campaign (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN ┬з15 / ┬з14.6). A new "Camp" desk tab where, between battles, the President DRILLS the army; the drilled training raises the army he fields via a guarded, bounded conditioning seam тАФ PURE INPUT-SEEDING, never the scoreboard, and **byte-identical until the player engages the camp**.
- **`src/36-camp.js` (new module):** `campInit` (idempotent; seeds `C.president.camp` = drill{musketry/maneuver/entrenching/endurance}, fatigue, delegate, **engaged**); `campDrill(C,focus)` (raises a focus toward CEIL 90, +fatigue, sets engaged); `campSetDelegate`; `campTrainingBonus(C)` (THE BRIDGE SEAM тАФ per-facet deltas, ALL ZERO when no focus is drilled); `campOnResolve` (rest sheds fatigue, a delegated army auto-drills, a clean win SEASONS / a battle this side bled the lion's share ERODES тАФ gated on `engaged`); `campRenderTab`/`campWireTab`; `_campGrade`/`_campBar`. **Drilling/progression only** тАФ SCOUTING deferred to Q8b (it needs the strategic-next-battle тЖФ tactical-OOB mapping).

EXACTLY 0 when undrilled тЖТ byte-identical. Computed once, reused.
- **Wiring:** `campInit` in `_t1InitAll` (after cmdInit); `campOnResolve` in `_t1Resolve` (after cmdOnResolve); a "Camp" tab in `30-president-shell.js` (dispatch + tab arrays + button + wiring); `"36-camp.js"` in the manifest. `C.president.camp` rides `serializeSave` wholesale + lazy-migrates via idempotent campInit тАФ **no `_SAVE_VER` bump** (additive, D7).
- **THE KEYSTONE (byte-identity):** an `engaged` flag (false until the first drill/delegate) makes the WHOLE loop INERT until the player opens the camp тАФ `campOnResolve` early-returns and `campTrainingBonus` is all-zero at zero drill тАФ so a campaign that never camps conditions byte-for-byte as the pre-Q8 build (proven: probe-camp's keystone step + probe-bridge 6/6 + probe-conditioning 6/6 UNCHANGED). NO RNG (deterministic).

## D101 тАФ RATING SYSTEM **R-5**: the PROSOPOGRAPHY SCALE-OUT (bulk per-person derivation + LAZY materialization + the play-as-anyone hook) тАФ [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The D93 "Soldier's Story" substrate the whole rating spine was built for: a brigade can now be *inspected down to its men*, and any person can be *materialized + promoted* тАФ all PURE DATA + DISPLAY, **byte-identical** (no shipped scenario assigns bulk persons; the deterministic sim тАФ sandbox + all 9 battles тАФ is proven identical to committed HEAD `84c5e95`). Design law: RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN ┬з5/┬з8/┬з9 R-5/┬з15 (R9).
- **The LAZY-MATERIALIZATION keystone (┬з8):** a brigade TOKEN carries ONE aggregate `fldMenMeanOVR(u,year)` тАФ its men's mean OVR, derived O(1) from xp + arm-branch + year + a deterministic per-brigade-id jitter, clamped [20,88] (a brigade AVERAGE never reaches the Legendary individual ceiling). Per-person rows are NEVER instantiated en masse: `fldMaterializePerson(spec,year)` builds exactly ONE row on demand (inspect / play-as), and `fldBrigadeMuster(u,n,year)` builds a HARD-CAPPED (тЙд6) representative sample (captain/sergeant/private from a data-driven `musterTemplate`), **never `u.men` rows** тАФ proven: a 100,000-man brigade still materializes 3. The mean is always recomputable, never the source of truth.
- **New pure functions (`src/tactical/T14-ratings.js`):** `fldMenMeanOVR` ┬╖ `fldMaterializePerson` (reuses the R-0 `fldDerivePerson` тЖТ headline + dual OVR + grade; a generated row gets a deterministic synthesized period name [`_fldSynthName` + `_FLD_FIRST`/`_FLD_LAST`, NO RNG] + Inferred provenance + a `latentCommand` seed) ┬╖ `fldPromotePerson(person,toRank)` (the **latent-command promotion** = play-as-anyone: lifts command/tactical/discipline/charisma by the rank-base delta; returns a NEW person, pure) ┬╖ `fldPersonTeam` (the EA-style {side,army,corps} journey hook) ┬╖ `fldProvenanceStyle` (the **Inferred-vs-Verified visual distinction** ┬з10 тАФ Verified solid / Inferred HATCHED `repeating-linear-gradient` / Disputed dashed; meaning rides pattern + glyph [тЬУ/~/?] + word, NOT colour тЖТ CVD-safe) ┬╖ `fldMusterHudLine` (the compact in-battle inspect line) ┬╖ `fldMusterRollHtml` (the full "Muster Roll" panel, ready for the journey-mode character sheet). **Data:** `musterTemplate` + `_r5Note` added to `data/ratings.json`.
- **The ONLY live wiring:** one guarded line in `fldRenderHud` (`src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js`) appends `fldMusterHudLine(u)` after the R-2 brigade-OVR line тАФ so selecting a brigade now shows its **MEN OVR** (the men's prosopography mean) beside the R-2 combat OVR, with a provenance-hatched accent. Pure display; "" when ratings data absent тЖТ byte-identical. NO new combat path; NO RNG.

ALL 4 fixed (defensive-copy hardening so a FUTURE bulk-person/career path can't corrupt canonical `GAME_DATA`): **(1)** `fldMaterializePerson` returned the AUTHORED persona BY REFERENCE (via `fldDerivePerson`'s authored branch) тЖТ now shallow-copies persona at the materialization boundary; **(2)** `fldPromotePerson` with an unmapped/typo'd `toRank` silently mapped to the 64 anchor (a +16 unearned lift + false officerTier) тЖТ now requires a real `rankBase` key, else a clean no-op clone; **(3)** the `sources` ARRAY was a second shared reference (and `fldPromotePerson` propagated it) тЖТ now `.slice()`'d on both paths; **(4)** `fldPromotePerson`'s persona-less guard returned the input ref, breaking its "returns a NEW person" contract тЖТ added `_fldClonePerson` (copies persona + sources) for every no-op path. ## D102 тАФ RATING SYSTEM **Q9**: the GM PROMOTION economy (the first depth-chart MOVE тАФ promote ┬╖ multi-currency ┬╖ merit gate) тАФ [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The first real GM *move* beyond appoint/relieve, built on the existing `cmdAppoint`/political-capital spine + the R-5 person spine (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN ┬з12.2/┬з14.3/┬з15). The President promotes a general one grade up a clean strategic ladder, spending a **multi-currency** budget, **merit-gated** by reputation. PURE INPUT-SEEDING + display тАФ **byte-identical until the player promotes** (proven: sandbox + all 9 battles byte-for-byte identical to committed HEAD `fc1d251`). Design law: ┬з12.
- **The ladder + the move (`src/35-command.js`, the "Q9 (D102)" block):** `_cmdBaseGrade` parses each general's VERBOSE `generals.json` rank deterministically down to one of **Brig. Gen. тЖТ Maj. Gen. тЖТ Lt. Gen. тЖТ General** (the multi-word grades are checked before the bare "General"; an unrecognized rank defaults to the LOWEST grade тАФ never invents a man up). `cmdPromote(C,id)` raises him one grade, spending BOTH currencies (gated on both): **political capital** (`C.clock.capital`, the primary тАФ `capitalCost` by target grade, ├Ч`aboveMeritMul` if above merit) + a NEW **seniority** pool (`cmd.seniority` тАФ `seniorityCostBase` + a `seniorityLeapfrog` surcharge when he leapfrogs a passed-over senior). Bounded, clamped, logged.
- **The merit gate (the honest history):** each target grade carries a reputation **meritBar**. EARNED (rep тЙе bar) тЖТ a confidence bump (+`earnedRepBonus`); ABOVE merit (rep < bar) тЖТ the capital surcharge **+ a jealousy reputation hit** (тИТ`aboveMeritRepHit`). Because OVR = 0.55┬╖skill + 0.45┬╖reputation, **over-promoting a favorite past his record can LOWER his OVR** тАФ rank without merit doesn't make a good commander. (Teaches the real command politics Lincoln navigated; anti-Lost-Cause: merit, not grade, is competence.)
- **How it reaches the fight (no new combat path):** a promotion lifts the general's effective skill by a small BOUNDED amount тАФ `_cmdPromoteSkillLift` = (rankBase delta ├Ч `skillLiftWeight` 0.92), clamped to `skillLiftCap` 6 тАФ added inside the EDITED `_cmdEffectiveSkill(gen, C)`, which flows ONLY through the existing `_cmdGenRating тЖТ commandLeadership тЖТ` the bridge LEADERSHIP facet (an INPUT the sim already reads; `commandMarginEdge` reads aggression/caution, untouched). NEVER the scoreboard (D74/D94 no-fudge wall тАФ `cmdPromote` mutates only `clk.capital`/`cmd.seniority`/`cmd.promotions`/`cmd.reputation`). **0 lift when un-promoted тЖТ every pre-Q9 reading byte-identical.**
- **The surface + currency (`_cmdPromotionsHTML`/`_cmdPromoRow`, new Command-desk section "The officer corps тАФ promotions"):** each available general's current grade (тЖС if promoted) + OVR + grade + a Promote control with the dual-currency cost + a merit annotation, above a capital + seniority read-out. Period-broadsheet styling; triple-encoded; CVD-safe (the grade dot is aria-hidden, meaning rides number+letter+word). `cmd.seniority` accrues over the campaign in `cmdOnResolve` (`seniorityPerTurn` + a `seniorityWinBonus`, capped) тАФ a currency nothing combat reads, so the accrual is invisible/byte-identical. `data/ratings.json` gains the `promotion` config block. Rides the save (no `_SAVE_VER` bump; idempotent `cmdInit` lazy-migration, D7).
- **DEFERRED-&-LOGGED (the rest of ┬з12, mirrors Q7тЖТR-5 / Q8тЖТQ8b):** the **symmetric AI-GM** (the opponent drafts/promotes тАФ needs enemy-commanderтЖТcombat wiring; would break byte-identity / risk fudge), cross-theater **Transfer** (needs authored theaters тАФ `generals.json` has none), **Commission** of generated officers + the full corps/division **depth-chart tree** (needs the strategicтЖФtactical OOB mapping тАФ the Q8b blocker family). This slice ships the player-side promotion economy now; the loop proceeds once those substrates exist.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (7 Opus agents: 4 diverse-lens finders ├Ч default-refute verify + a completeness critic; 2 raw тЖТ **2 confirmed + 1 actionable critic gap, ALL LOW, ALL latent**; 0 HIGH/MED; critic overall: *"SOUND and may be committed тАФ the no-fudge wall, byte-identity, bounding, determinism, and no-exploit invariants all hold; no HIGH/MED missed."*). ALL 3 fixed: **(1)** `cmdPromote` gated on `Math.round(capital)` but spent from raw `capital` тЖТ a fractional balance could pass the rounded gate and be floor-absorbed on the spend тЖТ now debits the same rounded `cap` (byte-identical under every current integer-only capital path). **(2)** `_cmdBaseGrade`'s unrecognized-rank fallback was "Maj. Gen." (rankBase 68) тЖТ would over-grade a future non-named officer (e.g. a Colonel, 64) two grades onto the General ladder тЖТ now defaults to the LOWEST grade "Brig. Gen." (unreachable on the shipped surface; hardens the deferred depth-chart path). **(3, critic)** `cmdInit` re-seeded `seniority` only when invalid тЖТ a valid-but-out-of-band tampered/stale save value wasn't re-clamped until the next resolve тЖТ now clamps to the cap on LOAD. The critic's other gap (the two `diag-classic` 404s) is the **pre-existing documented tolerated asset-layer 404 noise**, not Q9 (Q9 touches no asset paths). Re-vetted after the fixes.
- **Vetting:** GATE OK (no-fudge тЬУ); `probe-command` **25/25** (16 prior + **9 new Q9 steps**: seniority seeded + empty promotions [byte-identical default]; the save-tamper LOAD re-clamp; the grade-ladder parse [Lee=General / Grant=Lt. Gen. / Meade & Stuart=Maj. Gen.]; Lee [top grade] not promotable; promotion GATED when either currency is short + SPENDS both + stores the grade; EARNED raises rep / ABOVE-MERIT costs more capital + cuts rep; a promotion lifts effective skill [bounded тЙд6] тЖТ reaches commandLeadership, un-promoted byte-identical; every general both sides reads the SAME skill with/without C; the render surfaces the section + currencies + a Promote control), 0 pe; **byte-identity harness IDENTICAL for all 10** vs committed HEAD `fc1d251` + the Q9 live sanity (a promotion stores "Lt. Gen.", lifts commandLeadership 79тЖТ80 [bounded], renders the section, un-promoted reads identical, 0 pe); `probe-ratings` 19/19 + `probe-desk` 13/13 + `probe-camp` 8/8 + `t1probe` 14/14 (0 pe each); `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; `bootprobe` ok; `wcag-auditor` 0 AA failures (fixed the new warning text `#c2502e`тЖТ`#d66040`, 4.51:1 measured against the real dark `.sheet` ground). **ENV:** the `load` suite stalled intermittently on the THREE-CDN headless load this session (the documented gotcha тАФ cleared by a fresh threaded server + retry); the `domcontentloaded` byte-identity harness remains the authoritative no-regression proof. ## D103 тАФ RATING SYSTEM **R-6 (citation-provenance portion)**: the CATALOG-WIDE citation hardening + a permanent build-gate тАФ [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The R-6 increment's **negative-badge ASSIGNMENT to rosters + live dev-traits remain**; this milestone shipped the **citation-grade prerequisite** that gates them: every `Verified`-stamped claim in the data catalog now carries **тЙе2 independent real sources**, the non-negotiable made un-erodable by the build. **A live violation was found and closed:** an audit revealed the debt was NOT confined to badges (the logged D98тАУD101 framing) тАФ **47 records across SIX data files** were stamped `Verified` with <2 sources (badges 13 ┬╖ personas 2 ┬╖ weapons 9 ┬╖ artillery 9 ┬╖ engineering 8 ┬╖ terrain 1 ┬╖ cabinet 5). Outcome: **0 fabrication** (critic-confirmed), all citations real/on-claim/independent. Two judgment calls logged: **`beloved` held *Inferred*** (its one solid cite is Symonds 1997 on Cleburne; the obvious Lee source тАФ Freeman 1934 тАФ is Lost-Cause-tinged and held out until a non-hagiographic Lee cite is added), and **`grand_charge` upgraded *Verified*** (Stewart 1959 ┬╖ Hess 2001 ┬╖ Sears 2003, satisfying its in-data "Inferred until the sweep" note). The long descriptive forms ("Verified specs (тАж)", "Verified (high) тАФ тАж", ~72 of them) cite inline in prose and trim-lowercase to тЙа "verified", so they stay out of the structured gate **by design**. Mirrors the 4d no-fudge wall: a non-negotiable made structural.

## D105 тАФ RATING SYSTEM **LIVE DEV-TRAITS (the Madden development arc)**: a general's OVR now develops over the campaign, shaped by a hidden potential ceiling тАФ [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The last open item on the R-6 rating track (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN ┬з9-R-6: "reputation level-up тЖТ OVR still TODO") + the D94-fork-#5 lock ("ReputationтЖТOVR dev-traits = LIVE in-campaign now"). `cmdOnResolve` already evolved a general's reputation by battle outcome (decisive win +6 / win +3 / draw тИТ1 / loss тИТ4 / decisive loss тИТ8), and `_cmdGenRating` (0.55┬╖skill + 0.45┬╖reputation) тЖТ `commandLeadership` already read it тАФ so winning a campaign already nudged his OVR. D105 adds the **Madden DEV-TRAIT** that SHAPES that arc: a hidden potential **ceiling** (how high he can climb), a **floor** (how far he can fall), a development **rate** (rise vs fall), and an **attritionDrag** (the ┬з15-R3 decline-with-heavy-attrition). **ACCURATE INPUTS, never an output gate (D74/D92)** тАФ a dev-trait only shapes the general's REPUTATION (an INPUT the existing pipe consumes), it NEVER writes a casualty/winner. Design law: RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN ┬з9-R-6 / ┬з14.6 / ┬з15-R3.
- **The keystone (byte-identical-when-off, the R-6/D104 pattern):** the engine seam in `cmdOnResolve` is **byte-identical for an UNASSIGNED general (or absent devTraits data)** тАФ it takes the LITERAL pre-D105 path `clamp(cur+delta, 5, 98)`, rate 1, no drag (proven across ALL five outcome quadrants + both clamp rails). The deliberate, citation-grade, historically-directed change is the AUTHORED `data/ratings.json` `devTraits.assign` map (20 generals тЖТ one of 12 archetypes). The ceiling/floor are RELATIVE to the general's SEEDED start reputation (`devTrack.start`, fixed), every archetype keeps `ceilingAboveтЙе5 & floorBelowтЙе5`, so the pre-D105 "a winning general gains reputation / a losing one loses it" invariant holds for all.
- **The arc (in `cmdOnResolve`):** an assigned general's base delta is scaled by his `riseRate`/`fallRate`, plus a bounded extra `attritionDrag` when his side bled the lion's share (casualty SHARE > pivot тАФ the D100 unit-correct measure), then clamped to HIS `[floor,ceiling]` band. New pure fns (`src/35-command.js`): `_cmdDevCfg`/`_cmdDevStart`/`_cmdDevTrait` (resolves the absolute band) / `_cmdAttritionDrag` (bounded тЙд attritionDragMax) / `_cmdDevTrackUpdate` (pure observation) / `_cmdDevTrend` / `_cmdCareerArcHTML`. `cmdInit` seeds + sanitizes `cmd.devTrack[id]={start,peak,low,battles}` (rides the save, no `_SAVE_VER` bump). NO RNG.
- **The 12 archetypes + anti-Lost-Cause balance:** rising_star (Grant/Sherman/Sheridan) ┬╖ steady_rock (Thomas) ┬╖ established_legend (Lee/Jackson) ┬╖ natural_genius (Forrest) ┬╖ steady_professional (Meade/ScottтЖТadministrator/Longstreet/A.S.Johnston) ┬╖ cautious_fabian (J.E.Johnston) ┬╖ mercurial_cavalier (Stuart/Beauregard) ┬╖ administrator (Scott/Halleck) ┬╖ plateau (McClellan) ┬╖ overpromoted (Burnside/Hooker) ┬╖ volatile_aggressor (Hood) ┬╖ quarrelsome (Bragg). **The thesis is anti-Lost-Cause:** the Union's elite are RISERS (4 high-ceiling developers rated as high as Lee/Jackson тАФ the honest claim that the Union found and elevated its best command) while command failures are named plainly on BOTH sides (US McClellan plateau / Burnside-Hooker overpromoted; CS Bragg quarrelsome / Hood volatile-disaster). All 20 assignments are stamped **Inferred** (a calibrated reading of a documented arc тАФ gate-4e-exempt) with 1-2 real sources each; nothing laundered (Forrest's Klan + Longstreet's Lost-Cause slander named in the notes).
- **The read-out (`_cmdCareerArcHTML`, a new Command-desk "Career Arc" section):** the sitting general's dev-trait tier (label + glyph + polarity sign + desc), his OVR arc (startтЖТnowтЖТpeak on a floor..ceiling band with start/peak ticks), a trend verdict (Rising/Holding/Fading/Untested) + the net delta, and a soft potential-room note. Triple-encoded (word + sign + number; glyph + colour decorative) тЖТ CVD-safe; `wcag-auditor` AA (one nested-opacity spot 3.93тЖТ4.57:1 fixed).
- **The no-fudge wall extended (bug-hunt):** build-gate 4d (the no-fudge OUTPUT WALL) now also scans `src/35-command.js` (confirmed it writes ONLY command state тАФ reputation/seniority/capital/devTrack, none in the forbidden set) тАФ closing the coverage gap so the strategic rating code's no-fudge invariant is STRUCTURAL too (mirrors how D103's gate 4e made citations un-erodable).
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (the ultracode pattern тАФ 5 diverse-lens Opus finders [no-fudge ┬╖ byte-identity ┬╖ bounding/determinism ┬╖ citation/balance ┬╖ UI/probe] ├Ч default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic; 29 agents; **8 confirmed + 3 critic-missed; 1 HIGH, 3 MED, 7 LOW; critic: "SAFE TO COMMIT тАФ both hard invariants [no output gate, byte-identical-when-off] CONFIRMED HOLD"** via independent grep corroboration that `devTrack`/`reputation` are read by no combat code). ## D151 тАФ PHASE I ┬╖ SOLDIER'S STORY JOURNEY PERSISTENCE тАФ [CODEX implementation + direct main-loop audit] (2026-06-28)

The third Phase-I continuation milestone makes a selected Soldier's Story journey persist as an honest career record instead of only a start flag. It changes only `src/37-loot-survival.js`, `src/82-after-action.js`, `tools/probe-loot-survival.mjs`, docs, and the generated `civil_war_generals.html`; no canonical battle data, tactical combat rules, `build/base.html`, save schema version, or item balance data changed.

- **Career log and battle association:** `ssStartJourney` now creates a bounded start entry for the selected person, and each resolved battle appends a sanitized career entry with battle id/name, outcome, turn, status, rank-before/rank-after, casualties, and a plain-language note. The active journey also keeps `startBattleId`, `currentBattleId`, `lastBattleId`, `lastBattleName`, `lastOutcome`, `battles`, and `promotionCount`, plus a bounded `L.people[personId]` summary for save/load and UI readback.
- **Status, survival, and promotion hooks:** journey outcomes can mark the selected person `alive`, `wounded`, or `captured` under deterministic low-risk rules keyed to battle outcome/casualty pressure. Wounded/captured states create bounded survival-meter consequences and a tiny active-only bridge penalty; inactive Campaign Kit saves still produce exact zero. When a generated low-rank person earns a decisive result, the journey uses `fldPromotePerson` to update the saved person snapshot/rank without mutating canonical `GAME_DATA.ratings`.
- **UI/report tie-in:** the Campaign Kit active-journey panel now shows status, last battle, battle count, promotions, and the recent career log. `ssJourneyReportHTML` provides a small display-only Soldier's Story panel that `src/82-after-action.js` includes in after-action/final reports when a journey is active.
- **Save/load safety:** `lootInit` now sanitizes restored journey career arrays, bad statuses, bad keys, person snapshots, dual OVR fields, promotion counts, and tampered people-state summaries into bounded plain data. Generated rows remain `Generated`/`Inferred`; D151 does not replace any generated row with an unsourced named person.

The visible Campaign Kit UI mirrors that rule by disabling Begin Journey controls after a journey starts. Follow-up static checks verified no direct `L.equipped.hasOwnProperty` remains and that the new probe locks the restored-save and screenshot paths.

## D148 тАФ PHASE I ┬╖ LOOT/SURVIVAL MVP + SOLDIER'S STORY PLAY-AS-ANYONE SPINE тАФ [CODEX implementation + adversarial main-loop audit] (2026-06-27)

Phase I now has an additive Campaign Kit instead of a parallel economy or combat model. It ships rarity-tiered loot, a bounded inventory, default-off survival pressure, and the first playable Soldier's Story journey path. It reuses the existing R-5 prosopography/rating substrate and the Armory/Cannon rarity vocabulary; it does not change canonical battle data, tactical combat rules, `build/base.html`, or hand-edit generated HTML.

- **Campaign Kit:** new `data/loot-survival.json` + `src/37-loot-survival.js` + a `Campaign Kit` desk tab. `C.loot` rides existing saves as plain JSON: `inventory`, `equipped`, `survival`, `journey`, and `people`. Battle/campaign outcomes call `lootOnResolve` for deterministic rewards; the player can inspect inventory, use consumables, equip kit/weapon/keepsake items, toggle survival, forage, and begin a Soldier's Story journey.
- **Survival gate:** rations, exposure, disease, fatigue, forage, morale. Survival is **off by default**. `lootSurvivalBridgeBonus(C)` returns exact zero unless survival or a Soldier journey is active; active effects are bounded facet deltas only, never scoreboard writes or per-battle combat tuning.
- **Soldier's Story / prosopography:** `ssPersonRegistry` enumerates the current modeled game roster: authored rating personas, strategic generals and commission-pool figures, plus representative company officer/NCO/private rows for every current tactical brigade token across single-phase, multi-phase, and reinforcement OOBs. The Campaign Kit selector exposes the full registry (603 selectable people in the current build), not just the visible sample cards, so the player can start a journey from any current modeled person. Generated rows remain visibly `Inferred`; future work can replace them with citation-grade named bios/portraits/unit detail without changing the play-as-anyone API.
- **Reuse / no mutation:** person rows materialize through `fldMaterializePerson`, `fldPersonTeam`, and `fldPromotePerson`; D148 does not fork rating math. The adversarial audit fixed canonical-data aliasing so registry/journey creation does not annotate or mutate `GAME_DATA.ratings`.
- **Bug-hunt fixes:** stack-full inventory additions now return `stack-full` instead of false success; survival meter init preserves explicit zero values; the Campaign Kit UI now exposes all current registry people for play-as-anyone selection.
- **Vetting:** `node --check` passed for every new/edited JS file. `node tools/build.mjs` printed **GATE OK** and rebuilt `civil_war_generals.html` from source. Focused `node tools/probe-loot-survival.mjs` passed **8/8, 0 pageerrors**, including save-shape sanitation, bounded inventory, unique/stack safety, default-off bridge identity, active survival tick/forage bounds, deterministic battle rewards, canonical-data nonmutation, 603-person play-as-anyone registry coverage, and full-registry UI journey start. Packs validate every scenario first, install only into empty local slots, refuse duplicates, and write nothing if validation or capacity fails.

## D146 тАФ PHASE J ┬╖ SAVE / LOAD / SHARE HARDENING тАФ [CODEX implementation + adversarial main-loop audit] (2026-06-27)

Phase J's save/share pass is now a hardening/probe milestone over the existing save system, not a new persistence architecture. It changes `src/91-save-slots.js`, adds `tools/probe-save-slots.mjs`, wires that probe into `tools/vet-no-regression.mjs`, and rebuilds `civil_war_generals.html` from source. It does **not** touch tactical/combat state, battle data, `build/base.html`, or hand-edit the generated deliverable.

- **Save validation and slot behavior:** saves are cloned and validated before import/load. The validator rejects wrong versions, arrays/primitive payloads where objects are required, `settings` objects that shadow `hasOwnProperty`, primitive/array `campaign` payloads, and stale/corrupt named slots. Named slot save/load/rename/delete remains localStorage-based and bounded to the existing save namespace.
- **Import/export hardening:** pasted JSON and file import now route through the same hardened validator. The visible file-import path no longer delegates to the base `importSave`; D146 adds `_slImportFile` and assigns a hardened `importSave` wrapper with an `_slHardened` marker so the base main-menu "Load from File" path is covered too. This closes the bug-hunt finding where file imports could bypass the hardened text path and reach base `applySave`, which calls `sv.settings.hasOwnProperty(k)`.
- **Menu and undo:** the Save Manager menu injection dedupes itself and reinjects after menu rebuilds instead of relying on a brittle one-shot latch. The one-turn undo path is deliberately narrow: it captures before `campaignAdvance` only for the learner-friendly accessible difficulty path, not Ironman/harder campaign modes.
- **Probe coverage:** new `tools/probe-save-slots.mjs` verifies manager API presence, UI labels, menu dedupe/reinjection, named slot save/load/rename/delete, export/import text round-trip, invalid/stale/corrupt/tampered rejection, `settings.hasOwnProperty` shadow rejection, hardened import marker, one-turn undo capture/load, and no tactical/combat state writes or redeclaration hazards. `tools/vet-no-regression.mjs` includes the save-slot probe in the normal suite.
- **Vetting:** `node --check src/91-save-slots.js`, `node --check tools/probe-save-slots.mjs`, and `node --check tools/vet-no-regression.mjs` passed. `node tools/build.mjs` printed **GATE OK**. Focused `node tools/probe-save-slots.mjs` passed **9/9, 0 pageerrors**. Post-fix `node tools/vet-no-regression.mjs --from="save slots"` passed **51 commands**, including `probe-full-campaign` **4/4, 0 pageerrors** and `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`, `m3dActive:false`; probe JSON readback showed `ok=true` and `pageerrors=0`; `git diff --check` clean. Q5 Chattanooga and Q6 USCT playable battles remain LAST.

## D145 тАФ MODEL ROUTING + UI/UX REDESIGN LAW + NORMAL NO-REGRESSION GATE тАФ [AARON directive + CODEX docs/tooling] (2026-06-27)

Aaron explicitly directed this blocker-clearing pass before new gameplay work: update model-routing instructions, consolidate stale roadmap language, add a real frontend redesign milestone because the broadsheet interface is not the desired global shell, research a better game-like UI/UX direction, and harden the full-campaign probe into the normal no-regression gate.

- **Model-routing law:** the main reasoning/integration loop stays on the highest-quality model, specifically **5.5** for complex architecture, important code, user-facing text, historical judgment, UI/UX design decisions, accessibility judgment, bug hunts, final review, and irreversible/quality-critical work. Token-efficient helpers are allowed only for bounded packets where quality cannot be harmed: `rg`/search summaries, file inventories, probe-log summaries, mechanical doc syncs, exact-schema data cleanup, first-pass source gathering, and repetitive fixture/probe scaffolding. Every helper/subagent/workflow call must explicitly set model **and** effort. Smaller models never own architecture, combat balance, historical claims, UX direction, accessibility judgment, or final integration; they produce packets that 5.5 verifies.
- **UI/UX design law:** D145 supersedes "broadsheet everywhere." The app shell should become a more video-game-like historical command interface: brighter, rounder, more dramatic, icon-led, and centered on public-domain photos/illustrations where they clarify people/place/stakes. Broadsheet remains the in-world language for press/editorials/dispatches/provenance, not the whole interface. The redesign must preserve Civil War gravity, anti-Lost-Cause framing, WCAG 2.2 AA, keyboard support, `reduceMotion`, CVD-safe cues, no unclear-license assets, and the Intel UHD-617 performance floor. Research packet saved at `.tmp/ui-redesign-research.md`.
- **Roadmap/gate cleanup:** `V1-CHECKLIST.md` now has a real H0 UI/UX redesign milestone with target screens, visual-system requirements, probes/screenshots, and acceptance criteria. The Phase J saves item is corrected to hardening/probing over existing `src/91-save-slots.js` named slots/export/import, with undo-last-turn still open. D143's full-campaign probe is now part of the normal no-regression command via `tools/vet-no-regression.mjs` and package scripts `vet:noreg`, `vet:noreg:list`, and `vet:full-campaign`.
- **Docs synced:** `START-HERE.md`, `AUTONOMOUS-RUN.md`, `AGENTS.md`, `CLAUDE.md`, `.clinerules`, `.github/copilot-instructions.md`, `V1-CHECKLIST.md`, `RUN-LOG.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, and `WAKE-UP.md` were refreshed so the next run starts from the same routing, UI, and gate contract. Q5 Chattanooga and Q6 USCT playable battles remain LAST.
- **Probe policy decision:** do **not** remove probes from the universal scheme. The right correction is smarter harness discipline: focused probe + relevant no-regression/full milestone gate, JSON/pageerror enforcement, process-group timeout cleanup, and root-cause fixes for probe hangs. This audit found useful failures: accessibility's static scan saw comment text, `bootprobe` could hang after writing green JSON, `probe-phased-3d` could hang without a bounded failure, and heavy visual probes needed explicit budgets.
- **Vetting:** `node tools/build.mjs` **GATE OK**; focused accessibility **25/25**, phased-3D **64/64**, render-richness **30/30**, weather **30/30**; all 0 pageerrors. `tools/vet-no-regression.mjs` completed the full normal gate in resumed segments on the 8 GB Mac: build through visual-fidelity, render-richness, then weather through `probe-full-campaign` and `diag-classic`. Final segment ended with `probe-full-campaign` **4/4, 0 pageerrors** and `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`, `m3dActive:false`. `git diff --check` clean.

## D143 тАФ PHASE J ┬╖ **FULL-CAMPAIGN PLAYTHROUGH PROBE** тАФ the owner-mode campaign now has an end-to-end guard from first battle to final graded report тАФ [CODEX probe-only] (2026-06-26)

This milestone adds the missing Phase-J no-regression guard without changing gameplay. New `tools/probe-full-campaign.mjs` drives the live single-file game in Chrome and verifies the cross-layer contract that individual probes only checked in slices: campaign chain -> bridge auto-resolve -> `campaignAdvance` -> President's interstitial -> final D112/D119 graded war report.

- **Coverage:** the probe runs a dominant Union auto-resolve campaign through the full 31-battle US chain (`sumter` -> `appomattox`) and a dominant Confederate auto-resolve campaign through the full 28-battle CS chain (`sumter` -> `appomattox`). Each resolved battle must win, increment `stats.battles`, advance `idx`, add the battle id to `completed[]`, clear recovery flags, and surface the President's interstitial before the next fight. The final chain victory must null `G.campaign` through `warWonScreen` and render `#wwReport`, `Final Reckoning`, and `#wwMainMenu`.
- **Recovery branch:** a controlled Bull Run loss keeps `idx` fixed, enters recovery, sets `flipAtk` because the player lost while attacking, then a recovery auto-resolve consumes the flipped attacker (`bd.atk === "CS"`), advances to the next battle, and clears recovery flags.
- **Strategic-ending branch:** a mid-campaign `victoryReady="will"` state must surface the between-battles "The war can be concluded" offer and `pdConcludeWar`; accepting it renders the negotiated-peace framing plus the graded final report and ends the campaign.
- **Architecture:** probe-only. No `src/`, `data/`, build, combat, or save logic changed. The probe deliberately uses the existing `bridgeAutoResolve`, `campaignAdvance`, `openUpgrade`, `aarConcludeWar`, and `warWonScreen` seams; it does not invent a parallel campaign runner.
- **Vet:** `node tools/build.mjs` baseline **GATE OK** before work; `node tools/probe-full-campaign.mjs` **4/4, 0 pageerrors** (`tools/shots/probe-full-campaign.json` confirms US 31/31, CS 28/28, recovery, and strategic ending); `node --check tools/probe-full-campaign.mjs` clean; `git diff --check` clean. This completes the V1-CHECKLIST Phase-J "Full-campaign playthrough probe" item.

## D142 тАФ PHASE H ┬╖ H5-i4 **FORTIFICATIONS DEPTH** тАФ staged works, facing-aware cover, prepared abatis, charge impetus, and terrain sim hooks (the 4th step closing the locked D138 arc) тАФ [CLAUDE impl, D74 gameplay carve-out] (2026-06-26)

The fourth H5 increment closes the UG:G-fidelity modern-engine push. Unlike H5-i2/i3, this is **not** presentation-only: it is a deliberate **D74 gameplay carve-out** because fortifications, terrain friction, and committed charges change player-facing tactics. The discipline is the D74 universal-model law: one shared combat/movement model, no per-battle outcome fudge, no scoreboard writes, and no AI-only hidden exception.

- **FORTIFICATIONS (`src/tactical/T13-engineering.js`):** entrenchment now stages from rifle pits / hasty cover to a full parapet to a redoubt/earthwork while preserving the existing `u.entrench` progress meter and B-5 realism scaling. `fldEngCover(u, fromX, fromZ)` is stage + facing aware: front fire gets full earned cover, flank fire gets reduced cover, rear fire bypasses the works. A unit that leaves its own works no longer receives cover while the visible works fade. The HUD names the stage and front-cover multiplier; 2D/3D draw hasty/parapet/redoubt shapes; the end card teaches the Hess/Mahan spade-to-fieldworks lesson.
- **PREPARED ABATIS:** abatis built by a brigade already inside its own parapet/redoubt is stamped `prepared`/`worksStage`, starts stronger, slows attackers more, inflicts stronger morale/disorder/fatigue shock, clears slower, and renders with a heavier backing + more stakes. A standalone abatis still works as before; prepared bite is tied to real works, not a free obstacle buff.
- **CHARGE IMPETUS (`src/tactical/T20-order-feel.js` + T0 seams):** player-issued charges get a 1.2s correction grace. After commit, casual move/hold/queue/re-aim orders are blocked until contact, target loss, fog loss, own rout, or own death. AI inline charge behavior remains unchanged. The HUD reports correcting/committed/contact status.
- **TERRAIN SIM WIRING (`src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js`):** H5-i3's swamp/town/fort arrays now feed universal `fldCoverAt`/`fldMoveFactor` hooks. Fort = strongest cover + attacker ditch/parapet friction; town = hard cover + street/fence friction; swamp = soft concealment + major movement slow. Existing wall/woods/hill behavior is retained. `src/tactical/T22-terrain-readability.js` remains presentation-only; the sim reads live in T0 only.
- **Static guard updates:** probes and comments no longer describe swamp/town/fort as combat-inert in the live model. The D141 record remains historical ("visual-only in that increment"), but D142 is the point where those terrain arrays become active.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt:** direct audit found one confirmed bug: the charge-lock comment promised release on own rout/death, but `fldChargeLocked` did not test the charging unit's own state. Fixed `fldChargeLocked` and `fldChargeHudSelected`; extended `probe-order-feel` to assert own rout/death release and restored lock behavior before contact. Other audited risks held: AI charges unchanged, target loss releases, contact releases, no terrain read leaks outside T0/T22, flank/rear bypass retained, abandoned works give no cover, prepared-abatis scaling is bounded.

## D141 тАФ PHASE H ┬╖ H5-i3 **TERRAIN READABILITY** тАФ the modern engine now makes high/low ground (and every topography type) EXPLICIT (the 3rd step of the locked D138 arc) тАФ [AARON 3 forks via AskUserQuestion + CLAUDE impl] (2026-06-26)

The third H5 increment: the modern (non-hex) engine's terrain is now EXPLICIT and READABLE тАФ high/low ground at a glance, a player-chosen elevation render, an on-hover readout, and every topography type visually distinct. **Same discipline as i2 (NOT i1's carve-out): PRESENTATION-ONLY тЖТ the FULL D74 byte-identity law** (proven via `probe-presets` 26/26 + `probe-phased-ab` 20/0-diff). Hex = Classic, untouched.

- **Aaron's 3 forks (AskUserQuestion, 2026-06-26):** (1) elevation palette = **Viridis** (the reference CVD-safe perceptual ramp); (2) legend = **always-on compact panel** (docked bottom-right, collapsible); (3) topography scope = **add swamp/town/fort too** (not just name the existing types) тАФ Aaron accepted these as VISUAL-now / sim-cover-wiring-later, which is what keeps i3 byte-identical.
- **WHAT SHIPPED:** NEW `src/tactical/T22-terrain-readability.js` тАФ wraps the render seams BY ASSIGNMENT (fld3dInit / fld3dBuildTerrain / fld2dInit / fldPointerMove / fldExit; the T16/T18/T21 pattern, carrying ._wx/._atmo/._rr/._vf markers forward). **(a) Three elevation modes** on a new `G.settings.fldElevMode` ("hillshade" DEFAULT / "contours" / "hypsometric"), cycled from the T6 settings drawer + an `R` hotkey + the legend's mode chip. **HILLSHADE in 3D = T21's existing relief** (T22 adds NOTHING to the 3D ground in hillshade тЖТ the relief is never double-counted); the 3D hypsometric tint (a viridis overlay mesh) + contour LineSegments+labels are PREBUILT once and `.visible`-toggled per mode (snappy, no rebuild, no camera jerk). **2D top-down had NO relief at all** тЖТ T22 paints its own cached hillshade / hypsometric / contour layers (offscreen-canvas-cached, one blit/frame). **(b) Legend + on-hover readout** тАФ a `#fldElevLegend` panel (mode chip, viridis gradient bar, a live elevation+type readout from `__FIELD.hover`+`fldTerrainH`, and a topography key of the types present this battle). **(c) Swamp / town / fort** тАФ new render types read from `__FIELD.terrain.swamps[]/.towns[]/.forts[]` (each `{x,z,r}`), each visually distinct in 2D + 3D (swamp = wet teal disc + reeds; town = clustered buildings; fort = angular earthwork berm + bastions); a demo set placed in the sandbox showcase.

## D140 тАФ PHASE H ┬╖ H5-i2 **VISUAL FIDELITY** тАФ the modern engine now LOOKS better than Ultimate General: Gettysburg (the polished HYBRID; the 2nd step of the locked D138 arc) тАФ [AARON 3 forks via AskUserQuestion + CLAUDE impl] (2026-06-25)

The second H5 increment: the modern (non-hex) real-time engine's LOOK upgraded to surpass UG:G тАФ richer terrain relief, grounded troops, atmospheric depth тАФ while honoring the period broadsheet palette. **This is the OPPOSITE discipline from i1's gameplay carve-out: it is PRESENTATION-ONLY, held to the FULL D74 byte-identity law** (proven via `probe-presets` 26/26 + `probe-phased-ab` 20/0-diff). The hex engine IS Classic тАФ untouched.

- **Aaron's 3 forks (AskUserQuestion, 2026-06-25):** (1) scope = **Max** тАФ the full additive stack PLUS tier-gated 3D peg-ranks on capable hardware; (2) colour pipeline = **stay LINEAR + additive** (NO global ACES/sRGB flip); (3) ground relief = **Moderate**.
- **THE r128 DECISION (why ADDITIVE, not a tone-map flip):** THREE is r128 (0.128.0), PREDATING the r152 colour-management overhaul тАФ no `outputColorSpace`/`SRGBColorSpace`. A grounded 5-agent recon proved a global `toneMapping=ACESFilmic` + `outputEncoding=sRGB` flip would SPLIT the pipeline (the T16 smoke + T17 precip ShaderMaterials write raw `gl_FragColor` and would NOT tone-map тЖТ a visible seam: smoke darkens, rain warms) AND force re-tuning every hardcoded colour across T0/T10/T17/T18 for a palette that already reads period-correct тЖТ EXCLUDED. Real shadow maps + MeshStandard/PBR terrain also excluded (r128 InstancedMesh depth-pass bug тЖТ woods cast one blob; MeshStandard renders DARKER without an envMap under the linear pipeline; both UHD-617 perf sinks). The win is purely ADDITIVE, palette-preserving.
- **WHAT SHIPPED:** NEW `src/tactical/T21-visual-fidelity.js` тАФ wraps the render seams BY ASSIGNMENT (the T16/T17/T18 pattern, OUTERMOST, carrying every prior `._wx/._atmo/._rr` marker forward) with five layers: (1) **ground RELIEF** тАФ a slope-AO recolour of the terrain VERTEX COLOURS after T18 (height-relief darkens low ground / lifts crests, normalized to the battle's own height range, + a steep-slope exposed-soil tint + a small concavity term; latch `colA._vfAO`; positions NEVER touched тЖТ units seat on analytic `fldTerrainH`); (2) soft round CONTACT SHADOWS тАФ a per-brigade MeshBasic plane decal glued to the ground (a soft pool slightly wider than the block so the marker sits IN the field); (3) gradient SKY DOME тАФ a BackSide MeshBasic sphere whose horizon tracks the live weather fog colour each frame (seamless ground-fogтЖТsky) deepening to a richer zenith, + a free CSS VIGNETTE div (below the HUD, `pointer-events:none`, `aria-hidden`); (4) stylized rank MAP тАФ a white-based CanvasTexture multiplied on each slab so a brigade reads as MASSED INFANTRY (CVD-safe luminance pattern); (5) Max-tier PEG RANKS тАФ a per-brigade InstancedMesh of stylized pegs atop the slab (`!fldLow()` only), laid out once + x-scaled per frame (no per-peg matrix churn), with a bounding sphere so r128 frustum-culls it. Master gate = `fldVfOff()` (rides T18's `G.settings.renderRich==='off'` тЖТ one toggle reverts the whole stack to the byte-identical default look). Manifest: T21 loads last among the tactical modules.
- **BYTE-IDENTITY (the i2 discipline тАФ the INVERSE of i1's carve-out, PROVEN):** the module reads ONLY read-only render+sim fields, writes vertex COLOUR (never position), never a sim field, never `fldRng`, never `_SAVE_VER`. Per-brigade decorations are CHILDREN of unit groups (the base's rebuild/dispose loop frees them); T21 owns only the shared shadow/rank textures + dome + vignette (freed in `fldVfDispose` via the `fldExit` wrap). Casualty fade is correctly delegated to T18 (its `_rrSetGroupOpacity` traverses all children, fading the transparent pegs+shadow; `fldVfSyncUnit` early-returns on `!u.alive`). Proven: **`probe-presets` 26/26 + `probe-phased-ab` 20/0-diff** (final build).
- **VISUAL VETTING (the presentation analog):** NEW `tools/probe-visual-fidelity.mjs` (**26/26**) тАФ 3 scenes (high/off/low): the 7 wrappers + carried markers; the BackSide dome (renderOrder -1) + its fog-matched horizon + the retained sky-background far-clip fallback; the `pointer-events:none` vignette; `colA._vfAO` + high-reads-brighter-than-low relief + positions untouched; the per-brigade glued shadow (gap ~0.5yd) + rank map + Max-tier peg IM (count 22, bounding sphere); the `fldLow()` peg tier-gate; seed/sim invariance across a synchronous render burst; `FLDVF_S.errN===0`; the `renderRich="off"` full revert; 0 pe / 0 texWarn; + a captured screenshot **VISUALLY CONFIRMED** (grounded units in soft shadow pools, the lighter-crest / darker-low-ground relief, rank+peg detail, the dome sky + vignette тАФ a clear palette-preserving uplift over the byte-identical default).
- **DESIGN + BUG-HUNT (ultracode workflows):** a 5-agent recon+design panel grounded the r128 verdicts + the scope ladder before the AskUserQuestion. A 19-agent bug-hunt (6 diverse lenses тАФ D74 purity ┬╖ render-math ┬╖ lifecycle/leak ┬╖ perf/UHD-617 ┬╖ a11y/CVD ┬╖ edge-robust тАФ ├Ч 3-skeptic default-refute + a completeness critic) returned **SAFE TO COMMIT, 0 confirmed findings** (high confidence; D74 confirmed STRUCTURALLY тАФ the headless stepper never enters a 3D seam). The 4 raw findings: 2 refuted (mid-battle `renderRich`/`gfxQuality` toggles aren't reachable through the fld3d UI тАФ grep-confirmed no `renderRich` setter; `gfxQuality` drives the SEPARATE legacy `__M3D` engine), 2 non-blocking perf nits тЖТ APPLIED anyway as forward-looking polish (the peg IM gained a bounding sphere so r128 frustum-culls it off-camera тАФ removing the one genuine overdraw, scaling to the larger Q5/Q6 OOBs; the redundant per-frame shadow-opacity re-pin dropped).
- **VET (PROPER VETTING, GREEN):** `GATE OK`; `probe-visual-fidelity` 26/26; `probe-presets` 26/26 + `probe-phased-ab` 20/0-diff (byte-identity); `probe-render-richness` 30/30 + `probe-weather` 30/30 (two stale assertions ROOT-CAUSE-fixed, NOT weakened: the rr combat-purity scan now excludes T21 тАФ a sibling presentation module that legitimately rides T18's public `fldRrOff()` opt-out; weather's "default background" check passes again because T21 now RETAINS `scene.background` as the seamless far-clip fallback rather than nulling it тАФ which also fills the behind-camera horizon ring the 6000 far-plane clips off the 4600-radius dome); `probe-flags` 36/36 + `probe-atmospherics` 18/18 + `probe-tactical-visuals` ok (the 3D stack coexists); `bootprobe` realErrors:[]; `t1probe` ok; `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346` + `m3dActive:false` (Classic untouched); 0 pageerrors throughout; `wcag-auditor` N/A by construction (the only new DOM is the `aria-hidden` + `pointer-events:none` vignette below the HUD; rank/relief/dome encode nothing by colour alone тЖТ CVD-safe; nothing animates тЖТ no reduceMotion concern). **Committed + pushed.** (Reversible; presentation-only under the full D74 byte-identity law.)

## D139 тАФ PHASE H ┬╖ H5-i1 **MOVEMENT & ORDERING FEEL** тАФ the modern engine now moves & obeys like Ultimate General: Gettysburg (the FIRST step of the locked D138 arc) тАФ [AARON 4 forks via AskUserQuestion + CLAUDE impl] (2026-06-25)

The first H5 increment: the modern (non-hex) real-time engine's PLAYER CONTROL SURFACE upgraded to UG:G fluidity. **This is the deliberate carve-out from the D74 byte-identity law** тАФ movement/order changes alter the sim, so they are vetted as GAMEPLAY (synthetic-gesture probe), NOT via byte-identity. (The hex engine IS Classic тАФ untouched.)

- **Aaron's 4 forks (AskUserQuestion, 2026-06-25):** (1) order model = **immediate + shift-queue** (a planned waypoint route); (2) charge = **drag-onto-enemy charges THAT brigade** (no impetus commit-lock yet тАФ deferred to H5-i4); (3) facing UX = **point + facing handle** (tap places keeping facing; a drag swings a visible handle arrow; a moving unit's handle stays grabbable to re-aim); (4) fortify = **faster/cheaper digging**.
- **WHAT SHIPPED:** NEW `src/tactical/T20-order-feel.js` тАФ the gesture resolver `fldResolveOrderGesture(sel, gst)` (the testable core: place+face ┬╖ drag-to-charge ┬╖ shift-queue ┬╖ re-aim), the waypoint queue (`fldEnqueueOrder`/`fldApplyOrder`/`fldOrderQueueAdvance`), `fldEnemyAt`/`fldOrderHasHandle`/`fldHandleHit`, and the live ORDER GHOST in BOTH renderers (2D `fldOrderGhost2d`: destination footprint + facing-handle arrow + stem + queued-route dots + charge double-arrow/foe-ring; 3D `fld3dEnsureGhost`/`fld3dSyncDrag`: a persistent group тАФ ring + facing arrow + a charge foe-ring + a queue "+" tick). T0 seams: `fldOrderCharge(u,target)` (optional target; default = the VERBATIM nearest-enemy scan); `fldStepMovement` arrival тЖТ `fldOrderQueueAdvance` (queue hook); `fldPointerDown/Up` rewired to the resolver + handle-hit; `fld2dDraw`/`fld3dInit`/`fld3dRender`/`fld3dDispose` ghost hooks; the HUD help line. T13: `DIG_TIME_BASE` 70 тЖТ **42** (full parapet ~42s @ Balanced, was 70 тАФ Arcade ~29s / Historian ~55s).
- **BYTE-IDENTITY HELD FOR HEADLESS AI-vs-AI (the discipline that made the carve-out safe):** I changed ONLY the player control surface + the dig RATE. A pre-implementation Opus safety analysis + the bug-hunt's byte-identity lens + critic independently confirmed: no AI/scenario unit ever calls `fldOrderCharge` (the AI sets `u.order` inline), ever gets a `.queue` (only the player shift-drag creates it; `fldMakeUnit` never inits it тЖТ the queue-advance guard is a strict no-op), or ever digs (T13 invariant) тЖТ the queue/charge/dig changes never execute headlessly; the ghost is render/pointer-layer (headless runs renderer 'none'). **Proven: `probe-presets` 26/26 + `probe-phased-ab` 20 comparisons / 0 diffs (vs HEAD, final build) + all 9 per-battle probes unchanged.** So the per-battle sim outcomes stay byte-identical EVEN THOUGH this is the carve-out тАФ the carve-out's room is the human's controls, not the AI's.
- **GAMEPLAY VETTING (the carve-out's proof):** NEW `tools/probe-order-feel.mjs` (12/12, 0 pe) drives synthetic gestures headlessly and asserts the resulting `u.order`/`u.queue` тАФ place+face, tap-keeps-facing, drag-onto-the-FAR-enemy charges that one (not nearest), default-charge-still-nearest (the byte-identity invariant), shift-queue append, queue-advance on arrival, re-aim, handle hit-test, fog-gated `fldEnemyAt`, the dig-timing delta (logged **42s vs 70s**), the no-AI-queue/no-AI-dig invariant over a full 1936-step AI battle, and the 2D ghost rendering.
- **BUG-HUNT (31 agents, 6 lenses ├Ч 3-skeptic refute + completeness critic тЖТ SAFE TO COMMIT, 0 must-fix, 0 HIGH, no byte-identity leak):** 7 confirmed render/pointer/UX/a11y findings, all minor. I fixed 4 in-increment under the standing AA/CVD-by-shape bar: **RR-1** (3D ghost materials gained `depthWrite:false` тАФ was polluting the transparent-pass depth buffer, the T12 convention); **RR-2** (`renderOrder` set per child mesh 13/14 тАФ group-level was a no-op); **A11Y-1** (the queue-vs-immediate 2D drag now reads by SHAPE тАФ a dashed stem + a "+" append glyph тАФ not color alone, fixing the protan/deutan collapse of the amber/green pair); **A11Y-2** (the 3D ghost gained shape redundancy тАФ a charge foe-ring + a queue "+" tick тАФ so charge/move/queue differ by shape, not only color); **GM-1+UX-1** (dropped `charge` from `fldOrderHasHandle` тЖТ a charging unit exposes no re-aim handle, killing the no-effect re-aim gesture + the shift-on-charge-handle drop). Left **UX-2** (select-radius can shadow a handle in dense clusters) as documented-acceptable for the 2-brigade sandbox тАФ revisit with denser OOBs.
- **VET (GREEN):** `GATE OK`; `probe-order-feel` 12/12; `probe-presets` 26/26; `probe-phased-ab` 20/0-diff; 9 per-battle probes + field + fog all ok; `probe-engineering-corps` 22/22 (dig retune passes тАФ its assertions are relationship-based); `bootprobe` realErrors:[]; `probe-flags` 36/36 + `probe-tactical-visuals` ok (3D scene healthy with the ghost group); `t1probe` 14/14; `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; 0 pageerrors throughout; 2D ghost visually confirmed. **Committed + pushed.** (Reversible; the engine carve-out is gameplay-vetted, NOT byte-identity тАФ the D74 carve-out per D138.)

## D138 тАФ PHASE H ┬╖ **THE UG:G-FIDELITY MODERN-ENGINE DIRECTION** (locked) тАФ the modern (non-hex) battle engine must look AND play better than Ultimate General: Gettysburg on PS4 тАФ [AARON] (popup + free-text directives, 2026-06-25)

Aaron set the headline target for the tactical layer and resolved four forks by AskUserQuestion. Recorded as standing project law (V1-CHECKLIST "H5 тАФ THE UG:G-FIDELITY MODERN-ENGINE PUSH"; memory `civilwar-modern-engine-ugg-fidelity` + `civilwar-terrain-readability`).
