The **modern engine has NO hex boxes** тАФ it must "play and move fluidly like UG:G": **drag-click-and-direct** movement & charge orders, formation facing, and a **fortify/entrench option**. Zero grid snap.
- **Build order (the 4 answers):** (1) **Movement & ordering FEEL first** тАФ the fluid drag/click/direct control + fortify, before the other layers; this is GAMEPLAY/engine work that alters the sim, so it is NOT under the D74 byte-identical law and must be vetted as gameplay. (2) **Visual style = polished HYBRID** (3D terrain + stylized troop markers/flags, made far richer) тАФ NOT photoreal-3D-models, NOT painterly-2D. (3) **Terrain readability** тАФ explicit high/low-ground identification (legend + on-hover readout), a **shadingтЖФlines TOGGLE** (default **HILLSHADE**; toggle to contour-lines+labels and color-by-height), all topography visually distinct; presentation-only тЖТ honor D74. (4) **Asset budget = self-contained core + optional HD pack** тАФ ship the one file looking great offline-anywhere AND offer an optional downloadable HD texture/model pack (extends the run-k linked-assets relaxation; no media lib may require `SharedArrayBuffer`, D71).
- **Why:** Aaron wants the real-time engine to be the showpiece that beats a commercial title on both feel and looks, while Classic stays the faithful teaching board.
- **Sequencing:** this is the next major arc after the H1 PD-imagery milestones (D137 closes the imagery sweep's scenes item); Q5 Chattanooga + Q6 USCT battles remain LAST. (Reversible: a roadmap/direction decision, no code yet.)

## D137 тАФ PHASE H (graphics "make it come to life") ┬╖ H1 increment 5: **PD BATTLE-SCENE IMAGERY ON THE PRE-BATTLE BRIEFING** тАФ famous public-domain wartime photographs of the actual fields (Gardner's "Bloody Lane," O'Sullivan's "Harvest of Death," the Marye's-Heights stone-wall dead, the Rappahannock pontoon bridges, the Vicksburg siege lines, Sudley Ford) now head the briefing screen тАФ [AARON go (hands-off, edge-cases-only) + CLAUDE impl] (overnight run, 2026-06-25)

The fifth NEW-asset category in the standing "fully hands-off, edge-cases only" mode (D134). The pre-battle briefing (`bridgeBriefingHTML`) now shows a captioned PD photograph of the real ground the player is about to fight on, keyed by the campaign battle id.

- **WHAT SHIPPED:** `tools/source-scenes-imagery.mjs` (NEW тАФ Commons API, PD-only rasters + a scorer penalizing maps/engravings/monuments/reenactments/postwar, keyed by battle id тЖТ `assets/scenes/<id>.jpg` + `assets/scenes-imagery-provenance.json`) ┬╖ `tools/prep-embed-assets.mjs` (+`scenes` category, 480px/q72/JPEG landscape) ┬╖ `src/51-scenes-imagery.js` (NEW тАФ `sceneImageHtml(battleId)` тЖТ a parchment-framed **captioned `<figure class="scene-img">`** banner [img + figcaption = caption + holding-institution credit] or `""`) wired into `85-battle-bridge.js` `bridgeBriefingHTML` as ONE guarded line after the subtitle, before the army columns. __ASSETS = 198 (155 portraits + 8 weapons + 2 guns + 7 usct + 20 leaders + 6 scenes); embed 2.36MB raw (< 3.0MB HARD).

(3) `src/21-photo-embed.js` (NEW module, manifest after `20-president-render.js`) тАФ overrides `window.portraitFor`: base hi-res relative-path photo (data:image/jpeg) wins when present, else this embedded 128px tier (offline-safe, framed by a pixel-faithful copy of base `_framePhoto`/`_photoMount`), else the base engraving (data:image/png); + a `.lead-badge` MutationObserver upgrade (the base observer calls the CLOSURE `portraitFor`, not `window`). ## D132 тАФ PHASE H (graphics "make it come to life") ┬╖ BASE-ENGINE FIX: **MULTI-PHASE 3D SCENE REBUILD** тАФ the live 3D scene now rebuilds when a multi-phase battle advances a phase (the new unit cast becomes visible, the prior phase's meshes are disposed, the woods/walls/objective-beacon move to the new sector, the camera re-frames it) тАФ fixing a PRE-EXISTING base bug D131's bug-hunt surfaced тАФ [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-25)
The combat-path candidate Aaron chose (AskUserQuestion) over the H1/H2 external-asset layer (deferred тАФ needs Aaron present for the per-asset IP/licensing review). **The bug (pre-existing, git-traced to predate T10/H1b тАФ D131's bug-hunt SURFACED it, not introduced it):** the 4 multi-phase battles (Antietam ┬╖ Gettysburg ┬╖ Chickamauga ┬╖ Vicksburg тАФ 4 of the 9 shipped) each run as sequential phases, and recon confirmed **every phase declares its own distinct sector terrain (own woods/walls) AND its own objective**. On a 3D phase advance the engine (`_fldAdvancePhase`тЖТ`_fldBuildPhase`, T8) swapped in a FRESH unit cast (new ids), fresh terrain, and a fresh objective, but **never rebuilt the live 3D scene** тЖТ the new brigades got no `_u3d` group (INVISIBLE), the prior phase's groups + officer/supply/arms/eng meshes ORPHANED, and the woods/walls/objective-beacon stayed at the OLD sector. (2D was unaffected тАФ it reads live state each frame; the headless sim was unaffected тАФ no 3D. So the bug only ever showed in real 3D play of a multi-phase battle.)
- **EMPIRICALLY CONFIRMED FIRST (the prompt's requirement):** a NEW `tools/probe-phased-3d.mjs` drove each of the 4 battles in the live 3D renderer + advanced every phase exactly as the engine does, asserting the CORRECT post-fix invariants. Run against the **pre-fix** build it FAILED decisively (Antietam phase-1 `coverage=0` [4 units, 0 groups], `orphans=6`, the beacon stranded `dz=65` off the new objective at phase 2; Gettysburg the same) тАФ confirming both symptoms (invisible new units AND stale terrain/objective) before a line was changed.
- **THE FIX (presentation-only; combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION тАФ D74):** new `fld3dRebuildPhaseScene()` (T0), called from `_fldAdvancePhase` (T8) ONLY when `__FIELD.mode3d`, re-runs the same per-phase build sequence as `fld3dInit` тАФ `fld3dBuildTerrain()` (fresh ground/objective-ring+beacon/walls/markers/woods/water) + `fld3dBuildUnits()` (the fresh cast; the T10 wrapper re-skins flags) + officers/supply/arms/flags/eng тАФ then `_fld3dReaimPhase()` reseats the survey camera onto the new objective (B-6 side-aware). The scene-level per-phase terrain meshes are now tracked via `_fld3dTrackPhase` into `__FIELD._phaseScene[]` and disposed by `_fld3dDisposePhaseScene()` at the TOP of `fld3dBuildTerrain` (the renderer/camera/lights/scene/groups container persist; every unit-scoped builder already self-disposes). **The headless stepper (renderer 'none' тЖТ `mode3d` false) NEVER enters the rebuild тЖТ the sim is untouched.**
- **BYTE-IDENTITY PROVEN THREE WAYS:** `probe-presets` **26/26** (the difficulty/byte-identity gate); a NEW `tools/probe-phased-ab.mjs` headless A/B sweep (4 battles ├Ч 5 seeds ├Ч the committed pre-fix build vs the fixed build) = **20 comparisons, 0 diffs** тАФ winner/winBy/per-side casualties/phase-score/per-phase-log/steps identical number-for-number (and historically faithful: Antietam CS-tactical, Gettysburg/Vicksburg US, Chickamauga CS); and all 4 per-battle outcome probes green (their committed expected outcomes are the pre-fix baselines). No combat/data/save file touched; no `_SAVE_VER` bump; never `fldRng`.
- **ADVERSARIAL BUG-HUNT (6 diverse-lens Opus finders тЖТ the 4 findings, ALL FIXED).** The finders returned **4 findings, all one class тАФ a GPU-buffer leak the rebuild introduced by re-calling builders that weren't self-disposing:** **(HIGH + MED, same bug)** `fld3dBuildEng` (T13) did a bare `parent.remove(_engGroup)` (detach WITHOUT traverse-disposing) then dropped the mesh refs тЖТ a phase with entrenchments/abatis/pontoons (the Vicksburg siege) orphaned their geometries/materials on every advance, and the detached group escaped `fld3dDispose`'s scene-traverse at exit too тЖТ **FIXED** self-disposing (`_fld3dDisposeGroup(_engGroup)` first тАФ the berm/abatis/pontoon meshes are its children тАФ matching every other builder; does NOT touch water); **(MED)** `fld3dBuildWater` (T13) disposed its prior `_waterGroup` only AFTER the no-river early-return тЖТ a riverтЖТno-river phase advance left a stale + leaked river тЖТ **FIXED** by moving the dispose ABOVE the early-return; **(LOW)** the T8 rebuild call site fully swallowed exceptions, masking the very invisible-brigade failure D132 fixes тЖТ **FIXED** to `console.warn` (a real failure now surfaces + a probe's console gate catches it; the phase still advances). A **completeness self-check** then confirmed EVERY builder `fld3dRebuildPhaseScene` calls now self-disposes (terrain via `_phaseScene`, markers/beacon tracked, units/officers/supply/arms self-dispose, flags idempotent, eng + water now self-dispose) тЖТ the leak surface is fully closed. (The hunt's automated verify+critic legs were env-blocked тАФ a hung 6th finder + an OOM on the 8 GB Mac during the focused re-run тАФ so they were substituted by inline code-verification of all 4 findings + a standalone completeness-critic agent + the empirical re-vet, the D124/D128 substitution precedent.)
- **Re-vet after the fixes (PROPER VETTING, all GREEN):** `GATE OK`; `probe-phased-3d` **64/64** (all 4 battles, every phase: coverage=1 ┬╖ 0 orphans ┬╖ groupsChildren==units ┬╖ the beacon re-seats on the new objective at every phase ┬╖ woods rebuilt per sector ┬╖ non-blank render ┬╖ 0 pageerrors ┬╖ 0 texture warnings) тАФ re-confirmed AFTER the T13 fixes; `probe-presets` **26/26** re-confirmed post-fix; `probe-phased-ab` **20/20 0 diffs**; `probe-atmospherics` 18/18 ┬╖ `probe-weather` 30/30 ┬╖ `probe-render-richness` 30/30 ┬╖ `probe-audio-ambience` 22/22 ┬╖ `probe-flags` 36/36 ┬╖ `probe-tactical-visuals` 10/10 (the atmospheric/flag stack coexists); `bootprobe` realErrors:[]; `t1probe` ok; `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; VISUALLY CONFIRMED (the captured Burnside's-Bridge phase-2 shot now shows the fresh sector + visible brigades + the re-seated beacon under T17's dawn fog тАФ previously empty). `wcag-auditor` N/A by construction (no new DOM/UI тАФ only a camera re-aim + 3D mesh rebuild). **ENV:** `probe-engineering`/`probe-engineering-corps` are `waitUntil:'load'` тЖТ blocked by the documented THREE-CDN headless load-stall (D97/D110), NOT a regression тАФ the eng/water 3D builders are instead exercised by the `domcontentloaded` `probe-phased-3d` (which drives them through 12 phase advances) + `probe-tactical-visuals`. **Committed + pushed only after the full empirical gate passed.** (Reversible; non-negotiables honored: D74 combat byte-identity proven 3 ways ┬╖ the empirical-vet-before-push gate ┬╖ base.html untouched.)

## D131 тАФ PHASE H (graphics "make it come to life") ┬╖ H1b: **FLAGS & INSIGNIA DEEPENING** тАФ citation-grade battle-aware flag selection + corrected Kearny-patch corps-badge SHAPES (date-gated to the 1863 fields) drawn on the 2D/3D unit markers + the selected-brigade HUD, DEEPENING the existing `src/tactical/T10-flags.js` тАФ [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-25)

## D130 тАФ PHASE H (graphics "make it come to life") ┬╖ H4: **BATTLE-AMBIENCE AUDIO DEEPENING** тАФ a default-OFF, opt-in, stereo-spatialized procedural battle-soundscape bed (rolling-fire wash + gated cannonade sub-bass + fog-gated located cannon/musket reports) UNDER the existing T9 din+SFX тАФ [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-25)
The H4 increment per `.tmp/phase-h-design.md` item 4 + the D91 "continue audio incrementally" decision. The base.html `dinSet` din already gives a MONO intensity bed (rumble + cannon thump + musket crackle), and T9-audio.js (D77) bridges it into the modern tactical engine. H4 DEEPENS the subsystem with a NEW layer тАФ it does NOT replace T9. **Sub-choice decided-&-logged:** a NEW `src/tactical/T19-battle-ambience.js` module (the T16/T17/T18 wrap-by-assignment precedent) rather than editing T9 in place тАФ lowest-risk, idiomatic, keeps the SFX bridge intact. PROCEDURAL WebAudio synthesis only ($0 / single-file тАФ no external sound files; the linked-asset audio fork remains un-started + would be SURFACED first).
- **What shipped:** new `src/tactical/T19-battle-ambience.js` тАФ a spatialized "great-battle" bed layered UNDER T9's din+SFX, pairing 1:1 with the T16 gunsmoke (sound comes from where the smoke rises): (1) a continuous **rolling-fire wash** (looping band-passed noise + a slow swell-LFO tremolo, gain tracking battle intensity тАФ the "one continuous roar"); (2) a **cannonade sub-bass rumble** (looping low-passed brown noise, gated up by the count of brigades actually working their guns); (3) **located cannon/musket reports** тАФ a cannon = sharp crack + body thump + rolling reverberant tail; a musket = a filtered-noise volley "rip" тАФ each panned in stereo by the firing brigade's field-x (side-corrected to the camera end) and **fog-gated** (a hidden foe makes no located sound). Discoverable via a new accessible "Battle ambience" On/Off row appended to T9's audio panel; one-time captioned through T9's accessible caption.
- **ARCHITECTURE тАФ combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION (D74):** touches NO combat file. WRAPS `fld3dRender` / `fld2dDraw` (drive the per-frame decision tick, throttled) / `fldExit` (dispose) / T9's `_fldAudioPanelRows` (append the toggle row) BY ASSIGNMENT тАФ with a generic `keep()` helper that propagates EVERY prior introspection marker (`._atmo`/`._wx`/`._t9audio`/T18's) onto each new wrapper so the sibling probes still see the chain (a regression the no-regression sweep caught mid-build тАФ fixed before commit). OWNS a separate AudioContext (the AUDIO_SCORE / SOUND one-context-per-subsystem convention). Reads ONLY render + read-only sim fields (`u._artFlash`/`u.targetId`/`u.ammo`/`u.state`/`u.x`/`u.id`/`u.side`/`u.alive`, `__FIELD.phase/paused/fog/units`) + `G.settings`; writes NO sim field, NEVER calls `fldRng` (no randomness reaches the sim тАФ audio texture uses `Math.random` like base.html's din), no `_SAVE_VER` (the `battleAmbience` flag is lazy-defaulted). The SCHEDULING DECISIONS (intensity, fog-gate, pan) are recorded in a `FLDAMB` state object whether or not a real audio device exists тЖТ fully testable headless. Diff = `src/tactical/T19-battle-ambience.js` (new) + `src/00-manifest.json` (T19 after T18) + `tools/probe-audio-ambience.mjs` (new) + the generated HTML. Proven by `probe-presets` 26/26 byte-identity AND a per-pure-render-window sim-seed-invariance assertion (240├Ч `fldAmbUpdate`, seed unmoved).
- **ACCESSIBILITY / PERF (Intel UHD-617 floor):** **DEFAULT-OFF** (`G.settings.battleAmbience !== true` тЖТ zero sound, never built тАФ the byte-identical-mix default), **fully suppressed under `reduceMotion`** (the calm default тАФ the T16 convention), volume scaled by the existing `battleLoud` (offтЖТsilent) AND the master capped low (тЙд0.20, under the din's 0.26) so it never overwhelms the cues it sits under ("never jarring"). Located reports defer until the AudioContext is genuinely running (no first-gesture stampede); the bed self-silences on the 'over' screen (no idle-graph drain); source-voices node-pool bounded + all nodes disposed + context suspended on `fldExit`. CVD-safe (no colour-encoded info); the toggle row reuses T9's AA-vetted segmented-button markup (keyboard / focus / aria-pressed) тЖТ `wcag-auditor` N/A by construction.
- **Bug-hunt (the ultracode pattern тАФ 6 diverse-lens Opus finders [byte-identity ┬╖ webaudio-leaks ┬╖ fog-leak ┬╖ edge-robust ┬╖ a11y-ux ┬╖ lifecycle] ├Ч 3-skeptic default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic; 19 agents; critic confidence HIGH; "NO byte-identity violation, NO fog leak, marker-chain correct").** **1 confirmed + 2 critic-surfaced real edge-bugs + 1 LOW refinement, ALL FIXED:** **(CONFIRMED, MED, 3/3)** `fldAmbCaptionOnce` burned the one-shot `captioned` flag BEFORE the caption rendered тАФ but T9's `_fldAudioCaption` no-ops when captions are off (the default), so a user enabling captions mid-battle would never see the cue the layer advertises тЖТ the flag is now consumed ONLY inside the captions-on branch (re-checked cheaply each tick until shown). **(CRITIC, MED)** the six lenses only saw the probe's always-running context; in the real game the context is born SUSPENDED until a gesture, and located reports kept scheduling against the frozen clock тЖТ a stacked "stampede" the instant audio resumed тЖТ `fldAmbReports` now gates on `ctx.state === "running"`. **(CRITIC, LOW)** the live WebAudio graph idled indefinitely on the post-battle 'over' screen (master never zeroed there) тЖТ `fldAmbUpdate` now silences on `phase === "over"`. **(CRITIC, LOW)** StereoPanner nodes shared the source bag, diluting the documented voice cap + a dead `.stop()` per dispose тЖТ panners moved to a separate `pans` pool (cap counts audible voices only; panners disconnect-only). The lifecycle "stale per-phase state" finding was REFUTED 3/3 (singleton `__FIELD`; a negative men-delta clamps to 0; cooldowns expire across the interphase card тАФ benign). Probe strengthened 19тЖТ22 steps (the suspended-ctx gate, the 'over'-silence, the panner-pool disposal).
- **Vetting (PROPER VETTING, all GREEN):** `GATE OK`; `probe-audio-ambience` **22/22** (module + 4 wrappers ┬╖ opt-in activates + beds built + located reports scheduled ┬╖ pan тИИ [-1,1] ┬╖ separate panner pool ┬╖ suspended-ctx defers (0 reports/0 errors) ┬╖ 'over' self-silence ┬╖ sim-seed INVARIANT across 240 pure audio ticks ┬╖ `errN===0` ┬╖ accessible panel row ┬╖ DEFAULT-OFF silent ┬╖ reduceMotion suppressed ┬╖ `battleLoud="off"` master silent ┬╖ fog-gated 5тЖТ0 with lift-control 3 ┬╖ `fldExit` disposes beds+pools+ref ┬╖ 0 pe); `probe-presets` **26/26** (byte-identity тЖТ combat byte-identical, re-confirmed post-fix); `probe-atmospherics` **18/18** (T16 + marker chain) / `probe-weather` **30/30** (T17) / `probe-render-richness` **30/30** (T18) тАФ all coexist; `probe-tactical-visuals` **10/10** (0 texture warnings); `bootprobe` realErrors:[]; `t1probe` 14/14; `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`. ## D129 тАФ PHASE H (graphics "make it come to life") ┬╖ H3-i3: **TERRAIN & UNIT RENDER RICHNESS** тАФ procedural ground texture + woods wind-sway + banner cloth ripple + selection/march polish + casualty fade тАФ [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-24)
The next Phase-H increment after H3-i2 (D128), per `.tmp/phase-h-design.md` item 3. A NEW presentation-only module makes the battlefield itself feel alive тАФ the ground grows real texture, the woods sway, the colours ripple, marching columns bob, and a fallen brigade fades from the field instead of snapping out. Continues leading H with the code-only / single-file-safe / offline procedural wins before the external PD-imagery/footage layer (H1/H2, still to be SURFACED before starting).
- **What shipped:** new `src/tactical/T18-render-richness.js` тАФ (1) **3D ground vertex-colour enrichment** (procedural grass mottle + dry-ochre / damp-lush / bare-earth patches + tilled crop-row corduroy in a "cultivated" mask тАФ positions untouched, colours only); (2) **woods wind-sway** (per-cone tilt-about-base on the InstancedMesh); (3) **banner cloth ripple** (per-unit flag twist/dip, ties H1b flags); (4) **selection-ring pulse** + a **march bob** for moving brigades; (5) a **casualty fade-out** on death (the group settles into the ground + fades over ~0.85s). Plus 2D-canvas equivalents (a cached soft field-grain, a pulsing selection halo, the same casualty fade).
- **ARCHITECTURE тАФ combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION (D74):** touches NO combat file. WRAPS `fld3dBuildTerrain` (enrich + capture) / `fld3dRender` (frame hook) / `fld3dSyncUnit` (per-unit polish) / `fld2dDraw` (2D) / `fldExit` (dispose) BY ASSIGNMENT (the T9/T16/T17 seam; propagates the `._wx`/`._atmo` markers so the wrapper chain stays introspectable). All variation is **analytic value-noise + wall-clock sines тАФ NEVER `fldRng`**; reads ONLY render state + read-only sim fields (`u.x`/`u.z`/`u.alive`/`u.state`/`u.id`, `__FIELD.sel`); writes NO sim field, no `_SAVE_VER`. The ground enrichment recolors VERTICES only тАФ units seat on the analytic `fldTerrainH`, not the mesh, so they never float/sink. **THE BYTE-IDENTICAL DEFAULT:** `renderRich="off"` (or a fresh launch with it set) leaves the un-enriched ground + unswayed woods + flat flags. Diff = `src/tactical/T18-render-richness.js` (new) + `src/00-manifest.json` (T18 after T17) + `tools/probe-render-richness.mjs` (new) + the generated HTML. **No combat/data/save file touched** тАФ proven by `probe-presets` 26/26 byte-identity AND a new per-burst sim-field-invariance probe assertion (x/z/men/morale/facing/formation unchanged across 200 render frames).
- **ACCESSIBILITY / PERF (Intel UHD-617 floor):** every MOTION effect (woods sway, flag ripple, selection pulse, march bob, casualty fade) is suppressed under `reduceMotion` тАФ the STATIC ground texture stays (faithful detail, not motion; the T17 precedent). `renderRich="off"` disables the whole layer (motion reverts mid-battle; the 3D ground tint reverts on the next launch тАФ the T16/T17 apply-time pattern, documented). The woods sway recomputes each instance matrix from a cached base (no drift); `fldLow()` trims sway amplitude + grain cell size; the **2D field-grain is cached to an offscreen canvas** (built once per field/scale, blitted with one `drawImage` тАФ no per-frame fillrate on the weakest 2D-fallback GPU). No new draw call/shader тЖТ no `gl_PointSize` concern. CVD-safe (texture carries no colour-encoded info); no new DOM/text тЖТ `wcag-auditor` N/A by construction.
- **Bug-hunt (the ultracode pattern тАФ 6 diverse-lens Opus finders [byte-identity ┬╖ render-math ┬╖ perf ┬╖ a11y-gating ┬╖ edge-robust ┬╖ lifecycle] ├Ч 3-skeptic default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic; 37 agents; critic confidence HIGH).** **1 substantive bug + 7 real LOWs, ALL FIXED:** **(the one substantive defect, MED/HIGH across 4 lenses, 3/3 votes)** the casualty-fade `g.position.y -= (1-rec.fade)*5` was CUMULATIVE тАФ the base `fld3dSyncUnit` early-returns for a dead unit and never re-seats its Y, so the per-frame decrement compounded to ~125 yards of sink (frame-rate dependent), plunging the fading brigade through the terrain instead of the intended ~5yd settle тЖТ **rewritten ABSOLUTE** (`g.position.y = fldTerrainH(u.x,u.z)+4 - (1-f)*5`), bounded + frame-rate-independent (probe now asserts `maxSink тЙд 8`; measured 4.96). Pure visual glitch тАФ no sim write, D74 intact (the finders + critic confirmed). **(LOW, real)** the fade had no visibility guard тЖТ a fog-hidden enemy that died popped into view as a fading block (a fog-of-war leak) тЖТ guarded on `rec.wasVis` (the base's last-living-frame visibility) + a white-box probe test. **(critic-found LOWs)** a SELECTED unit that died kept its ring at full opacity over the fading ghost тЖТ the ring now fades with the corpse; the fade-end `transparent=false` flip corrupted the textured T10 flag's alpha (latent) тЖТ `_rrSetGroupOpacity` never flips the flag/ring transparent flag; the 2D grain was re-filled (~1300 `fillRect`s) every frame тЖТ offscreen-canvas cache; `renderRich="off"` toggled mid-battle didn't revert the motion effects тЖТ the early-return was removed so the motion-off reset paths run; the probe only proved seed-stability (not sim-field invariance) тЖТ added the x/z/men/morale/facing snapshot; the empty-catch wrappers swallowed per-unit throws silently тЖТ a counted + once-warned `FLDRR_S.errN` the probe asserts is 0. **Probe strengthened 24тЖТ30 steps.**
- **Vetting (PROPER VETTING, all GREEN):** `GATE OK`; `probe-render-richness` **30/30** (module + 5 wrappers + chain markers ┬╖ ground enriched [meanAbsDelta 0.0178, 92% of vertices changed] + positions untouched ┬╖ woods sway/reset ┬╖ flag ripple/reset ┬╖ selection pulse ┬╖ casualty fade visible+opacity-in-(0,1)+BOUNDED-sink+fog-ghost-guarded+hidden-when-done ┬╖ sim seed + sim-field INVARIANT ┬╖ `errN===0` ┬╖ `renderRich="off"` un-enriched/unswayed/flat ┬╖ reduceMotion keeps texture suppresses motion ┬╖ 2D paints, 0 pe); `probe-presets` **26/26** (byte-identity тЖТ combat byte-identical, re-confirmed post-fix); `probe-atmospherics` **18/18** (T16 coexists); `probe-weather` **30/30** (T17 coexists); `probe-tactical-visuals` **10/10** (all 9 battles render, 0 texture warnings); `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; `bootprobe` realErrors:[]; `t1probe` 0 fails/0 pe. VISUALLY CONFIRMED (the field reads as real terrain with patches + tilled stripes; woods sway, flags ripple in the live battles). **NEXT in H3/H4:** H4 audio deepening тЖТ H1b flags/insignia polish тЖТ H1/H2 PD imagery + reenactment footage (**SURFACE first** тАФ external assets / network / single-file stress). **Q5 Chattanooga + Q6 USCT battles LAST** (Aaron's locked queue). (Reversible; non-negotiables honored тАФ D74 no sim write + the empirical-vet-before-push gate.)

## D128 тАФ PHASE H (graphics "make it come to life") ┬╖ H3-i2: **WEATHER + TIME-OF-DAY ATMOSPHERE** тАФ procedural sky/light re-tint + rain/snow precipitation per a citation-grade per-battle weather hint тАФ [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-24)
The natural successor to H3-i1 (D127). A NEW presentation-only module gives each battle a sky and light that match its history. Designed + data-scoped at `.tmp/phase-h-design.md`. Continues leading Phase H with the code-only / single-file-safe / offline procedural wins before the external PD-imagery/footage layer (H1/H2, still to be SURFACED before starting).
- **What shipped:** new `src/tactical/T17-weather.js` тАФ re-tints the 3D `scene.background` / `scene.fog` / sun (directional) / hemisphere AND washes the 2D canvas to a resolved `{sky, time}` palette (sky тИИ clear/overcast/rain/fog/haze/snow; time тИИ dawn/morning/midday/afternoon/dusk), plus optional procedural **rain/snow precipitation** (a second `THREE.Points` cloud reusing the T16 shader pattern) and a faint 2D precip hatch. A one-time accessible **weather note** is announced at battle start via the existing role=status `fldScenarioBanner`. **Marquee visible win: Antietam's dawn Cornfield ground-fog** (the one genuinely non-clear sky in the roster); the rest carry faithful time-of-day light (warm afternoons, cool mornings).
- **ARCHITECTURE тАФ combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION (D74):** touches NO combat file. WRAPS `fld3dInit` (re-tint) / `fld3dRender` (precip + note) / `fld2dDraw` (wash + note) / `fldExit` (dispose) BY ASSIGNMENT (the T9/T16 seam; propagates T16's `._atmo` marker so the wrapper chain stays introspectable). Reads ONLY the scenario's structured `weather` hint (`_scenTop.weather` for multi-phase, else `scenData.weather`) + render state; its OWN LCG for the precip drift тАФ **NEVER `fldRng`** (probe-asserted: the sim seed is untouched across a synchronous wx render loop); no sim write, no `_SAVE_VER`. **THE BYTE-IDENTICAL DEFAULT:** a NO weather hint тАФ or a `clear`/`midday` hint тАФ resolves to `null` and applies ZERO change (every currently-shipped look is preserved until a battle opts in). Diff = `src/tactical/T17-weather.js` (new) + `src/00-manifest.json` (T17 after T16) + the 9 `data/*.json` weather blocks + `tools/probe-weather.mjs` (new) + the generated HTML. **No combat/save file touched.**
- **THE CITATION-GRADE DATA (research+verify Workflow, 18 agents: 9 Opus historians ├Ч 9 default-refute Opus verifiers):** each battle's documented modeled-window weather, тЙе2 real sources, anti-fabrication. The verifiers earned their keep тАФ they REFUSED to fabricate drama: Gettysburg `hazeтЖТclear` (Rev. Jacobs' instrument log: bright, 4/10 cumulus at the 2pm Pickett's-Charge window); Fredericksburg `fogтЖТclear/afternoon` (the Rappahannock fog LIFTED ~10am, before the noon-to-dark assault тАФ the note still teaches the morning fog that hid the crossing); Shiloh `clear/morning` (the famous torrential rain was OVERNIGHT, outside the modeled day); Vicksburg removed a misattributed Theodore Lyman source (an Army-of-the-Potomac aide, never at Vicksburg). **The honest finding: the "fog of war" at most of these battles was POWDER-SMOKE (already shipped via T16), not weather** тАФ so the sky was usually clear; only Antietam's dawn fog is a real non-clear sky. Final hints: bullrun1 clear/afternoon ┬╖ malvernHill clear/afternoon(Inferred) ┬╖ **antietam fog/dawn** ┬╖ fredericksburg clear/afternoon ┬╖ chancellorsville clear/morning ┬╖ gettysburg clear/afternoon ┬╖ shiloh clear/morning ┬╖ vicksburg clear/midday(a no-op) ┬╖ chickamauga clear/afternoon.
- **ACCESSIBILITY / PERF (Intel UHD-617 floor):** the static sky/light TINT is faithful + motion-free тЖТ it applies under `reduceMotion`; only the PRECIPITATION (motion) is suppressed under `reduceMotion` (probe-verified: tint kept, no `wxPrecip` cloud). `G.settings.weather==="off"` disables the whole layer тЖТ the clear default. Fog far-plane held **тЙе1500** in EVERY palette (incl. the time blends) so the objective never vanishes (probe-asserted). One `THREE.Points` precip cloud (single draw call) + `fldLow()` budget (520/200) + a `gl_PointSize` clamp to the driver `ALIASED_POINT_SIZE_RANGE` max. Neutral atmospheric wash (no colour-encoded info тЖТ CVD-safe); no new DOM/text/interactive surface (the note reuses the AA-vetted `fldScenarioBanner`) тЖТ `wcag-auditor` N/A by construction.
- **DECIDED-&-LOGGED (D61) тАФ Antietam's battle-level dawn-fog:** the fog/dawn hint is applied to ALL THREE Antietam phases (Cornfield тЖТ Bloody Lane тЖТ Burnside's Bridge), though historically the ground fog opened the Cornfield (Phase 1) and burned off by the later phases. Kept as the iconic, verified BATTLE SIGNATURE (the modeled engagement opens in the dawn mist, and the note teaches "it thinned as the sun rose"); per-phase weather would touch the T8 combat-path phase view (`_fldPhaseView`) and is logged as a clean future H3-i3 enhancement, NOT this milestone. The bug-hunt verifiers SPLIT on this (no majority-confirm) тЖТ a simplification, not a defect.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (6 diverse-lens Opus finders [byte-identity/RNG ┬╖ lifecycle/GPU-leak ┬╖ WebGL1/r128 shader ┬╖ a11y/perf/fog-readability ┬╖ robustness/edge ┬╖ effect-correctness+history+probe-rigor] ├Ч 3-skeptic default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic; the critic leg STALLED after the finder+verify phases completed тАФ substituted by a rigorous INLINE completeness pass, the D124 precedent). **8 findings; 1 HIGH confirmed, fixed; the rest LOW/refuted, addressed:** **(HIGH, 3/3 confirmed)** the atmosphere note re-fired EVERY render frame тАФ `_wxLaunchKey` included `__FIELD.seed`, which `fldRng` MUTATES every sim tick тЖТ the per-launch key changed each frame тЖТ the "noted" flag reset тЖТ banner/SR-status spam. **FIXED:** key the note on the STABLE `__FIELD.scenario` (fldExit resets it for a relaunch) + a new probe assertion that renders sim-ticking frames and asserts EXACTLY ONE weather banner. **(LOW, real)** `FLDWX.SKY["constructor"/"__proto__"]` resolves an inherited `Object.prototype` member (truthy) тЖТ bypassed the `!FLDWX.SKY[sky]` guard тЖТ a palette with no `.bg`. **FIXED:** `Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(...)` validation + a malformed-input probe assertion. **(LOW/refuted, locked anyway)** precip-dispose-on-`fldExit` + malformed-input safety were un-probed тЖТ added assertions; the `fld3dDispose`-wrap finding was refuted 3/3 (T17's `fldExit` wrapper runs `fldWxDispose` BEFORE the engine teardown; the scene-traverse disposes the mesh regardless; a stale ref self-heals on next build). A real **probe test-pollution bug** (the synth scenes mutated the SHARED `GAME_DATA` weather object, clobbering a later scene's pristine hint) was caught by the note-once assertion and fixed (inject onto a shallow copy).
- **Vetting (PROPER VETTING, all GREEN):** `GATE OK`; `probe-weather` **30/30**, 0 pe, 0 texture warnings (the byte-identical default ┬╖ each sky palette applies ┬╖ fog far тЙе1500 on the real fog battle ┬╖ rain/snow `wxPrecip` built + DISPOSED on exit ┬╖ `reduceMotion` suppresses precip but keeps the tint ┬╖ the once-per-launch note ┬╖ malformed-input safety ┬╖ the driver `gl_PointSize` clamp ┬╖ the sim seed UNCHANGED across the wx render loop); `probe-presets` **26/26** (9-baseline byte-identity тЖТ **combat byte-identical**, seed-for-seed); `probe-atmospherics` **18/18** (T16 + T17 coexist; the transitive `._atmo` marker holds); `probe-tactical-visuals` **10/10** (the now-tinted battles render with beacons seated, 0 texture warnings, 0 pe); `bootprobe` realErrors:[]; `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; `t1probe` ok; broad no-regression GREEN in isolation (field/fog/motion/arms/officers/csplayer/tactical-roster/command/camp/engineering-corps/accessibility тАФ an initial batched sweep threw spurious `steps:0` launch failures from 8 GB-Mac memory pressure under the concurrent sweep+bug-hunt; re-running each in isolation was GREEN). **VISUALLY CONFIRMED:** Antietam's pale warm dawn ground-fog (distant brigades fading into the mist, the objective still readable); the grey rain field with falling streaks. ## D127 тАФ PHASE H (graphics "make it come to life") ┬╖ H3-i1: **BATTLEFIELD GUNSMOKE ATMOSPHERICS** тАФ procedural black-powder smoke / artillery muzzle-belch / impact dust on the real-time tactical engine (the period "fog of war") тАФ [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-24)
**FORK CLEARED (AskUserQuestion):** Phase E completed (E1тАУE4, D126); the next pillar was open (F/I/H/J). Aaron chose **Phase H**. Sub-choice decided-&-logged: lead H with the **code-only / single-file-safe / offline procedural** wins (no external-asset licensing/IP risk; honors D30.8) before the heavy PD-imagery/footage ingestion (H1/H2, which I'll SURFACE before starting тАФ the one external-asset, network-touching item). H3-i1 = the marquee battlefield-atmosphere increment. (Full ordered H roadmap + the H3-i2 weather/time-of-day design at `.tmp/phase-h-design.md`.)
- **What shipped:** new `src/tactical/T16-atmospherics.js` тАФ procedural gunsmoke that billows from firing lines + artillery, accumulates into a sector pall, drifts on a per-battle wind, and slowly clears; artillery muzzle-belch; impact dust where rounds strike. Renders in BOTH the 2D fallback canvas (cached soft-sprite stamps) and the live 3D scene (one `THREE.Points` cloud + a tiny per-particle alpha/size/colour shader). **Teaching tie-in:** black-powder smoke literally WAS the period's fog of war (the reason real commanders lost sight of their own lines).
- **ARCHITECTURE тАФ combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION (D74):** touches NO combat file. WRAPS `fld2dDraw` / `fld3dRender` / `fldExit` by ASSIGNMENT (the T9-audio seam pattern). Reads firing/impact state READ-ONLY (`u.targetId`/`u.ammo`/`u._artFlash`/`u.underFire`/`u.facing`/`u.state`/`u.x`/`u.z`). Uses its OWN private LCG (`A.rs`) тАФ **NEVER `fldRng`** (the sim seed is provably untouched тАФ probe-asserted across 240 synchronous spawn steps), no sim write, no `_SAVE_VER`. New `src/95-playstyle.js` тАФ a **"Play Your Way"** hub holding (1) **play-style presets** тАФ President (owner-mode focus) / General-Commander (battle focus) / Free Command (the shipped neutral) тАФ and (2) the **D39 Historian teaching layer** (the alt-history emergent-only toggle, a read-only Command-&-Realism read-out, and hand-offs to the existing pickers). Surfaced TWO ways from ONE panel body (`_psPanelHTML(ctx)`): an 18th President's-Desk tab (rendered inline like the Codex tab, ctx="desk") AND a main-menu overlay (`openSheet`, ctx="menu"). Period-broadsheet styled, CVD-safe (glyph decorative + the word label carries meaning + the тЦ╕ marker), full keyboard/ARIA, reduce-motion-safe.
- **D123.1 тАФ play-style is an EMPHASIS, never a hard gate (faithful to D39.1).** In this game both layers are always available (the locked "both battle modes selectable" charter), so a play-style preset must NOT remove content. Its genuine, pure-UI consumers: (a) `psDefaultDeskTab` sets which Desk tab the desk first lands on (CommanderтЖТCommand; President/FreeтЖТthe War Effort overview; **unset or unknown тЖТ "economy" тЖТ byte-identical** for existing players, guarded by a `deskTabs` whitelist), and (b) it is remembered + tailors the hub's own guidance. `openWarDept`'s literal `_wdTab="economy"` became `_wdTab=psDefaultDeskTab()`. (Reversible.)
- **D123.2 тАФ PURE settings layer; byte-identical combat BY CONSTRUCTION (D74).** The module writes ONLY two NON-combat strategic flags тАФ `G.settings.playStyle` (new, owned here) and `G.settings.altHistoryEmergentOnly` (a SECOND surface for the divergence-tab flag) тАФ plus a private `cw_playstyle` localStorage bundle (the proven T6 boot-load pattern, defaults-only). NO RNG; NO `_SAVE_VER` bump. (Reversible.)
- **D123.3 тАФ the desk context is READ-ONLY for hand-offs.** A mid-campaign desk hand-off to `fldPresetMenu`/`openSettings`/`openMainMenu` would tear down the desk sheet + its between-battles continuation chain (`_pdAfterDeskClose`), so the desk-tab context shows read-only hints; the menu-overlay context offers the live "AdjustтАж/OpenтАж" buttons (which return cleanly to the menu). No T6/base edit required тЖТ preserves the byte-identity argument. (Reversible.)

## D122 тАФ E2 increment 3: **THE GUIDED TUTORIAL** тАФ a multi-step modal tour orienting the player across all three layers тАФ [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-24)
- **What shipped:** the third E2 / S4-education item тАФ a GUIDED TUTORIAL. New `src/94-tutorial.js` renders a self-contained, 7-step modal tour (`#tutOverlay`) тАФ the sequenced onboarding the static welcome/help cards aren't. Steps: the three layers ┬╖ the President's Desk ┬╖ the Great Decisions ┬╖ the Battles ┬╖ **the Codex & the Glossary** (showcasing E2-i1/i2) ┬╖ Winning the War ┬╖ Play Your Way. Back/Next/Skip, a "Step N of M" indicator + progress dots, full keyboard control (Esc/Left/Right/Enter), a focus trap, ARIA dialog semantics, reduce-motion-safe fade. Launched from THREE entry points wired into the `src/92-help-overlay.js` spine: the first-launch welcome card, the How-to-Play panel, and a main-menu "GUIDED TOUR" button.
- **ACCESSIBILITY-FIRST:** role=dialog + aria-modal + aria-labelledby/describedby; the step `<h2>` (tabindex=-1) is focused per step with an `aria-label` "Step N of M: <title>" so a screen-reader announces both position and heading; the background is `aria-hidden` while the modal is open (restored on close); a symmetric Tab focus trap cycles [Skip, Back, Next]; reduce-motion disables the fade; the dots/glyph are decorative aria-hidden (the text carries meaning). wcag-auditor AA (added a `:focus-visible` ring for the Skip button; contrast 4.30тАУ13.23:1).
- **Architecture тАФ PURE UI / HELP LAYER (byte-identical combat BY CONSTRUCTION):** the tutorial reads NO campaign/sim state and writes nothing but a localStorage "seen" flag (no campaign mutation, no RNG, no `_SAVE_VER`). No tactical/combat/tick/resolve/bridge path references the tutorial (grep + a probe static-scan over 20 combat files). The three 92 launch hooks are `typeof`-guarded. Diff = `src/94-tutorial.js` + `src/00-manifest.json` (`94-tutorial.js`) + `src/92-help-overlay.js` (3 launch hooks + a "?"-modality guard) + `tools/probe-tutorial.mjs` + the generated HTML.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt (5 diverse-lens Opus finders ├Ч default-refute verify + a completeness critic; 14 agents) тЖТ invariantsHold=FALSE initially; 8 confirmed findings (deduped ~6), ALL FIXED + probe-locked:** **(MED)** the forward-Tab focus trap never reached the Skip button (broken focus order, WCAG 2.4.3) тЖТ rewrote the trap as an explicit symmetric cycle over [Skip, Back, Next] with the announce-only title routing in; **(MED)** the global "?" hotkey opened How-to-Play BEHIND the open modal tour (modality leak / stacked dialogs) тЖТ guarded the "?" handler to bail when the tour is open; **(LOW)** a double-`tutStart` captured the focus-restore target as `<body>` (it removed the prior overlay before reading activeElement) тЖТ capture before teardown, guarded; **(LOW)** the background wasn't made inert for AT тЖТ `aria-hidden` the background under the modal (+ a double-start inert-restore so no stale `aria-hidden` leaks); **(LOW)** the step position wasn't announced тЖТ folded into the title's `aria-label`; **(LOW)** a ~50ms interactive pre-mount menu window on the welcome/help launch тЖТ dropped the `setTimeout` (the z-index 100001 modal covers the menu immediately). Purity + content (the 7 step bodies: balanced HTML, accurate, anti-Lost-Cause) fully held.
- **Vet (PROPER VETTING, all GREEN):** `GATE OK ┬╖ citations тЬУ`; `probe-tutorial` **15/15** (deck schema ┬╖ ARIA dialog ┬╖ Next/Back/finish ┬╖ arrows/Esc ┬╖ title-focus + trap ┬╖ last-step "To the Field" + seen-flag ┬╖ reduce-motion ┬╖ pure-readout ┬╖ the 6 fix-locks ┬╖ static-scan), **0 pageerrors**; no-regression GREEN тАФ `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`, `probe-codex` 18/18, `probe-glossary` 12/12, `probe-desk` 13/13, `probe-decisions` 19/19, `probe-divergence` 14/14, `probe-afteraction` 15/15, `bootprobe` ok (realErrors:[]), `t1probe` 14/14 (all 0 pe). ## D121 тАФ E2 increment 2: **THE INLINE GLOSSARY** тАФ hover/tap/focus codex definitions woven into the teaching prose тАФ [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
- **What shipped:** the second E2 / S4-education item тАФ an INLINE GLOSSARY. New `src/93-glossary.js` DOM-decorates the rendered teaching prose of the two read-only teaching desk tabs (After-Action, Your War vs History): a TreeWalker wraps codex terms in inline `<button class="gl-term">` triggers (a dotted brass underline) and a shared `#glTip` tooltip shows the definition on hover/focus/tap. It reads the SAME codex data as the i1 Codex tab (`cxGlossaryIndex`/`cxLookupShort`) тАФ one source of truth. Hooked into `_wdRefresh` (guarded, scoped to afteraction/warvshistory), byte-identical when absent.
- **ACCESSIBILITY-FIRST:** the definition rides each trigger's `aria-label` ("<visible matched text> тАФ <short> (glossary term)") so a screen-reader announces it on FOCUS regardless of the visual tooltip; the tooltip is `aria-hidden` role=tooltip decorative reinforcement (no double-announce). Triggers are real keyboard-operable `<button>`s; Esc dismisses; a scoped `:focus-visible` ring; reduce-motion disables the tooltip transition; the cue is a dotted UNDERLINE (shape), not color-alone. wcag-auditor AA (tooltip 13.51:1, term/border 8.10:1; no edits).
- **Surface-derivation (the keystone design):** matchers are built from DERIVED SURFACES, not the raw `en.term` тАФ the core noun phrase (leading "The " + trailing "(...)" clarifier stripped), any parenthetical acronym (e.g. "(USCT)" тЖТ USCT), and authored aliases тАФ so the spellings prose ACTUALLY uses match (e.g. "The Lost Cause (Myth)" тЖТ "Lost Cause"; "United States Colored Troops (USCT)" тЖТ "United States Colored Troops" + "USCT"). High-value bare-form **aliases** added to 3 codex entries (emancipation, blockade/Anaconda Plan, conscription/draft) тАФ pure data the codex already supports.
- **Architecture тАФ PURE READ-OUT (byte-identical combat BY CONSTRUCTION):** `glDecorate` reads `GAME_DATA.codex` (via cx accessors) and DECORATES already-rendered DOM; it WRITES NOTHING to the sim (no campaign state, no save, no RNG). No tactical/combat/tick/resolve/bridge path references `gl*` (grep-confirmed + a probe static-scan over 20 combat files) тЖТ battles byte-identical by construction. The `_wdRefresh` hook clears `data-gl-done` before each render (the reused `#wdContent` element) so re-viewing a teaching tab re-decorates. Diff = `src/93-glossary.js` + `data/codex.json` (3 aliases) + `src/00-manifest.json` (`93-glossary.js`) + `src/30-president-shell.js` (the guarded hook) + `tools/probe-glossary.mjs` + the generated HTML.

## D119 тАФ E4-i2: **THE STRATEGIC WAR-END** тАФ a reached `victoryReady` (a negotiated peace / a recognized independence) concludes the war via the graded report, for a victory that did NOT complete the battle chain тАФ [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
- **What shipped (the locked Phase-E item after E1):** the strategic arc's missing closure. Before D119 the war ended ONLY at battle-chain completion (`campaignAdvance` тЖТ `warWonScreen` at `idx>=chainLen`). Now a reached **`C.strategy.victoryReady`** тАФ a **negotiated peace** (Northern/enemy will broken, `enemyWillтЙд30` in 1864+ or `тЙд18` any year) or a **recognized independence** (recognition тЙе60, CS) тАФ can CONCLUDE the war through the SAME D112 graded after-action report, surfaced as a **non-forced OFFER** on the between-battles interstitial ("The war can be concluded тАФ accept the peace / claim independence", or fight on). This is the frozen campaign-loop closure the prompt named (E4-i2), built via the authorized `warWonScreen` override pattern (D116 authorized the frozen-loop override autonomously).
- **Architecture тАФ an additive OFFER + the existing warWonScreen; byte-identical combat BY CONSTRUCTION:** new pure helpers in `src/82-after-action.js` тАФ `aarStrategicEndAvailable(C)` (returns `"will"` for either side / `"recognition"` **CS-ONLY** / null), `_aarEndFraming(C,reason)` (side-aware title/subtitle/verdict/offer copy), `aarStrategicEndOffer(C)`, `aarConcludeWar(reason)`. The `warWonScreen` OVERRIDE now frames the title/verdict via `_aarEndFraming`; at chain completion (`_aarEndReason` null) it is the **byte-identical D112 "The War is Won / Victory!"** screen with the base Main-Menu wiring + `G.campaign=null` preserved verbatim. The offer banner is one guarded IIFE in `_pdInterstitialHTML` (`src/20-president-render.js`) тАФ returns `''` when no offer тЖТ **byte-identical interstitial** when `victoryReady` is null; wired (`#pdConcludeWar`) in `_pdShowTurnInterstitial` (`src/30-president-shell.js`). **No tactical file touched; no combat/tick/resolve/bridge path reads `aarStrategicEnd*`/`_aarEndReason`/`aarConcludeWar`** (grep-confirmed) тЖТ 9 battles byte-identical by construction. No new save state (`_aarEndReason` is a transient module var); NO `_SAVE_VER` bump; NO RNG.
- **SIDE-CORRECTNESS (anti-Lost-Cause):** `"recognition"` is gated **CS-only** тАФ the Union never "wins" because the Confederacy gains recognition (D111 noted recognition is unreachable for US by normal play; the gate is the defensive belt). `"will"` is correct for either side (the enemy sues for terms), framed side-aware (US: "the rebellion lays down its arms"; CS: "Washington consents to let the South go"). A CS strategic victory is framed honestly as the survival of a slaveholding republic тАФ never valorized тАФ and the D112 graded report body carries the anti-Lost-Cause Reconstruction accounting (keyed on `victoryReady`, which `aarConcludeWar` does not clear, so the honest accounting renders correctly through the conclusion).

## D113 тАФ ┬з12.3 THE ELECTION-SUPPORT RELIEF-BIND тАФ a commissioned political general costs more capital to relieve before the 1864 vote (the bind Lincoln lived) тАФ [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
- **What shipped (the GM ┬з12.3 keystone the Commission move D109 was built around, now unblocked by the 1864-election state E4/D112):** a commissioned POLITICAL general (Banks/Butler/Sigel/McClernand тАФ `commission.kind:"political"` + a `politicalValue`) delivers his constituency's votes to the war effort while he serves, so relieving him in the run-up to the 1864 election forfeits that support тАФ an ADDITIVE surcharge on his relief cost (`_cmdReliefCost`) that rises year over year toward the vote (1862<1863<1864) and FALLS to zero the moment `clock.resolved1864` is set (the bind is spent). `surcharge = round((politicalValue/100) * windowByYear[year] * surchargeMax)`, bounded [0, surchargeMax=14]. A new teaching tell on the active-general card names the constituency + the `+N capital` cost ("Lincoln lived this bind"). Teaches the ┬з12.3 command-politics lesson concretely: Banks in command costs commandLeadership 49 vs Grant's 87 (D109) AND can't be cheaply dumped before November 1864.

## D110 тАФ RATING SYSTEM **Q12: THE DIVISION SUB-TIER** (seat pool generals into division billets nested under a seated corps тАФ the next rung of the GM depth-chart over the OOB tree) тАФ [CODEX code + CLAUDE close-out] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
The next rung of RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN ┬з12.1's billet tree (Army тЖТ Corps тЖТ **DIVISION** тЖТ Brigade), built HIERARCHICALLY on the Q10 corps depth-chart (D108). Beyond seating the army's IтАУIV Corps, the President now SEATS pool generals into each seated corps's **DIVISION** billets (3 per corps), spending `seatCost` (2) political capital (`C.clock.capital` тАФ the existing GM currency, no new resource per ┬з12). A division is staffable ONLY UNDER a SEATED corps (the real chain of command тАФ a division belonged to a corps), so the depth chart becomes a TREE the President builds top-down.
- **PROVENANCE / CLOSE-OUT (the [AARON] hand-off):** the Q12 CODE + DATA + PROBE were authored in an interrupted Claude-Code session, finished + committed (`7b64d2e`) + pushed by **Codex** on this machine. Codex shipped a sound, builds-GATE-OK, byte-identical-to-source feature **but did NOT run the adversarial bug-hunt or write any doc trail** (a PROPER-VETTING gap vs CLAUDE.md #3 + a record-in-repo gap vs #5). This entry + the bug-hunt below are the **CLAUDE close-out** that brings D110 to the project's "done" bar. (No code was reverted тАФ the commit is sound; this adds the missing vetting + documentation, plus the one bug-hunt fix.)
- **HOW IT REACHES THE FIGHT (no new combat path; D74/D94 no-fudge):** seated division commanders only shape the army's LEADERSHIP facet тАФ an INPUT the bridge already reads тАФ via a small BOUNDED lift folded into `commandLeadership`, summed exactly like the corps lift: `_cmdDivLift` = clamp(╬г over seated divisions of (`effDivRating`тИТ64)├Ч`perSlotWeight`, ┬▒`liftCap`) = clamp(╬г├Ч0.03, ┬▒2). `effDivRating` = the general's GM OVR (`_cmdGenRating`, carries the Q9 promotion lift) minus `belowGradePenalty` (4) when his current grade is below `preferredGrade`. The lift is DELIBERATELY SMALLER than the corps lift (cap 2 vs 4, weight 0.03 vs 0.05) so the influence hierarchy holds тАФ **army (~┬▒17, ┬з27) > corps (┬▒4) > divisions (┬▒2):** a lower tier is a smaller modifier, never dominant. It reaches combat ONLY through the existing `commandLeadership тЖТ bridge LEADERSHIP facet` pipe, NEVER the scoreboard (build-gate 4d scans `35-command.js`). NO RNG.
- **THE GRADE-FIT (a division was a Maj. Gen.'s billet in BOTH armies):** `preferredGrade` is a bare Maj. Gen. for US and CS alike тАФ distinct from the corps tier (a US corps a Maj. Gen.'s, a CS corps a Lt. Gen.'s). Many divisions were in fact led by Brigadier Generals early in the war, so any Brig. Gen. seated over a division leads `belowGrade` until promoted (the Q9 synergy, biting on both sides here). `data/ratings.json` `divisionCommand`: perCorps 3 ┬╖ seatCost 2 ┬╖ preferredGrade {US,CS: "Maj. Gen."} ┬╖ perSlotWeight 0.03 ┬╖ liftCap 2 ┬╖ belowGradePenalty 4 ┬╖ **Inferred** ┬╖ 2 real sources (Glatthaar, *General Lee's Army*; Weigley, *A Great Civil War*).
- **BYTE-IDENTICAL until you seat a division:** no division seated тЖТ the ╬г is over zero slots тЖТ lift 0 тЖТ `commandLeadership` unchanged тЖТ the sandbox + all 9 battles identical to HEAD `7d86fcf` (a vacant division contributes 0, NOT a penalty; `_cmdDivLift` has a fast-path returning 0 without walking the roster when `cmd.divisions` is empty/absent тАФ so a pre-Q12 save with no record reads identically). **ONE BILLET PER MAN:** a general holds at most one of {army command, a corps, a division}; seating him in a division clears any corps/other division he held, and appointing/seating him HIGHER clears his division. **Vacating a corps CASCADES** тАФ its orphaned divisions stop contributing lift, enforced at the READ layer (`cmdDivSeated`/`_cmdDivLift` filter divisions whose parent corps is no longer seated; `_cmdDivClean`:795 requires the parent corps seated) and cleaned on the next load-sanitize. `cmd.divisions = {corpsIdx:{divIdx:generalId}}` (nested) rides the save (no `_SAVE_VER` bump); `cmdInit` sanitizes a tampered/imported record on LOAD (drop array/non-object/out-of-range/bogus/dead/army-commander/corps-holder/orphaned-corps/dupes тАФ the Q9/Q10/Q11 idiom). Writes ONLY `cmd.divisions` + `C.clock.capital`. Carries the Q9/Q10/Q11 hardening verbatim: the `isFinite` capital guard, the commission gate (`_cmdByIdRoster`+`cmdCommissioned`), and debit-the-rounded-gate-value.
- **THE TEACHING (anti-Lost-Cause, both sides):** a corps was only as good as its divisions тАФ A. P. Hill's hard-hitting "Light Division" and Hood's and Pickett's divisions were the cutting edge of Lee's corps, **as were the Union's hard-fighting divisions under Hancock's II Corps (Gibbon, Barlow)** тАФ while a corps with weak divisions underdelivered. New UI: division sub-rows nested under each seated corps in the "The Corps Command тАФ Depth Chart" section + a combined corps+division lift read-out; every new colour annotated тЙе4.5:1 (WCAG-AA), every dynamic value `_cmdEsc`-escaped.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt (the close-out Codex skipped тАФ run NOW on the shipped diff):** a Workflow of **5 diverse-lens Opus finders** (no-fudge/byte-identity ┬╖ economy/determinism/bounding ┬╖ citation/anti-Lost-Cause/no-fabricated-officers ┬╖ XSS/escaping ┬╖ UI/edge/save-tamper) ├Ч default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic. **4 lenses CLEAN; 1 confirmed LOW, FIXED:** the division teaching exemplars (A. P. Hill's Light Division, Hood's, Pickett's) were **all-Confederate** while the rating mechanism is genuinely side-neutral and the sibling corps tier deliberately named both sides (the rout of Howard's XI Corps) тАФ the exact Lost-Cause over-celebration pattern CLAUDE.md #4 guards against. FIXED (copy-only, byte-identical): added the Union counterpart (Hancock's II Corps divisions, Gibbon/Barlow тАФ accurate at Gettysburg/Wilderness/Spotsylvania) to both the player-facing `divFoot` string and the `divisionCommand` `_note`. The save-tamper lens independently executed an 18-vector battery against `_cmdDivClean` (Array/null/non-object/out-of-range/float-key/bogus/dead/army-commander/corps-holder/orphaned-corps/cross-corps-dupe) тАФ all sanitize correctly; the no-fudge lens grep-confirmed no combat path reads `cmd.divisions`; escaping confirmed safe (`htmlEsc` at render + `_cmdEsc` in the UI).

## D109 тАФ RATING SYSTEM **Q11: THE COMMISSION MOVE** (bring documented POLITICAL GENERALS into the officer pool for political capital; the GM "Commission" move) тАФ [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
The GM depth-chart move of RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN ┬з12.2/┬з12.3 ("Commission тАФ bring a new officer into the pool"). A new Command-desk **"Commission an officer тАФ the political generals"** section lists each with his (LOW) combat OVR beside his (HIGH) political value, his constituency, an honest one-line record, and a Commission control (gated on capital + the `maxCommissions` slate). Teaches the GM layer's central command-politics lesson (┬з12.3, the keystone): political generals were **cheap to commission and weak in the field** тАФ Lincoln and Davis took them for the factions, votes, and immigrant regiments they delivered, not their generalship тАФ so once you appoint or seat one, his low OVR drags the army's leadership, the bind Lincoln lived. **PICK RATIONALE (decide-&-log within the cleared NEXT menu):** chose Commission (option C) over the symmetric AI-GM (B, [hard]) and the DIVISION sub-tier (B-alt, lower-risk-but-thinner) because it fills the GM layer's missing teaching keystone (the political-general bind the ┬з12.3 anti-gamey constraints are built around), uses the proven `cmdAppoint`/`cmdSeatCorps`/`cmdPromote` byte-identical-until-used spine + the ┬з8 person concept, and adds 6 new citation-grade historical figures. ## D108 тАФ RATING SYSTEM **Q10: THE CORPS DEPTH-CHART** (seat pool generals into corps billets over the D106 OOB tree; the GM depth-chart MOVE) тАФ [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
The GM depth-chart MOVE of RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN ┬з12.1/┬з12.2/┬з12.4 ("an army version of waiver/trading/transfer"). Beyond appointing the ARMY commander (the existing `cmdAppoint` billet), the President now SEATS pool generals into the army's CORPS billets (IтАУIV Corps) over the D106 OOB tree, spending **political capital** (`C.clock.capital` тАФ the EXISTING GM currency, also spent by appoint/promote; no new resource per ┬з12). A new Command-desk **"The Corps Command тАФ Depth Chart"** section lists the 4 billets, each showing its seated commander (name + grade + OVR + a below-grade tell) with a Vacate control, or "Vacant" + a pool `<select>` + a Seat control (gated on capital); a live read-out shows the net leadership the staffed corps add. Teaches real command organization тАФ Lee's First (Longstreet) and Second (Jackson) Corps against the Army of the Potomac's churning corps commands; the rout of Howard's XI Corps at Chancellorsville. **PICK RATIONALE (decide-&-log within the cleared NEXT menu):** chose the depth-chart MOVES (option A) over the symmetric AI-GM (option B, flagged [hard] тАФ an enemy-command shadow wired to combat risks byte-identity/no-fudge) because A extends the proven `cmdAppoint`/`cmdPromote` spine over the D106 substrate and is byte-identical-until-moved like Q9; the new officer-slot/vacancy concept the derived T15 corps lacked is the `cmd.corps` slot map + the side-aware grade-fit.
- **HOW IT REACHES THE FIGHT (no new combat path; D74/D94 no-fudge):** seated corps commanders only add a small BOUNDED lift to `commandLeadership(C)` тАФ an INPUT the bridge already reads тАФ via `_cmdCorpsLift(C)` = `clamp( SUM over seated slots of (effectiveCorpsRating тИТ 64) ├Ч perSlotWeight, тИТliftCap, +liftCap )` (perSlotWeight 0.05, liftCap 4). `effectiveCorpsRating` = the general's GM OVR (`_cmdGenRating`, which already carries the Q9 promotion lift) minus `belowGradePenalty` (6) when his CURRENT grade is below the **SIDE-AWARE** `preferredGrade`. It reaches combat ONLY through the existing `commandLeadership тЖТ bridge LEADERSHIP facet` pipe тАФ NEVER the scoreboard (build-gate 4d scans `35-command.js` + `tactical/T15-oob.js`). The army commander still weighs most (`(ratingтИТ64)├Ч0.7`, swing ~┬▒17); the corps lift (┬▒4) is a secondary modifier (┬з27: small, never dominant).
- **THE SIDE-AWARE GRADE-FIT (historically precise, the Q9 synergy):** a US corps was a **Major General's** command; a CS corps a **Lieutenant General's** тАФ the CS authorized the Lt. Gen. grade by Act of Sept. 18, 1862 and promoted Longstreet/Jackson that October to command the ANV's new corps (formally organized GO No. 6, Nov. 6, 1862). So on the shipped roster only CS **Stuart** (a Maj. Gen.) seats below grade over a corps (he leads stretched); promoting him to Lt. Gen. (Q9) removes the penalty. On the US roster every named general already meets the Maj. Gen. floor (a correct latent guard for any future junior/commissioned officer). `data/ratings.json` `corpsCommand` block: `slots 4 ┬╖ labels [I..IV Corps] ┬╖ seatCost 3 ┬╖ preferredGrade {US:"Maj. Gen.", CS:"Lt. Gen."} ┬╖ perSlotWeight 0.05 ┬╖ liftCap 4 ┬╖ belowGradePenalty 6 ┬╖ prov Inferred ┬╖ 2 real sources` (Sears 1988 on AoP corps creation; Glatthaar 2008 on ANV corps).
- **BYTE-IDENTICAL until the player seats a corps:** no corps seated тЖТ the SUM is over zero slots тЖТ lift 0 тЖТ `commandLeadership` unchanged тЖТ the sandbox + all 9 battles identical to HEAD `2d11bd7`. A vacant billet contributes 0 (NOT a baseline penalty тАФ that would break byte-identity). `cmd.corps` rides the save (no `_SAVE_VER` bump); `cmdInit` SANITIZES a stale/tampered/imported record on LOAD (drop invalid slots/ids/dead generals/the army commander; one corps per general; arrayтЖТ{}). Constraints: one corps per general (reassign clears the old slot); the army commander cannot also hold a corps (excluded from the pool; `cmdAppoint` clears the appointee's corps); seating gates on capital and debits the SAME rounded value the gate compared (the Q9/Q8b hardened idiom); vacate is free; re-seating the same slot+general is a no-op (no re-charge). New fns (`src/35-command.js` Q10 block): `_cmdCorpsCfg`/`_cmdCorpsSlots`/`_cmdCorpsLabel`/`_cmdCorpsPreferredGrade`/`_cmdCorpsClean`/`cmdCorpsSeated`/`_cmdCorpsBelowGrade`/`_cmdCorpsEffRating`/`_cmdCorpsLift`/`cmdCorpsCommanderFor`/`_cmdCorpsPoolFor`/`cmdSeatCorps`/`cmdVacateCorps`/`_cmdCorpsSelect`/`_cmdCorpsSlotRow`/`_cmdCorpsDepthHTML`; edits to `commandLeadership` (+the lift term), `cmdInit` (seed+sanitize), `cmdAppoint` (clear billet), `cmdRenderTab`/`cmdWireTab`. NO RNG.
- **THE OOB-BOARD DISPLAY JOIN (T15, pure display):** seated commanders NAME the player's DERIVED corps on the D106 board (`fldCampaignOOB` attaches `co.commander` when `player.source==='derived'`; `_fldOOBSideExact` renders it). The predicted EDGE is UNCHANGED by seating (leadership is captured in the actual fight, never double-counted on the board). Authored battles show the historical brigades (no corps-slot naming); the enemy is NEVER named by the player's depth chart.

## D107 тАФ RATING SYSTEM **Q8b: THE BETWEEN-BATTLE CAVALRY RECONNAISSANCE** ("scout the enemy" тАФ tier-reveal the enemy OOB, scaled by the appointed general's cavalry) тАФ [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
The camp loop's deferred SCOUTING (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN ┬з15; deferred at D100 until the D106 OOB-mapping substrate existed). On the President's-Desk Command tab, an **"Order a reconnaissance"** control inside the D106 Order-of-Battle board lets the President spend a small amount of **political capital** (`C.clock.capital` тАФ the EXISTING GM currency, also spent by `cmdAppoint`/`cmdPromote`; no new resource per ┬з12) to reveal the **enemy** order of battle to a TIER scaled by the appointed army commander's persona **`cavalry`** attribute. Teaches that good cavalry leadership buys good intelligence тАФ Stuart's reconnaissance rides, and the catastrophic intelligence vacuum at Gettysburg when his cavalry was absent (named as a real Confederate command failure, not glorified). **PICK RATIONALE (decide-&-log within the cleared NEXT menu):** both the GM depth-chart MOVES and Q8b scouting were unblocked by D106; I chose scouting over the depth-chart MOVES because its scaling input (the `cavalry` persona attribute, spread 50тАУ70 across the 9 generals) and its `reveal` hook in `fldCampaignOOBHtml` BOTH already existed, `36-camp.js` explicitly deferred scouting to exactly this substrate, the D106 board already advertised a dead "Scout the enemy" CTA, and scouting is **pure display + an economy spend (never touches combat)** тАФ the safest possible byte-identity. The corps-billet depth-chart MOVES need a new officer-slot concept the derived T15 tree lacks (bigger surface) тАФ deferred next.
- **THREE RECON TIERS (┬з15):** **light** (unscouted тАФ the passive D106 estimate: force grade band + rough brigade count + the CTA) тЖТ **better** (scouted, cavalry < `cavalryFullThreshold` 65: the enemy commander NAMED + per-corps grade + a posture/terrain advisory, NO per-brigade detail) тЖТ **full** (scouted, cavalry тЙе 65: the complete enemy OOB, the exact view). With the 9 generals' cavalry: Grant (66) + Lee (70) тЖТ full; the rest тЖТ better; a no-appointee campaign uses the HISTORICAL DEFAULT commander's cavalry (not a flat baseline). Intel is **fresh per engagement** тАФ the scout record is keyed to the next-battle id, so it reverts to light when the battle changes.
- **ARCHITECTURE (the D106 wall preserved):** the WRITE (`cmdScout`) lives in `src/35-command.js` (it gates on capital like `cmdAppoint`, reads the appointee's `cavalry` via `_cmdGenPersona`, computes the tier via the pure `_cmdScoutTierForCavalry`, and writes ONLY `cmd.scout` + debits `C.clock.capital` тАФ NEVER the scoreboard); **T15-oob.js stays a PURE READ-OUT** тАФ `fldCampaignOOBHtml(C, {reveal, reconHtml})` is told the tier + the recon-control HTML by `cmdRenderTab`, and only ADDS the "better"-tier renderer (`_fldOOBSideScouted` + `_fldScoutPosture`). No combat/resolve/tick/conditioning path reads `cmd.scout` (grep-confirmed) тЖТ a campaign that never scouts is byte-identical to the pre-Q8b build, and the 9 tactical battles are untouched. Build-gate 4d already scans both `35-command.js` + `tactical/T15-oob.js`. `cmd.scout` rides the save (C.president serialized wholesale); `cmdInit` lazily sanitizes a malformed/tampered record (dropтЖТnull; validтЖТbounded) тАФ no `_SAVE_VER` bump. Data: a `scout` config block in `data/ratings.json` (cost 3 ┬╖ cavalryFullThreshold 65 ┬╖ baselineCavalry 54 ┬╖ 2 real sources). NO RNG (deterministic).
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 diverse-lens Opus finders [no-fudge/byte-identity ┬╖ economy/determinism/bounding ┬╖ citation/anti-Lost-Cause/no-fabricated-officers ┬╖ XSS/escaping ┬╖ UI/WCAG/edge-render] ├Ч default-refute Opus verify ├Ч3 + a completeness critic; **9 agents; invariantsHold = TRUE** тАФ the critic independently grep-confirmed no combat path reads `cmd.scout`, cmdScout writes only `cmd.scout`+capital, the 9 battles byte-identical, no fabricated officers, citations real). **1 confirmed LOW + 2 critic-surfaced LOW; all actionable ones fixed:** **(LOW, confirmed)** `cmdScout` gated on `Math.round(capital)` but debited RAW `clk.capital` тАФ the exact Q9 gate/debit rounding divergence `cmdPromote` was hardened against (byte-identical under today's integer-only capital paths, but a latent fractional bug + a consistency hazard) тЖТ FIXED to debit `cap - cost` (the hardened idiom). **(LOW, critic-surfaced)** `_fldScoutPosture` read the UN-flipped historical attacker, ignoring `C.flipAtk` (the alt-history attacker swap the resolver applies) тЖТ the "better"-tier posture could mis-describe who attacks after a recovery refight тЖТ FIXED by honoring `C.flipAtk` with the SAME non-mutating `Object.assign({}, bd, {atk:swapped})` swap the resolver uses (strength/edge are attacker-symmetric, so only the posture line needs it; a probe assertion locks it). **(LOW, deferred тАФ critic agreed no action)** `cmd.scout.turn` is a cosmetic provenance stamp nothing reads (bounded on load).
- **Vetting (PROPER VETTING, all GREEN):** `GATE OK ┬╖ no-fudge тЬУ ┬╖ citations тЬУ`; **combat byte-identity STRUCTURAL** (no combat path reads `cmd.scout`; the source diff is display + an economy spend) and EMPIRICAL (all 10 battle probes land on their historical results, unchanged); `probe-oob` **15/15** (+the SCOUT TIERS step: lightтЖТbetterтЖТfull ladder, "better" names + per-corps + posture + NO per-brigade leak, the flipAtk posture-flip + non-mutation), `probe-command` **40/40** (+6 Q8b steps: tier mapping at the threshold + fresh="light"; cmdScout reveals at the appointee's tier + debits EXACTLY the cost; the gate + idempotence [short capital no-op, no re-charge]; stale-reconтЖТlight; save-tamper sanitize; no-output-gate + unscouted-offers-button); FULL no-regression GREEN тАФ `probe-desk` 13/13, `probe-ratings` 21/21, `probe-camp` 8/8, `probe-officers` 15/15, `probe-field` 13/13, `t1probe` 14/14, `bootprobe` ok, ALL 9 battles + `probe-csplayer` green (bullrun 15 ┬╖ antietam 16 ┬╖ fredericksburg 22 ┬╖ gettysburg 16 ┬╖ chancellorsville 24 ┬╖ malvern 24 ┬╖ shiloh 29 ┬╖ vicksburg 18 ┬╖ chickamauga 18 ┬╖ csplayer 16); `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; 0 pageerrors throughout; `wcag-auditor` AA (one contrast fix `#d66040`тЖТ`#e86840` on the new "Needs capital to scout" span тАФ the auditor measured `#d66040` at 3.92:1/4.33:1, sub-AA; **NOTE for a future pass: the existing `#d66040` usages elsewhere in `35-command.js` are the same sub-AA тАФ pre-existing, out of this scope, logged**). **ENV:** the run was PAUSED mid-vet on an Aaron "pause internet" directive (the battle probes fetch THREE from a CDN; the bug-hunt + wcag are API calls) and RESUMED cleanly; intermittent THREE-CDN load-stalls cleared by retry (the documented gotcha). ## D106 тАФ RATING SYSTEM **THE OOB-MAPPING SUBSTRATE** + a read-only Order-of-Battle board (the ┬з12.1 roster screen; the shared blocker for the GM depth-chart MOVES + Q8b scouting) тАФ [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The shared plumbing the GM depth-chart MOVES (┬з12.2) and Q8b SCOUTING (┬з15) both depend on: a READ-ONLY layer mapping the strategic next-battle (`_brgNextBattle`) to a STRUCTURED order of battle тАФ commander тЖТ corps тЖТ brigade тАФ for BOTH sides, each billet carrying its OVR/grade/strength/provenance (the T14 rating spine). New module **`src/tactical/T15-oob.js`** (spliced after T14; `fldOOBForSide`/`fldCampaignOOB`/`fldCampaignOOBHtml` + helpers). Surfaced as a new **"Order of Battle тАФ the Next Engagement"** section on the President's-Desk Command tab (one render line in `cmdRenderTab`). The recommended-but-FORK-RISKY item was scoped SMALL first per the run plan: a read-only query layer + roster board, **no combat wiring** (the procedural skirmish `_fldCampaignSkirmishParams` is UNCHANGED). Design law: RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN ┬з12.1/┬з13/┬з15. **No new fork surfaced** тАФ `BATTLES[]` already carries real `cmdUS`/`cmdCS` per battle and the 9 scenarios carry real brigade OOBs, so the substrate is buildable read-only + citation-clean without contradicting a shipped teaching.
- **TWO SOURCES, ONE SHAPE:** a battle WITH a hand-built tactical scenario (`fldScenarioData`) exposes its REAL brigade OOB (real commanders + the authored provenance read straight from each unit note via `_fldOOBProvFromNote`, reusing the Q7 reader `_fldOOBUnits` which scopes a multi-phase battle to phase 0); a procedural battle DERIVES a deterministic corps/brigade tree split from the authored totals (`bd.us`/`bd.cs`/year), seeded by id+side (NO RNG). Derived billets are FORMATION-LABELED (I Corps ┬╖ 1st Brigade ┬╖ Garrison) with `commander:null` тАФ **NEVER a fabricated officer** (CLAUDE.md #4 / D92). The army-commander headline names only the player's APPOINTED general (the GM payoff + his `_cmdGenRating` OVR) or the battle's historical `cmd<Side>` (BATTLES тАФ Verified). NEVER invents.
- **THE WALL (D74/D94/D92):** a PURE READ-OUT + DISPLAY, called ONLY from `cmdRenderTab` тАФ never a resolve/tick/conditioning path. Writes NOTHING; read at no point in combat resolution тЖТ the sandbox + all 9 battles are byte-identical **BY CONSTRUCTION** (the generated html diff vs committed HEAD `7df4372` is ALL-ADDITIONS тАФ the T15 block + one desk-render line, **ZERO removed/modified lines**). build-gate 4d's `RATING_MODULES` now ALSO scans `tactical/T15-oob.js` (the no-fudge OUTPUT-WALL structural over it too).
- **ENEMY-FUZZY (┬з15):** the board renders the PLAYER's own OOB EXACT and the ENEMY as a FUZZY estimate (force grade + brigade count + commander, NO per-brigade detail) тАФ the designed hook **Q8b scouting will DEEPEN via a higher `reveal` tier**. The substrate returns the FULL data for both sides (so the GM/scouting can query it); only the BOARD gates the enemy. Triple-encoded + CVD-safe (OVR = number+letter+word; provenance = hatch+glyph+word; the edge = a labeled % bar); all data names routed through `_fldOOBEsc` (XSS-safe).
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 diverse-lens Opus finders [no-fudge/purity ┬╖ determinism/bounding ┬╖ citation-honesty/anti-Lost-Cause ┬╖ UI/WCAG/XSS ┬╖ integration/edge] ├Ч default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic; 15 agents; **5 confirmed: 1 HIGH + 4 MED; critic "NOT SAFE AS-IS" until fixed; the hard invariants [no-fudge/byte-identity, determinism, no-fabricated-officers, XSS-safe] independently CONFIRMED HOLD**).
